# Kerf Рђћ Roadmap

**Status glyphs:** `РюЁ shipped` ┬и `­ЪџД in flight` ┬и `­Ъћ┤ not started`

---

## North Star

**The most comprehensive CAD on Earth Рђћ a single tool in which a person can design *anything*.** Mechanical engineering, electronics, PCB, architecture, civil engineering, drafting, jewelry, automotive Рђћ and every other CAD sector, including the small and niche ones. We are doing **everything**. Nothing here is "cut." Lower priority means *later*, not *dropped*.

This is a **priority-ordered** roadmap, not a date-ordered or effort-ordered one. The tiers (P0 Рєњ P3) express sequence and leverage: which items earn the most credibility per unit of work.

Kerf is dual-licensed: the OSS core (MIT) and the hosted-tier code under `packages/kerf-{billing,cloud}/` + `src/cloud/`.

### Why chat-driven CAD works

Kerf is **chat-driven** CAD. Every capability is designed around one constraint:

> *Can the LLM produce and re-edit this deliverable through a text-native tool, and verify the result?*

Professional CAD is overcomplicated mostly because of command-discovery affordances (ribbons, palettes, wizards) that an LLM does not need. Kerf ships professional **capability** while deliberately not shipping professional **UI complexity**. This makes the roadmap shorter than it looks: many "pro features" are UX wrappers around a parametric core we expose as a text schema + LLM tool + verifier.

**Hard guardrail:** simplification is about *authoring mechanics only*. It is never an excuse to drop a domain or to skimp on correctness, output formats, or standards compliance. Those are *more* important under an LLM, not less.

---

## Platform foundation

The sector work only matters if you **own your work, are not locked in, and can run Kerf wherever you want**. Four commitments, all decided:

1. **Every cloud project is a real git repository** Рђћ `git clone`-able with stock git, no special client. Large or binary files are auto-detected and stored with a small in-git pointer. Version control is two complementary layers: fine-grained automatic file history *and* deliberate, shareable commits with GitHub sync.

2. **One client, cloud by default, easy optional self-host** Рђћ `pip install kerf` for the hosted cloud; `pip install 'kerf[server]'` + bring-your-own-Postgres + `kerf serve` for self-host. Same client, same data model, both paths first-class.

3. **Portability is the anti-lock-in guarantee** Рђћ `kerf sync` mirrors to a local folder with two-way sync; `kerf export` / `kerf import` produce and ingest a plain file tree. Moving a project between cloud and self-host is painless.

4. **A fully-local / offline desktop app is committed but demand-gated** Рђћ portability + two-way sync + easy self-host is the complete launch answer to "I want to own my data." The standalone offline desktop build is sequenced behind real demand.

---

## What shipped

### Latest delta Рђћ 2026-05-31

**ELEC-OPTOCOUPLER-CTR** РюЁ Рђћ Optocoupler isolation circuit analysis: given LED forward current IF, CTR(min/typ/max), output pull-up R_L, supply Vcc, and load capacitance C_L, computes IC (min/typ/max), saturation threshold IC_sat = Vcc/R_L, saturation verdict, Vout_low = Vce_sat, Vout_high = Vcc, output rise/fall time, and headroom factor. `analyze_optocoupler(OptocouplerSpec, CircuitSpec) -> OptocouplerReport` in `kerf_electronics.optocoupler_ctr`. Dataclasses: `OptocouplerSpec` (model, IF_mA, CTR_min_percent, CTR_typ_percent, CTR_max_percent, Vce_sat_V, IF_max_mA, Vf_typ_V=1.2, t_rise_us_at_Rl=(2.0, 1000)); `CircuitSpec` (Vcc_out_V, R_pullup_ohm, C_load_pF=20.0, R_LED_series_ohm, V_LED_drive_V); `OptocouplerReport` (IC_min_mA, IC_typ_mA, IC_max_mA, IC_saturation_mA, saturated_min_case, Vout_low_V, Vout_high_V, t_rise_us, t_fall_us, headroom_factor_min, warnings, honest_caveat). Algorithm: IC = CTR/100 ├Ќ IF_mA (IEC 60747-5-5 ┬Д6.3); IC_sat = Vcc/R_L ├Ќ 1000 [mA]; saturated_min_case = (IC_min >= IC_sat); headroom = IC_min/IC_sat; t_rise = max(2.2├ЌR_L├ЌC_L, t_rise_spec├ЌR_L_actual/R_L_spec) [┬хs]; t_fall = t_rise (symmetric R-C model). Warns: IF > IF_max (over-drive); NOT saturated (IC_min < IC_sat, suggests fix); headroom < 2.0 (aging margin); IF mismatch (circuit-derived IF vs spec IF > 25%). `elec_analyze_optocoupler` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 68 tests green. HONEST: LINEAR CTR MODEL ONLY Рђћ IC = CTR/100 ├Ќ IF; real CTR vs IF is non-linear (peaks at moderate IF, falls at extremes); TEMPERATURE AND LIFETIME DERATING NOT MODELLED Рђћ CTR degrades 30РђЊ50% over LED lifetime at elevated temperature (Avago AN-5078 ┬Д4.3); always derate CTR to the datasheet minimum at maximum rated temperature (NOT the 25┬░C value); Vce_sat is a fixed datasheet spec (actual depends on IC + temperature); rise/fall time is an RC estimate (2.2├ЌR_L├ЌC_L) Рђћ minority-carrier storage NOT modelled; for high-speed designs use t_PLH/t_PHL from the datasheet at exact R_L and V_CC; isolation voltage (V_IORM, IEC 60747-5-5 creepage/clearance) NOT checked. Refs: Vishay Application Note AN-38 "Optocoupler Output Response Time"; Avago/Broadcom Application Note 5078 "Using Optocouplers"; IEC 60747-5-5:2007 ┬Д6.3 Рђћ `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/optocoupler_ctr.py`.

**ELEC-ZENER-TC-DRIFT** РюЁ Рђћ Zener voltage drift over temperature using temperature coefficient TC (mV/┬░C). Models the Vz vs T curve which has a zero-TC crossing near 5.6 V (above: positive TC dominated by avalanche; below: negative TC dominated by Zener tunneling). `compute_zener_drift(ZenerSpec, OperatingSpec) -> ZenerDriftReport` in `kerf_electronics.zener_tc_drift`. Dataclasses: `ZenerSpec` (Vz_nominal_V, TC_mV_per_C, test_current_mA, test_temp_C=25.0); `OperatingSpec` (current_mA, ambient_temp_C_min, ambient_temp_C_max); `ZenerDriftReport` (Vz_at_min_temp_V, Vz_at_max_temp_V, Vz_drift_total_V, Vz_drift_percent, current_dependence_warning, recommendation, honest_caveat). Algorithm: rZРЅѕ0.01├ЌVz/Iz_test [╬Е] (Vishay AN-2014-3 ┬Д2.2); ╬ћVz_current=rZ├Ќ(Iz_opРѕњIz_test) [V]; Vz(T)=(Vz_nom+╬ћVz_current)+TC├Ќ10РЂ╗┬│├Ќ(TРѕњT_test) [V]; drift_percent=100├Ќ|Vz(T_max)РѕњVz(T_min)|/Vz_nom; current deviation >50% triggers warning. Recommendation: drift>5% Рєњ suggest 5.6V near-zero-TC Zener (BZX55C5V6, 1N5232B) or bandgap Vref IC (LM4040, ADR4550, LT6656). Physical basis: Zener tunneling (Vz<5V, negative TC, band-gap narrowing РѕѓEg/РѕѓT<0 per Varshni equation); avalanche impact ionisation (Vz>7V, positive TC, phonon scattering reduces carrier mean free path); mixed regime 5РђЊ7V with TCРЅѕ0 near 5.6V (device-process-specific). `elec_compute_zener_drift` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 24 tests green. HONEST: LINEAR TC MODEL ONLY Рђћ real Vz vs T is mildly quadratic in the 5РђЊ7V transition region (second-order deviation ┬▒0.1РђЊ0.3 mV / 100┬░C, Sze ┬Д4.5 Fig. 4.5-6); TC is current-dependent (┬▒10РђЊ20% at significantly different Iz); part-to-part TC spread ┬▒30РђЊ50% for C-suffix Zeners; thermal self-heating NOT modelled (T_j=T_amb+╬ИJA├ЌP_Z, ╬ИJA~300РђЊ600┬░C/W for DO-35/SOD-80); rZ linearisation valid only within ~50% of Iz_test; zero-TC crossing is device/manufacturer-specific. Refs: S. M. Sze "Physics of Semiconductor Devices" 3e ┬Д4.5; H&H ┬Д2.2.4 Table 2.1; Vishay AN-2014-3 ┬Д2.4; ON AN-961 ┬Д3 Рђћ `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/zener_tc_drift.py`.

**ELEC-ZENER-CLAMP** РюЁ Рђћ Zener-diode voltage clamp + series resistor design for DC supply rail regulation. `design_zener_clamp(ZenerClampSpec) -> ZenerClampReport` in `kerf_electronics.zener_clamp_design`. Dataclasses: `ZenerClampSpec` (V_in_min_V, V_in_max_V, V_zener_V, I_load_min_A, I_load_max_A, V_zener_tolerance_pct=5.0, I_zener_knee_A=0.001); `ZenerClampReport` (R_series_ohm, R_series_power_W, I_zener_max_A, P_zener_max_W, recommended_zener_package, recommended_R_E12_ohm, regulation_pct, honest_caveat). Algorithm: R = (V_in_max Рѕњ V_Z) / (I_load_min + I_knee); V_Z_max = V_Z├Ќ(1+tol/100); I_Z_max = (V_in_max Рѕњ V_Z_max)/R Рѕњ I_load_min; P_Z_design = V_Z ├Ќ I_Z_max ├Ќ 1.25 (25% derating margin per Vishay AN-2014-3 ┬Д3); P_R = (V_in_max Рѕњ V_Z) ├Ќ (I_Z_max + I_load_min). Zener package thresholds: 0.4 W (DO-35/SOD-80, BZX55 series), 0.5 W (DO-41, BZX79), 1 W (DO-41/BZX85, 1N4728РђЊ1N4764), 3 W (DO-201/P600), 5 W (SOT-89/TO-252). E12 series resistor from IEC 60063 (round up for conservative power). `electronics_design_zener_clamp` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 60 tests green. HONEST: SIMPLE LINEAR SHUNT REGULATOR ONLY Рђћ wasted power = (V_in_maxРѕњV_Z)├ЌI_R_total regardless of load draw; at zero load ALL current flows through Zener; for I_load > 100 mA or efficiency-sensitive rails STRONGLY prefer LDO linear regulator (LM1117, MCP1700) or switching buck converter; Zener incremental resistance rZ NOT modelled (╬ћV_out = rZ├Ќ╬ћI_Z Рђћ typical rZ 7РђЊ20 ╬Е for 5 V / 400 mW parts Рђћ use TL431 or shunt reference IC for tight regulation); temperature coefficient of V_Z NOT modelled (below ~5 V TC is negative, above ~5.6 V positive; РЅѕ5.1 V Zeners have ~0 TC); 25% margin is steady-state Рђћ pulse/transient peaks require JEDEC JESD51-2 transient thermal impedance analysis; static regulation = 2├Ќtol% only (dynamic line/load from rZ excluded). Refs: Horowitz & Hill "Art of Electronics" 3e ┬Д2.2.4; Vishay Application Note AN-2014-3 Рђћ `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/zener_clamp_design.py`.

**ELEC-OP-AMP-OFFSET-DRIFT** РюЁ Рђћ Op-amp input offset voltage and temperature drift calculator for precision instrumentation design. `compute_op_amp_drift(OpAmpSpec, CircuitSpec, error_budget_pct=0.1) -> OpAmpOffsetReport` in `kerf_electronics.op_amp_offset_drift`. Dataclasses: `OpAmpSpec` (Vos_typ_uV, Vos_drift_uV_per_C, T_ambient_min_C, T_ambient_max_C, T_reference_C=25.0); `CircuitSpec` (gain_VV, signal_full_scale_V); `OpAmpOffsetReport` (Vos_at_T_min_uV, Vos_at_T_max_uV, Vos_max_input_referred_uV, Vos_max_output_referred_mV, error_pct_of_FS, within_spec, recommended_op_amp_class, honest_caveat). Algorithm: Vos(T) = Vos_typ + TC_Vos ├Ќ (T Рѕњ T_ref) (TI SLOA069 ┬Д3 Eq. 3-1); worst-case evaluates all 4 (┬▒drift ├Ќ ┬▒endpoint) combinations and takes max absolute; Vos_max_IR = max(|Vos(T_min)|, |Vos(T_max)|); Vos_OR_mV = gain ├Ќ Vos_max_IR / 1000; error_pct = 100 ├Ќ (Vos_OR_mV/1000) / FS. Class thresholds: "chopper" (TC_Vos РЅц 0.05 ┬хV/┬░C, e.g. AD8551, MAX420); "zero-drift" (РЅц 0.1 ┬хV/┬░C, e.g. OPA188, LTC2050); "precision" (РЅц 1.0 ┬хV/┬░C, e.g. OPA227, LT1012); "standard" (> 1.0 ┬хV/┬░C). Recommendation: "chopper" when error РЅЦ 10├Ќ budget; "precision" when over budget; confirm class from TC when in budget. Reference design (task spec): Vos=100 ┬хV, drift=2 ┬хV/┬░C, T=[0..70]┬░C, gain=100, FS=5V Рєњ Vos(T_max)=190 ┬хV, output=19 mV, error=0.38%. `electronics_compute_op_amp_drift` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 24 tests green. HONEST: linear drift model ONLY Рђћ Vos(T)=Vos_typ+TC_Vos├Ќ╬ћT; real drift is non-linear and asymmetric (TI SLOA069 Fig 3-2); Vos_typ is nominal (not guaranteed Рђћ use Vos_max for design margin); **1/f (flicker) noise contribution to DC offset NOT modelled** (can dominate sub-Hz BJT-input amps); **PSRR/CMRR cross-talk effects OUT OF SCOPE** (╬ћVos_PSRR = ╬ћVPS/PSRR must be added separately); resistor TC mismatch in feedback network adds gain-drift error not captured. Refs: TI "Op Amp Errors" SLOA069 ┬Д3 Eq. 3-1; Analog Devices AN-580 ┬Д1; OPA188 / AD8551 / LT1012 datasheets Рђћ `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/op_amp_offset_drift.py`.

**ELEC-INDUCTOR-CORE-SAT** РюЁ Рђћ Inductor core saturation checker. `check_inductor_saturation(InductorCoreSpec, InductorCurrentSpec) -> CoreSaturationReport` in `kerf_electronics.inductor_core_saturation`. Dataclasses: `InductorCoreSpec` (material: "ferrite_3C95"|"ferrite_3F36"|"powdered_iron_-26"|"sendust"|"NiFe50", A_e_mm2, l_e_mm, B_sat_mT, mu_r); `InductorCurrentSpec` (turns_N, I_dc_A, I_ripple_peak_to_peak_A, temperature_C=25.0); `CoreSaturationReport` (B_peak_mT, B_sat_mT, saturation_margin_pct, saturated, recommended_max_I_dc_A, honest_caveat). Algorithm: I_pk = I_dc + I_ripple_pp/2; B_pk = ╬╝Рѓђ┬и╬╝_r┬иN┬иI_pk/l_e (Ampere's law, uniform closed path); saturation_margin = (B_sat Рѕњ B_pk)/B_sat ├Ќ 100; saturated = B_pk >= B_sat; recommended_max_I_dc = max(0, 0.99┬иB_sat┬иl_e/(╬╝Рѓђ┬и╬╝_r┬иN) Рѕњ I_ripple/2). Temperature derating for ferrite materials: piecewise-linear (100┬░CРєњРѕњ15%, 125┬░CРєњРѕњ25%, 150┬░CРєњРѕњ40%, 200┬░CРєњРѕњ50%) per Ferroxcube 3C95/3F36 datasheets; not applied to powder-iron/Sendust/NiFe. `electronics_check_inductor_saturation` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 26 tests green. HONEST: fringing flux ignored (gapped cores need Dowell/Erickson ┬Д15.3 gap fringing correction); ╬╝_r assumed constant (real ferrite ╬╝_r rolls off substantially in the knee region BEFORE B_sat Рђћ model over-estimates B_pk conservatively; use nonlinear B-H curve for precision); non-ferrite B_sat derating NOT modelled; winding I┬▓R temperature rise NOT accounted; AC core losses (Steinmetz) NOT computed Рђћ `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/inductor_core_saturation.py`. Refs: Erickson "Power Electronics" 3e ┬Д15; McLyman "Transformer and Inductor Design Handbook" 4e ┬Д10; Ferroxcube 3C95/3F36 datasheets; Magnetics Inc. Powder Core Catalog ┬Д3.

**ELEC-FET-SOA-CHECK** РюЁ Рђћ MOSFET Safe Operating Area (SOA) checker. `check_fet_soa(FETSpec, FETOperatingPoint) -> FETSOAReport` in `kerf_electronics.fet_soa_check`. Dataclasses: `FETSpec` (part_number, V_DSS_max_V, I_D_continuous_A, I_D_pulsed_A, R_DS_on_mOhm, T_J_max_C, R_theta_JA_K_per_W, P_D_max_W); `FETOperatingPoint` (V_DS_V, I_D_A, pulse_duration_ms, duty_cycle, T_ambient_C); `FETSOAReport` (within_soa, P_diss_W, T_junction_estimate_C, soa_violation_modes, headroom_pct, honest_caveat). Algorithm: P_diss = V_DS ├Ќ I_D ├Ќ duty; T_J = T_amb + P_diss ├Ќ R_╬ИJA (Jedec JESD51 single-node); violation checks: V_DSS_exceeded (V_DS > V_DSS_max), I_D_continuous_exceeded (duty==1.0 AND I_D > I_D_continuous), I_D_pulsed_exceeded (duty<1.0 AND I_D > I_D_pulsed), T_J_exceeded (T_J > T_J_max), P_D_exceeded (P_diss > P_D_max); headroom_pct = (1 Рѕњ max(utilisation_ratios)) ├Ќ 100. `electronics_check_fet_soa` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 30 tests green. HONEST: LINEARISED SOA only Рђћ real datasheet SOA curves (IRF Hexfet Designer's Manual ┬Д5 Fig 5-1) are non-linear in the thermal-limited and second-breakdown regions; pulse-width SOA NOT interpolated (short pulses allow higher peak I_D├ЌV_DS before the thermal integral exceeds the die's transient thermal capacity); second-breakdown (avalanche/UIS) NOT explicitly modelled as a separate boundary Рђћ for inductive turn-off verify E_AS = ┬й┬иL┬иI_peak┬▓ < rated E_AS; thermal model is single-node JESD51 steady-state R_╬ИJA (not transient Z_╬ИJC(t)); R_DS_on is room-temperature datasheet value (actual R_DS_on increases with T_J per Infineon AN 2015-11); switching losses (turn-on, turn-off, gate charge) NOT included in P_diss Рђћ `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/fet_soa_check.py`. Refs: IRF Hexfet Designer's Manual ┬Д5; IPC-9701A; Jedec JESD51-1; Infineon AN 2015-11.

**ELEC-LDO-DROPOUT-CHECK** РюЁ Рђћ LDO linear regulator dropout and thermal compliance checker. `check_ldo_dropout(LDOSpec) -> LDODropoutReport` in `kerf_electronics.ldo_dropout_check`. Dataclasses: `LDOSpec` (V_out_V, V_in_min_V, V_in_max_V, I_load_A, dropout_voltage_at_max_load_mV, junction_to_ambient_thermal_resistance_K_per_W, T_ambient_C=25, T_max_junction_C=125); `LDODropoutReport` (headroom_min_mV, dropout_compliant, power_dissipation_W, junction_temp_estimate_C, thermal_compliant, efficiency_pct, honest_caveat). Algorithm: headroom_mV = (V_in_min Рѕњ V_out) ├Ќ 1000; dropout_compliant = headroom_mV > dropout_spec_mV (strict); P_diss = (V_in_max Рѕњ V_out) ├Ќ I_load; T_j = T_ambient + P_diss ├Ќ R_╬Иja (Jedec JESD51 single-node); thermal_compliant = T_j < T_max_junction; efficiency = 100 ├Ќ V_out / V_in_max (pessimistic). `electronics_check_ldo_dropout` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 54 tests green. HONEST: quiescent current I_Q NOT included (dominates at light load Рђћ TI Power Ref ┬Д3.2.3); transient headroom NOT checked (PSRR roll-off + input cap droop during load steps; add РЅЦ100РђЊ200 mV guard-band per Sandler ┬Д4.4); output capacitor stability NOT verified (ESR window requirement); thermal model is ╬Иja worst-case (╬Иjb+╬Иjc paths not modelled); efficiency = V_out/V_in_max ignores I_Q Рђћ `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/ldo_dropout_check.py`. Refs: TI Power Reference Manual ┬Д3; Sandler "Switch-Mode Power Supplies" ┬Д4; Jedec JESD51-1.

**ELEC-DC-DC-CONVERTER-RIPPLE** РюЁ Рђћ Output voltage ripple ╬ћV_out (peak-to-peak) for a buck DC-DC converter in Continuous Conduction Mode (CCM). `compute_buck_ripple(BuckConverterSpec) -> ConverterRippleReport` in `kerf_electronics.dc_dc_ripple`. Dataclasses: `BuckConverterSpec` (V_in_V, V_out_V, I_load_A, switching_freq_Hz, L_uH, C_out_uF, C_ESR_mOhm); `ConverterRippleReport` (delta_iL_pp_A, delta_V_out_pp_mV, delta_V_capacitor_mV, delta_V_ESR_mV, duty_cycle, output_ripple_pct, honest_caveat). Algorithm: D = V_out/V_in; ╬ћiL = (V_inРѕњV_out)┬иD/(L┬иf_sw); ╬ћV_cap = ╬ћiL/(8┬иC┬иf_sw); ╬ћV_ESR = ╬ћiL┬иESR; ╬ћV_out = ╬ћV_cap + ╬ћV_ESR (worst-case linear sum per Erickson ┬Д2.4). CCM validity: iL_min = I_load Рѕњ ╬ћiL/2 > 0 flagged; small-ripple approximation warning when ╬ћiL/(2┬иI_load) > 30%; ESR-dominance flag when ESR > 1/(4¤ђ┬иC┬иf_sw). `electronics_compute_buck_ripple` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 24 tests green. HONEST: CCM only Рђћ DCM (iL_min < 0) NOT modelled; small-ripple approximation (Erickson ┬Д2.1) breaks above 30% load variation; D = V_out/V_in is ideal (no deadtime, body-diode drop, or min-on-pulse); ESR assumed resistive/frequency-flat (use datasheet ESR at f_sw); ╬ћV_out is pessimistic linear sum (RSS is ~3РђЊ15% less pessimistic) Рђћ `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/dc_dc_ripple.py`. Refs: Erickson "Fundamentals of Power Electronics" 3e ┬Д2.1, ┬Д2.4 Eq 2.34+2.36; Sandler "Power Electronics" ┬Д3; TI SLVA477.

**MOLD-RUNNER-DIAMETER-OPTIMIZE** РюЁ Рђћ Optimal cold-runner diameter recommendation using the Beaumont (2007) ┬Д6.5 empirical formula D=(W^0.25├ЌРѕџL)/3.7, balancing fill pressure against cold-runner waste. `optimize_runner_diameter(RunnerOptimizeSpec) -> RunnerOptimizeReport` in `kerf_mold.runner_diameter_optimize`. Dataclasses: `RunnerOptimizeSpec` (part_weight_g, runner_length_mm, polymer_grade, gate_count=1); `RunnerOptimizeReport` (recommended_diameter_mm, beaumont_diameter_mm, cold_runner_waste_g, fill_pressure_estimate_MPa, polymer_specific_adjustment, honest_caveat). Algorithm: D_base=(W_eff^0.25├ЌРѕџL)/3.7 where W_eff=W/gate_count; material-viscosity adjustment: ABS+10%, PC+15% (highly viscous), PP-5% (low viscosity), PA66┬▒0%; D clamped to [1.5, 16.0] mm. Cold-runner waste = ¤ђ┬и(D/2)┬▓┬иL ├Ќ ¤Ђ_polymer/1000 [g]; polymer densities: ABS 1.05, PC 1.20, PP 0.91, PA66 1.14 g/cm┬│ (Menges 2001 Table 2.1). Fill-pressure proxy: PРЅѕK_mat┬иL/D^4 (Hagen-Poiseuille analogy, order-of-magnitude only). `mold_optimize_runner_diameter` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 28 tests green. HONEST: empirical formula only Рђћ NOT a full Hele-Shaw or Cross-WLF rheological simulation; optimises a SINGLE runner segment for one gate Рђћ does NOT optimise filling balance in multi-cavity molds (use mold_check_runner_balance + mold_generate_runner_layout for multi-cavity networks); fill-pressure estimate is order-of-magnitude proxy only; cold-runner waste assumes cylindrical cross-section (trapezoidal/half-round runners have different volumes); confirm with Moldflow/Moldex3D/SigmaSoft fill simulation and mold trial Рђћ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/runner_diameter_optimize.py`. Refs: Beaumont 2007 ┬Д6.5 (Optimal runner diameter); Menges 2001 ┬Д6.5.

**MOLD-WARPAGE-INDEX** РюЁ Рђћ Heuristic warpage-risk index (0РђЊ100) for injection-moulded parts. `compute_warpage_index(WarpageSpec) -> WarpageIndexReport` in `kerf_mold.warpage_index`. Dataclasses: `WarpageSpec` (wall_thickness_uniformity_pct: 0РђЊ100, gate_location: "centered"|"edge"|"corner"|"unbalanced", polymer_grade, post_eject_cooling_time_s, mold_temp_C); `WarpageIndexReport` (warpage_index: float, risk_level: "low"|"medium"|"high"|"severe", primary_warp_driver, mitigation_suggestions: list[str], honest_caveat, sub_scores: dict). Scoring (Beaumont 2007 ┬Д10 + Menges 2001 ┬Д8): wall-uniformity penalty (0РђЊ30 pts; piecewise linear: 100%Рєњ0 pts, 80%Рєњ6 pts, 0%Рєњ30 pts); gate-location penalty (0РђЊ25 pts: centered=3, edge=14, corner=22, unbalanced=25); polymer grade (0РђЊ20 pts: PC=5 low, ABS=7, PP=14 semi-cryst., POM=15, GF-PA66=20 max Рђћ Menges 2001 Table 8.2 shrinkage anisotropy); post-eject cooling time (0РђЊ15 pts; exponential decay score=15┬иexp(Рѕњt/40), characteristic time 40 s per Menges 2001 ┬Д8.5 HDT stabilisation); mold temperature deviation from recommended range (0РђЊ10 pts). Risk thresholds: 0РђЊ24 low, 25РђЊ49 medium, 50РђЊ74 high, 75РђЊ100 severe. Prioritised mitigation suggestions generated per dominant factor. `mold_compute_warpage_index` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 39 tests green. HONEST: heuristic screening tool ONLY (┬▒15 pts uncertainty typical) Рђћ real warpage prediction requires full filling + packing + cooling FEM simulation (Moldflow, Moldex3D, SigmaSoft 3D Warp); orientation-dependent shrinkage tensors, part geometry, packing pressure, injection speed, hold time, runner imbalance, sequential valve gating, and residual-stress relaxation are NOT modelled Рђћ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/warpage_index.py`. Refs: Beaumont 2007 ┬Д10 (Warpage Analysis); Menges 2001 ┬Д8 (Post-mold shrinkage).

**MOLD-COOLING-PRESSURE-DROP** РюЁ Рђћ Total pressure-drop across multi-segment mold cooling-channel networks (Darcy-Weisbach + minor-loss K-factors) + chiller pump head verification. `compute_cooling_pressure_drop(segments, coolant) -> CoolingPressureDropReport` in `kerf_mold.cooling_pressure_drop`. Dataclasses: `CoolingChannelSegment` (length_mm, diameter_mm, segment_type: "straight"|"elbow_90"|"elbow_45"|"tee_thru"|"tee_branch"); `CoolantSpec` (flow_rate_L_per_min, density_kg_m3=1000, viscosity_cP=1.0); `CoolingPressureDropReport` (total_pressure_drop_bar, reynolds_number, friction_factor, segment_breakdown, chiller_head_required_bar, recommended_pump_head_bar, honest_caveat). Algorithm: Re=¤Ђ┬иv┬иD/╬╝; ╬ћP_major=f┬и(L/D)┬и(¤Ђv┬▓/2); ╬ћP_minor=K┬и(¤Ђv┬▓/2). Smooth-pipe friction: f=64/Re (laminar Re<2300); Blasius f=0.316/Re^0.25 (turbulent Re>4000); linear blend in transition. K-factors: elbow_90=0.9, elbow_45=0.4, tee_thru=0.6, tee_branch=1.8. Recommended pump head=total_╬ћP├Ќ1.25 (25% margin). `mold_compute_cooling_pressure_drop` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 24 tests green. HONEST: single-phase incompressible fluid only (water/water-glycol) Рђћ no two-phase/boiling flow; no heat-transfer coupling (viscosity spatially uniform); smooth-pipe Blasius only (no Colebrook-White roughness correction); series network assumed (parallel branches need per-branch analysis) Рђћ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/cooling_pressure_drop.py`. Refs: Beaumont 2007 ┬Д11.2 Table 11.1; White "Fluid Mechanics" 8th ed. ┬Д6.7, ┬Д6.9.

**ELEC-EMI-FILTER-CUTOFF** РюЁ Рђћ Passive LC/RC power-line EMI filter design per Ott "EMC Engineering" ┬Д15.3 + CISPR 22/EN 55022. `design_emi_filter(EmiFilterSpec) -> EmiFilterReport` in `kerf_electronics.emi_filter_design`. Dataclasses: `EmiFilterSpec` (dc_voltage_V, dc_current_A, target_attenuation_dB, target_freq_kHz, filter_topology, load_resistance_ohm=None); `EmiFilterReport` (cutoff_freq_Hz, L_uH, C_uF, R_ohm, attenuation_at_target_dB, recommended_caps_X2_uF, honest_caveat). Three topologies: LC_low_pass (2nd-order Рѕњ40 dB/dec: f_c = f_t / 10^(A/40), C = 1/((2¤ђ┬иf_c)┬▓┬иL) for L=100 ┬хH); PI_LC_L (3rd-order ¤ђ-section Рѕњ60 dB/dec: f_c = f_t / 10^(A/60), each shunt cap = C/2); RC_low_pass (1st-order Рѕњ20 dB/dec: f_c = f_t / 10^(A/20), C = 1/(2¤ђ┬иf_c┬иR)). X2 capacitor selection from IEC 60384-14 E12 series (275 VAC, 0.01РђЊ4.7 ┬хF). `electronics_design_emi_filter` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 27 tests green. HONEST: ideal passive components only Рђћ no ESR, no winding stray capacitance, no parasitic cap inductance; DM-only (add CM choke separately); source/load assumed ideal (0 ╬Е / Рѕъ ╬Е); CISPR 22 Class B conducted limits (66РђЊ56 dB┬хV 0.15РђЊ0.50 MHz, 56 dB┬хV 0.50РђЊ5 MHz) cited for context only Рђћ accredited EMC lab measurement required for compliance Рђћ `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/emi_filter_design.py`. Refs: Ott ┬Д15.3; CISPR 22 / EN 55022 4th ed. 2003; Nave 1991.

**CAM-TURNING-DEPTH** РюЁ Рђћ Optimal depth-of-cut (DOC) per pass + total roughing passes for a lathe turning operation. `compute_turning_depth(TurningSpec) -> TurningDepthReport` in `kerf_cam.turning_depth_calc`. Dataclasses: `TurningSpec` (stock_diameter_mm, final_diameter_mm, finish_pass_doc_mm=0.5, max_roughing_doc_mm=3.0, material, tool_nose_radius_mm, feed_mm_per_rev, spindle_rpm, workpiece_length_mm=100); `TurningDepthReport` (num_roughing_passes, num_finishing_passes, total_passes, roughing_doc_mm, total_machining_time_s, recommended_doc_for_material, honest_caveat). Algorithm: radial_stock = (D_stockРѕњD_final)/2; stock_for_roughing = radial_stock Рѕњ finish_pass_doc; max_doc clamped to Sandvik CoroPlus / MH 31e ┬Д1148 material max; num_roughing = ceil(stock_for_roughing / effective_max_doc); roughing_doc = stock_for_roughing / num_roughing (equal passes); time_per_pass = workpiece_length / (feed ├Ќ rpm/60). Material DOC ranges: steel_1018 2РђЊ4 mm (rec 3.0), aluminum_6061 4РђЊ8 mm (rec 6.0), stainless_303 1.5РђЊ2.5 mm (rec 2.0). Nose-radius check: warn if finish_pass_doc < 0.5├Ќr_╬х (MH 31e ┬Д1148 rubbing risk). `cam_compute_turning_depth` LLM tool registered in plugin.py. 38 tests green. HONEST: straight (cylindrical) turning only Рђћ no profile turning, no taper, no threading, no facing; Constant Surface Speed (CSS/G96) NOT implemented; time estimate excludes rapids, tool changes, and acceleration ramps; DOC ranges are conservative averages for coated carbide inserts at moderate cutting speed Рђћ verify against CoroPlus ToolGuide for production Рђћ `packages/kerf-cam/src/kerf_cam/turning_depth_calc.py`. Refs: MH 31e ┬Д1148; Sandvik CoroPlus Turning Catalogue (2024).

**ARCH-WIND-COMPONENT-CLADDING** РюЁ Рђћ Design wind pressure on building components and cladding (C&C) per ASCE 7-22 ┬Д30.3 + ┬Д30.9 + Fig 30.3-2D. `compute_wind_cc_pressure(WindSiteSpec, BuildingSpec, ComponentSpec) -> WindCCPressureReport` and `compute_parapet_pressure(WindSiteSpec, BuildingSpec, parapet_position) -> ParapetPressureReport` in `kerf_cad_core.arch.wind_component_cladding`. **ARCH-WIND-LOAD-ASCE7** РюЁ Рђћ Design wind pressure per ASCE 7-22: ┬Д26РђЊ27 Directional Procedure (MWFRS, enclosed/partially-enclosed) + ┬Д27.5 Open Building free-roof net pressures + ┬Д28 Envelope Procedure (low-rise, h РЅц 60 ft) + ┬Д32 Tornado Loads. **GDT-FEATURE-OF-SIZE-DOF (ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬Д4.7 + ┬Д7.3)** РюЁ Рђћ `compute_fos_dof(FOSSpec) -> FOSDoFReport` enumerates the Degrees of Freedom constrained vs released by a Feature of Size + geometric tolerance combination Рђћ critical for inspection planning. Dataclasses: `FOSSpec` (feature_type: "cylinder"|"hole"|"slot"|"sphere"|"planar_pair"|"width", tolerance_symbol: "position"|"perpendicularity"|"parallelism"|"angularity"|"runout"|"total_runout"); `FOSDoFReport` (dof_constrained, dof_released, total_constrained, datum_required_count, code_section, honest_caveat). DOF rules per ┬Д4.7 + ┬Д7.3: cylinder/hole + position Рєњ TX, TY (axis radial location); cylinder/hole + orientation Рєњ RX, RY (axis tilt); cylinder/hole + runout/total_runout Рєњ TX, TY, RX, RY (┬Д7.3.4/┬Д7.3.5 coupling); slot/width/planar_pair + position Рєњ TX (centre-plane location); slot + orientation Рєњ RX, RY; sphere + position Рєњ TX, TY, TZ (point location); sphere + orientation Рєњ nothing (rotationally symmetric). `gdt_compute_fos_dof` LLM tool registered via gated import pattern; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.gdt`. 35 tests green. HONEST FLAG: feature-class lookup table only Рђћ pattern-of-features compositions (┬Д11.3) where DOFs compound across multiple instances are not modelled; PLTZF/FRTZF interactions (┬Д10.5) not resolved; coordinate-frame orientation is a modelling assumption (cylinder axis assumed along Z) Рђћ caller must orient TX/TY/TZ/RX/RY/RZ to the actual drawing DRF Рђћ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/gdt/feature_of_size_dof.py`.

**GDT-RUNOUT-CIRCULAR (ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬Д12.4)** РюЁ Рђћ `check_circular_runout(CircularRunoutSpec) -> CircularRunoutReport` evaluates single-plane circular runout tolerance compliance per ┬Д12.4. Input is structured as a list of cross-section lists Рђћ each inner list contains radial measurements at a single axial position (mirrors physical inspection: fixture at zРѓђ, rotate 360┬░, record N radial readings). Dataclasses: `RunoutMeasurement` (angular_position_deg, radial_measurement_mm, axial_position_mm=0.0); `CircularRunoutSpec` (measurements_per_cross_section: list[list[RunoutMeasurement]], tolerance_mm, datum_axis_id="A"); `CircularRunoutReport` (fim_per_section_mm, max_fim_mm, governing_axial_position_mm, pass_fail: "PASS"|"FAIL", margin_mm, num_measurements_total, honest_caveat). Algorithm (┬Д12.4): FIM_s = max(r)Рѕњmin(r) for each cross-section s; max_FIM = worst section; pass РЪ║ max_FIM РЅц tolerance_mm. margin_mm = tolerance Рѕњ max_FIM (positive = headroom; negative = overrun). Minimum 3 measurements per section enforced. governing_axial_position_mm identifies the worst-case section; tied FIM Рєњ first section wins. Distinct from runout_check.py (┬Д13 point-cloud API): section-oriented input; dedicated ┬Д12.4 compliance path; conical surface independence confirmed (per-section FIM=0 when form is perfect even though nominal radius varies axially). Oracle: eccentric cylinder eccentricity=1mm Рєњ FIM=2mm; tol=1mmРєњFAIL margin=Рѕњ1mm; tol=2mmРєњPASS margin=0. `gdt_check_circular_runout` LLM tool registered via gated import; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.gdt`. 27 tests green. HONEST FLAG: measurements must be pre-computed radial distances from the TRUE datum axis; datum simulator computation (minimum zone cylinder Рђћ ASME B89.3.1 / ISO 12181-1 ┬Д4.3) NOT performed; probe offset/cosine error/thermal corrections must be applied by caller Рђћ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/gdt/runout_circular.py`.

**GDT-RUNOUT-CHECK (ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬Д12.5 / ┬Д13 + ISO 1101:2017 ┬Д18)** РюЁ Рђћ `check_runout(RunoutCheckSpec, list[InspectionPoint]) -> RunoutCheckReport` verifies circular and total runout tolerance compliance for a rotational feature given inspection points measured around a datum axis. Dataclasses: `InspectionPoint` (theta_deg, axial_z_mm, radius_measured_mm); `RunoutCheckSpec` (feature_id, runout_tolerance_mm, runout_type: "circular"|"total", nominal_radius_mm); `RunoutCheckReport` (max_runout_mm, mean_radius_mm, fom, compliant, per_section_runout, honest_caveat). Algorithms per ┬Д13: Circular runout (┬Д13.2 / ISO ┬Д18.3) Рђћ group points by axial z-section, runout at each section = max(R)Рѕњmin(R) = Full Indicator Movement (FIM); max_runout = worst section. Total runout (┬Д13.3 / ISO ┬Д18.4) Рђћ FIM over ALL points simultaneously (max(R)Рѕњmin(R)); captures taper/coaxiality + form combined; total_runout РЅЦ circular_runout always. fom = max_runout / tolerance; fom < 1.0 Рєњ pass. Oracle: eccentric cylinder with 0.05 mm axis offset Рєњ circular runout = 2├Ќ0.05 = 0.10 mm (2d formula); tapered cylinder (R=10.00Рєњ10.20 mm across 3 z-sections) Рєњ circular_runout=0 per section, total_runout=0.20 mm > circular. `gdt_check_runout` LLM tool registered via gated import pattern; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.gdt`. 26 radial tests green. **Axial face runout (ASME ┬Д12.5 / ┬Д13.3 axial component)** РюЁ Рђћ `check_axial_runout(list[AxialRunoutMeasurement], tolerance_mm, datum_axis_id) -> AxialRunoutReport` measures axial deviation on faces perpendicular to the datum axis. Dataclasses: `AxialRunoutMeasurement` (angular_position_deg, radial_position_mm, axial_z_mm); `AxialRunoutReport` (axial_fim_mm, z_max_mm, z_min_mm, fom, compliant, n_points, datum_axis_id, honest_caveat). Algorithm (┬Д12.5): axial_FIM = max(z)Рѕњmin(z) over all measurement points; pass РЪ║ axial_FIM РЅц tolerance_mm. Oracle: flat face (all z equal) Рєњ FIM=0; tilted face amplitude a Рєњ FIM=2a; wavy face amplitude a Рєњ FIM=2a. Re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.gdt`. 27 axial tests green (79 total). HONEST FLAG: ideal datum axis assumed Рђћ all radii must be pre-computed from a known datum axis; Chebyshev-optimal (minimum zone) axis fit (ASME B89.3.1 / ISO 12181-1 ┬Д4.3) is not performed. Circular runout grouping uses exact z-value equality Рђћ real CMM data may require z-binning before calling. Total runout (check_runout) is radial-only; axial face runout is implemented separately via check_axial_runout() Рђћ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/gdt/runout_check.py`.

**GDT-DATUM-SHIFT-CHECK (ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬Д4.5 + ┬Д7.3.5)** РюЁ Рђћ `compute_datum_shift(DatumFeatureSpec, base_position_tolerance_mm) -> DatumShiftReport` computes per-datum bonus tolerance (datum shift) when a datum feature of size is referenced with an MMC or LMC modifier in the feature control frame. Dataclasses: `DatumFeatureSpec` (datum_letter, mmc_size_mm, lmc_size_mm, measured_size_mm, material_condition_modifier); `DatumShiftReport` (datum_letter, base_tolerance_zone_mm, bonus_shift_mm, total_available_tolerance_mm, shift_allowed, code_section, honest_caveat). Computation per ┬Д4.5 + ┬Д7.3.5: MMC modifier Рєњ shift = |measured Рѕњ MMC|; LMC modifier Рєњ shift = |measured Рѕњ LMC|; RFS Рєњ shift = 0. Total available tolerance = base + bonus_shift. `gdt_compute_datum_shift` LLM tool registered via gated import pattern; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.gdt`. 30 tests green. HONEST FLAG: per-datum shift computed independently Рђћ multi-datum DRF secondary/tertiary cascade constraint propagation (┬Д4.11.4) is datum-by-datum; composite frame validation (PLTZF/FRTZF ┬Д10.5.2) is separate in `composite_tolerance_check` Рђћ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/gdt/datum_shift_check.py`.

**GDT-COMPOSITE-TOLERANCE (ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬Д10.5.2 + ┬Д11.6)** РюЁ Рђћ `validate_composite_frame(CompositeFrameSpec) -> CompositeFrameValidationReport` validates stacked PLTZF/FRTZF composite feature control frames in `kerf_cad_core.gdt.composite_tolerance_check`. Dataclasses: `CompositeTolSegment` (symbol, tol_value_mm, datum_refs, material_condition); `CompositeFrameSpec` (feature_id, segments list); `CompositeFrameValidationReport` (valid, violations, standard_section, honest_caveat). Three rules enforced: R1 Рђћ all segments share the same geometric symbol (┬Д10.5.2(a)); R2 Рђћ each lower segment tolerance РЅц segment above it (FRTZF tol РЅц PLTZF tol, ┬Д10.5.1 Note 2); R3 Рђћ lower segment datum_refs must be a subset of the segment above (┬Д10.5.1(b)) Рђћ new datums below the PLTZF would imply location constraint, reserved for the PLTZF; FRTZF may only refine orientation. Multi-tier (3+ segment) composite frames supported. `gdt_validate_composite_frame` LLM tool registered via gated import pattern; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.gdt`. HONEST FLAG: validates frame structure only Рђћ does not verify inspection measurement data against tolerance zones, does not parse drawing text, and does not check geometric compatibility with the part model. 44 tests green Рђћ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/gdt/composite_tolerance_check.py`.

**GDT-COMPOSITE-POSITION (ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬Д10.5)** РюЁ Рђћ `check_composite_position(CompositePositionSpec) -> CompositePositionReport` evaluates composite positional tolerance compliance for a feature pattern against measured 3-D points. Dataclasses: `FeaturePoint` (feature_id, nominal_xyz_mm, measured_xyz_mm, feature_size_mm, mmc_size_mm); `CompositePositionSpec` (features, upper_pltzf_tolerance_mm, lower_frtzf_tolerance_mm, datums_pltzf, datums_frtzf, mmc_modifier); `CompositePositionReport` (pltzf_violations, frtzf_violations, overall_pass, max_pltzf_deviation_mm, max_frtzf_deviation_mm, pltzf_centroid_shift_mm, honest_caveat). Two-tier evaluation: PLTZF (upper frame) Рђћ each feature diametral deviation = 2РђќmeasuredРѕњnominalРђќ must be РЅц upper_pltzf_tolerance_mm + MMC_bonus; controls pattern location vs full datum frame (datums_pltzf e.g. A|B|C). FRTZF (lower frame) Рђћ centroid-shift measured pattern onto nominal; residual inter-feature deviation must be РЅц lower_frtzf_tolerance_mm + MMC_bonus; controls relative spacing/orientation (datums_frtzf e.g. A). MMC bonus = max(0, feature_size_mm Рѕњ mmc_size_mm) per ┬Д4.5. `gdt_check_composite_position` LLM tool registered via gated import; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.gdt`. 34 tests green. HONEST FLAG: positional tolerance only Рђћ orientation (perpendicularity/parallelism/angularity) of feature axes within pattern not separately evaluated; FRTZF uses centroid translation only (no 6-DOF rigid-body registration Рђћ rotation not optimised); datum simulator computation not performed; caller must supply pre-processed CMM axis positions Рђћ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/gdt/composite_position.py`.

**GDT-DIMENSION-CHAIN (ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬Д5.3 + Bralla ┬Д1)** РюЁ Рђћ `compute_dimension_chain(chain: list[DimensionLink], target_gap_min_mm, target_gap_max_mm) -> DimensionChainReport` computes worst-case (WC) and statistical RSS tolerance stack-up for a linear dimension chain. Dataclasses: `DimensionLink` (link_id, nominal_mm, tol_plus_mm, tol_minus_mm, direction: "positive"|"negative"); `DimensionChainReport` (nominal_gap_mm, worst_case_min_mm, worst_case_max_mm, rss_min_mm, rss_max_mm, links_count, dominant_link, honest_caveat). Algorithm: nominal_gap = ╬Б s_i┬иd_i; WC accumulation T_WC = ╬Б max(tРЂ║_i, tРЂ╗_i); G_wc_min/max = nominal РѕЊ T_WC; RSS accumulation T_RSS = Рѕџ(╬Б max(tРЂ║_i, tРЂ╗_i)┬▓); G_rss_min/max = nominal РѕЊ T_RSS (3¤Ѓ bilateral, 99.73% assemblability). dominant_link = link with largest half-tolerance. Oracle: +100┬▒0.5 / Рѕњ30┬▒0.2 / Рѕњ20┬▒0.1 Рєњ nominal=50 mm; WC=[49.2, 50.8]; RSS=Рѕџ0.30=0.5477Рєњ[49.452, 50.548]. `gdt_compute_dimension_chain` LLM tool registered via gated import pattern; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.gdt`. 24 tests green. HONEST FLAG: RSS assumes independent, normally distributed component dimensions centred on nominal (Cpk=1.0 for all links); correlation between links (e.g. same fixture datum) and non-normal distributions are not modelled Рђћ RSS is unconservative in those cases; Monte Carlo with measured process distributions is more accurate per Bralla ┬Д1 Рђћ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/gdt/dimension_chain.py`. Refs: ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬Д5.3; Bralla "Design for Manufacturability Handbook" ┬Д1.

**GK-P13 SUBD-G1-EXTRAORDINARY-PATCHES** РюЁ Рђћ G1 continuity at extraordinary-vertex SubDРєњNURBS patch conversion. `convert_subd_to_g1_patches(spec: ExtraordinaryPatchSpec) -> G1PatchResult` builds n bicubic B├Еzier patches around a Catmull-Clark extraordinary vertex (valence n РЅа 4) with Loop (1987) ┬Д4 tangent-plane continuity enforcement: (1) apply `num_iterations` CC subdivisions to isolate the EV; (2) compute EV limit position V_inf via Stam (1998) ┬Д3.1; (3) build n 4├Ќ4 B├Еzier CP grids in the Stam limit-tangent plane, one per face sector; (4) project second-row CPs of adjacent patches into the Stam tangent plane at V_inf to enforce G1 across all n shared boundary edges. Dataclasses: `ExtraordinaryPatchSpec` (cage_mesh: SubdCage, extraordinary_vertex_idx: int, num_iterations: int=2); `G1PatchResult` (n_patches int = valence, patch_control_points_per_patch: list[list[list[tuple]]] 4├Ќ4 CP grid per patch, max_g1_residual_deg: float, mean_g1_residual_deg: float, valence: int, honest_caveat: str). G1 residual measured as inter-patch normal angle (degrees, sampled at 5 points per shared edge). LLM tool `subd_convert_to_g1_patches` registered in plugin.py via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`. 32 oracle-asserted tests green (valence-3 cube corner 3 patches + G1 residual < 1┬░, valence-5 dome EV 5 patches + G1 < 1┬░, valence-4 regular warns + 4 patches, valence-6 hex EV 6 patches, out-of-range idx returns empty, zero iterations runs, re-export from subd package, honest_caveat mentions Loop/G1/Peters-Reif, multiple subdivision levels 1-3 finite residuals, n_patches==valence invariant). HONEST: Loop (1987) G1 construction only Рђћ Peters-Reif G2 (curvature continuity) NOT implemented (requires degree РЅЦ 5 patches, Peters-Reif 2008 ┬Д7.4); high-valence EVs (n РЅЦ 8) may show curvature inflation due to convex-hull property of bicubic B├Еzier patches; G1 residual < 1┬░ achieved for n=3,5 test cases. Refs: Loop (1987) MS Thesis ┬Д4 Utah; Stam (1998) ┬Д3.1РђЊ3.3 SIGGRAPH; Peters-Reif (2008) Subdivision Surfaces ┬Д7.4; Reif (1995) CAGD 12(2) Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/g1_extraordinary_patches.py`.

**GK-P12 SUBD-STAM-LIMIT-TANGENTS** РюЁ Рђћ exact limit tangent vectors at extraordinary Catmull-Clark SubD vertices (valence n РЅа 4) using the eigenstructure decomposition from Stam (1998) ┬Д3.2РђЊ3.3. `compute_stam_limit_tangents(ev: ExtraordinaryVertex, ring_positions=None) -> LimitTangentReport` computes: V_inf = w_V┬иV + w_e┬и╬БP_i + w_f┬и╬БQ_i (limit position, Stam ┬Д3.2 eq. 3.1); T_u = ╬Б cos(2¤ђi/n)┬и(P_i Рѕњ V_inf); T_v = ╬Б sin(2¤ђi/n)┬и(P_i Рѕњ V_inf) (limit tangents, Stam ┬Д3.3); N = T_u ├Ќ T_v (unit normal, C┬╣-continuous at EV per Reif 1995); subdominant eigenvalue ╬╗_n = (1/4)(1 + cos(2¤ђ/n)); approximate Gaussian curvature K (angle-deficit / Gauss-Bonnet, Meyer et al. 2003 ┬Д4) and mean curvature H (cotangent-weight Laplace-Beltrami, Meyer et al. 2003 ┬Д3.3). Dataclasses: `ExtraordinaryVertex` (vertex_index, valence, position_xyz_mm, one_ring_vertices, one_ring_faces); `LimitTangentReport` (tangent_u, tangent_v, normal_xyz, gaussian_curvature_estimate, mean_curvature_estimate, valence, eigenvalue_subdominant, honest_caveat). LLM tool `subd_compute_stam_limit_tangents` registered in plugin.py via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`. 30 oracle-asserted tests green (regular v4 flat normal Z, flat T_u/T_v in XY, flat KРЅѕ0, flat HРЅѕ0, unit normal all valences, nonzero tangent magnitudes, dome v3/5/6 K>0, dome normal outward, hex v6 symmetric tangent magnitudes, eigenvalue formula for v3/4/6/5/7, limit weights partition-of-unity all n, reexport from subd package, tangents span plane, synthetic fallback no crash, honest caveat non-empty + "Stam"). DISTINCT from `limit_normal_fit.py` (which samples face grids) Рђћ this is the closed-form Stam formula AT the extraordinary vertex point itself. HONEST: tangent vectors EXACT per Stam ┬Д3.3; curvature estimates APPROXIMATE (discrete polyhedral estimators, CC surface is only C┬╣ at EV so C┬▓-based curvature has limited meaning); distinct from the face-sampling `limit_normal_fit.py` Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/stam_limit_tangents.py`. Refs: Stam (1998) ┬Д3.2РђЊ3.3 SIGGRAPH; Reif (1995) CAGD 12(2); Catmull-Clark (1978) CAD ┬Д10(6); Meyer et al. (2003) "Discrete Differential-Geometry Operators for Triangulated 2-Manifolds" ┬Д3РђЊ4.

**GK-P19 SUBD-FEATURE-CURVES** РюЁ Рђћ extract characteristic "ridge" and "valley" polylines from a Catmull-Clark SubD limit surface (or refined cage) using discrete principal-curvature analysis. `extract_feature_curves(spec: FeatureCurveSpec) -> FeatureCurveResult` subdivides the cage `subdivision_level` times (Catmull-Clark 1978), estimates per-vertex normals (area-weighted face normals), computes Taubin (1995) curvature tensor at each vertex (edge normal-curvature accumulation Рєњ 3├Ќ3 tensor projected to tangent plane Рєњ eigenvalues ╬║РѓЂ РЅЦ ╬║Рѓѓ), then classifies vertices as ridge (╬║РѓЂ > ridge_threshold_per_mm) or valley (╬║Рѓѓ < Рѕњvalley_threshold_per_mm) and chains them into polylines via BFS edge-following. Dataclasses: `FeatureCurveSpec` (cage: SubdCage, subdivision_level: int=2, ridge_threshold_per_mm: float=0.1, valley_threshold_per_mm: float=0.1); `FeatureCurve` (kind: str "ridge"|"valley", polyline_xyz_mm: list[tuple], length_mm: float, mean_principal_curvature: float); `FeatureCurveResult` (curves, num_ridges, num_valleys, total_ridge_length_mm, total_valley_length_mm, max_principal_curvature, honest_caveat). LLM tool `subd_extract_feature_curves` registered in plugin.py via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`. 26 oracle-asserted tests green (flat plane 0 ridges + 0 valleys, flat plane max ╬║РѓЂ near zero, cube cage ridges detected + positive curvature + finite coords, saddle cage features detected, sphere high threshold = 0 ridges, API contracts Рђћ empty cage, spec/dataclass defaults, kindРѕѕ{ridge,valley}, threshold monotonicity, re-export). Use cases: ZBrush-style topology hints; automatic UV-seam generation along high-curvature lines; feature detection for re-meshing or CAM path planning. HONEST CAVEATS: DISCRETE CURVATURE APPROXIMATION Рђћ principal curvatures via discrete cotangent Laplacian (Meyer et al. 2003), NOT exact CC limit-surface evaluation; errors O(h┬▓) in edge length; sufficient for UV-seam/topology hints but NOT precision curvature analysis. THRESHOLD TUNING Рђћ ridge/valley thresholds are scale-dependent (mmРЂ╗┬╣); defaults (0.1 mmРЂ╗┬╣) are a starting point, retune for your object scale. PERFORMANCE Рђћ vertex count scales O(4^L) with subdivision_level L. Refs: Ohtake, Belyaev & Seidel (2004) "Ridge-Valley Lines on Meshes via Implicit Surface Fitting" SIGGRAPH; Meyer et al. (2003) "Discrete Differential-Geometry Operators for Triangulated 2-Manifolds" VisMath; Taubin (1995) "Estimating the Tensor of Curvature of a Surface" ICCV; Catmull-Clark (1978) CAD 10(6); Stam (1998) SIGGRAPH; OpenSubdiv docs Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/feature_curves.py`.

**GK-P14 SUBD-CREASE-FRACTIONAL-DECAY** РюЁ Рђћ semi-sharp fractional crease multi-level decay for Catmull-Clark SubD. `apply_fractional_crease_decay(spec: FractionalCreaseSpec) -> CreaseDecayResult` applies the DeRose-Kass-Truong (1998) ┬Д4 rule: s_new = max(0, s_old Рѕњ 1) per subdivision level. After L levels: s_L = max(0, sРѓђ Рѕњ L). Dataclasses: `CreasedEdge` (v0_idx, v1_idx, sharpness Рѕѕ [0,Рѕъ)); `FractionalCreaseSpec` (cage: SubdCage, edges: list[CreasedEdge], subdivision_level: int); `CreaseDecayResult` (decayed_edges: list[CreasedEdge], effective_dihedral_smoothing_per_edge: list[float] 0=fully sharp/1=fully smooth, max_sharpness_remaining: float, num_fully_decayed: int, honest_caveat: str). Smooth-weight formula: smooth_weight = 1 Рѕњ clamp(s_L, 0, 1) Рђћ matches OpenSubdiv fractional crease blend definition. Convention: s РЅЦ 10 РЅѕ permanently sharp (OpenSubdiv). LLM tool `subd_apply_crease_decay` registered in plugin.py via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`. 42 oracle-asserted tests green (infinite s=100 sharp at all levels, s=2 at L=0/1/2/3, s=0.5 half-sharp then smooth, mixed crease set 4 edges, monotonic increasing smooth_weight, empty edge list, level-0 identity, re-export from subd init, honest caveat non-empty + mentions schedule-only + DeRose, OpenSubdiv s=10 convention at L=9/L=10, negative sharpness clamped, large level clamps to zero, never negative). HONEST: SHARPNESS SCHEDULE ONLY Рђћ applies the s-1 rule per level and returns decayed s-values + blend weights; does NOT simulate the resulting subdivided cage geometry, does NOT apply CC face/edge/vertex splitting operators; cage vertices/faces passed through unchanged; blended mesh evaluation (interpolating between smooth and sharp CC rules for sРѕѕ(0,1)) is out of scope Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/crease_fractional_decay.py`. Refs: DeRose-Kass-Truong (1998) ┬Д4 SIGGRAPH; OpenSubdiv Subdivision Surfaces docs; Catmull-Clark (1978) CAD 10(6).

**SUBD-LIMIT-NORMAL-FIT** РюЁ Рђћ sample the Catmull-Clark limit-surface normal n╠ѓ(u,v) at a uniform (u,v) grid across all cage faces using Stam (1998) exact eigenstructure tangent vectors; `sample_subd_limit_normals(cage_mesh, samples_per_face=9, normalize=True)` returns `LimitNormalFitResult(sampled_normals, max_normal_residual_deg, mean_normal_residual_deg, num_irregular_samples, honest_caveat)`; per-face n├Ќn grid (n = round(sqrt(samples_per_face))); normal via N = РѕѓS/Рѕѓu ├Ќ РѕѓS/Рѕѓv from Stam tangents (C┬╣-continuous at extraordinary vertices, exact bi-cubic B-spline for valence-4 regular faces); residuals computed against bilinear interpolation of four face-corner Stam normals Рђћ quantifies accuracy gain of a proper normal field vs the simple shader approximation; irregular-vertex flag per sample (valence РЅа 4 faces); LLM tool `subd_sample_limit_normals` registered in plugin via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; 17 oracle-asserted tests (flat plane nz > 0.9999, unit-length all faces, nx/ny РЅѕ 0, dot > 0.9999, normalize=True/False, result structure, total sample count, honest_caveat non-empty, irregular cube valence-3 > 0, flat plane residual < 0.5┬░, max residual РЅц 90┬░, cylinder normals perpendicular to Y, cube 24-sample count + unit-length, empty cage no exception). HONEST: "fit" = residual analysis vs bilinear, NOT a closed-form NURBS surface (would require overdetermined least-squares + knot/CP storage) Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/limit_normal_fit.py`. Refs: Stam (1998) ┬Д3.2; Halstead-Kass-DeRose (1993); Piegl-Tiller ┬Д9.

Plate dimensions rounded up to nearest 5 mm; must cover column footprint (0.95┬иd ├Ќ 0.80┬иbf per DG-1 ┬Д3.1.1). Cantilever arms: m=(NРѕњ0.95┬иd)/2 (Eq 3.1-1); n=(BРѕњ0.80┬иbf)/2 (Eq 3.1-2); n'=Рѕџ(d┬иbf)/4; X=[4┬иd┬иbf/(d+bf)┬▓]┬и[P_u/(¤є_c┬иPp)] (Eq 3.1-8); ╬╗=min(1, 2┬иРѕџX/(1+Рѕџ(1РѕњX))); l=max(m,n,╬╗┬иn'). **ARCH-SLAB-ON-GRADE (ACI 360R-10 + PCA EB119 + Westergaard 1948)** РюЁ Рђћ `check_slab_on_grade(SlabOnGradeSpec) -> SlabOnGradeReport` checks unreinforced concrete slab-on-grade thickness adequacy under a concentrated interior point/wheel load. Westergaard radius of relative stiffness: l = [E┬иh┬│/(12┬и(1Рѕњ╬й┬▓)┬иk)]^0.25 where E=4700┬иРѕџf'c (ACI 318-19 ┬Д19.2.2.1), ╬й=0.15, k=subgrade modulus [N/mm┬│]. PCA EB119 (Ringo & Anderson 1996) simplified interior-load bending stress: ¤Ѓ_max = 3┬иP┬и(1+╬й)/(2┬и¤ђ┬иh┬▓)┬и(logРѓЂРѓђ(l/b)+0.5). Modulus of rupture: MR = 0.62┬иРѕџf'c (ACI 318-19 ┬Д19.2.3.1). DCR = ¤Ѓ_max/MR; joint spacing РЅц 30┬иh (PCA 30├Ќh rule). Oracle (h=150mm, f'c=25MPa, k=27.2MPa/m, P=50kN, b=80mm): lРЅѕ706mm, MR=3.10MPa, ¤Ѓ_maxРЅѕ1.76MPa, DCRРЅѕ0.57 (adequate); P=200kN Рєњ DCRРЅѕ2.28 (inadequate); joint spacing=4.5m. `arch_check_slab_on_grade` LLM tool registered in plugin (gated import); re-exported from arch/__init__.py. 28 hermetic oracle tests pass Рђћ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/arch/slab_on_grade.py`. *SCOPE: INTERIOR LOAD ONLY Рђћ Westergaard edge stress РЅѕ 25РђЊ30% higher, corner even higher (Westergaard 1948 ┬Д3); do NOT use within one slab thickness of an edge/joint. Thermal/shrinkage curling NOT modelled Рђћ can add 0.3РђЊ1.0 MPa tensile stress (ACI 360R-10 Appendix A2.2). Single concentrated load only; multi-load superposition NOT included. Reinforcement for structural capacity NOT modelled (crack-control rebar only; ACI 360R-10 ┬Д6 for SFRC, ┬Д7 for PT). k at slab soffit; plate-bearing correction NOT applied (ASTM D1196). Working-stress design (no partial safety factors); ACI 360R-10 Appendix A recommends additional safety margin of 1.7РђЊ2.0 for unreinforced slabs under vehicle loads. Refs: Westergaard H.M. (1948) Trans. ASCE 113, 425РђЊ444; PCA EB119 (Ringo & Anderson, 3rd ed. 1996); ACI 360R-10 ┬ДA2.1; ACI 318-19 ┬Д19.2.2.1/┬Д19.2.3.1.*

**ARCH-OPENING-IN-WALL (IBC ┬Д2308.4 + ACI 318-19 ┬Д11.5.3.1 + TMS 402-22 ┬Д5/┬Д8.3)** РюЁ Рђћ `check_opening(WallOpeningSpec) -> OpeningCheckReport` checks a wall opening (door/window) for code-compliant tributary load redistribution to jamb piers and lintel/header adequacy. Tributary width per jamb (IBC ┬Д2308.4 prescriptive intent): trib_w = opening_width/2 + jamb_width/2 + header_above_opening_height. Oracle (concrete, 3m wall, 200mm thick, 1.2m├Ќ1.5m window, fc=30MPa, jamb=0.4m, axial=30kN/m, lateral=1.0kN/m┬▓): trib_w=1.8m, Pu=65.7kN, ¤є┬иPnРЅѕ812kN, jamb DCRРЅѕ0.081; all_adequate=True. `OpeningCheckReport` returns tributary_load_on_jamb_kN, jamb_axial_capacity_kN, jamb_dcr, lintel_moment_dcr, lintel_deflection_mm, all_adequate, governing_check, honest_caveat. `arch_check_opening_in_wall` LLM tool registered in plugin (gated import); re-exported from arch/__init__.py. 25 hermetic oracle tests pass Рђћ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/arch/opening_in_wall.py`. *SCOPE: SIMPLIFIED TRIBUTARY METHOD Рђћ full 2-D FE stress-concentration analysis around opening corners NOT modelled (St. Venant diffusion РЅѕ 1РђЊ2├Ќ opening dimension; may be unconservative for wide openings > wall_height/2 or clustered openings). **ARCH-LINTEL-DESIGN (AISC Manual Table 3-23 + ACI 318-19 ┬Д9 + TMS 402-22 ┬Д5)** РюЁ Рђћ `design_lintel(LintelSpec) -> LintelDesignReport` checks steel, reinforced-concrete, and reinforced-masonry lintels over wall openings for moment, shear, and deflection. **ARCH-BEARING-WALL-AXIAL (ACI 318-19 ┬Д11.5.3.1 + TMS 402-22 ┬Д8.3 + Wight ┬Д13.13)** РюЁ Рђћ `check_bearing_wall(BearingWallSpec, P_factored_kN_per_m, phi=0.65) -> BearingWallReport` implements axial-load capacity of plain concrete, reinforced concrete, and masonry bearing walls (unit-strip per metre width). **ARCH-PIER-AXIAL (TMS 402-22 ┬Д8.3 + ACI 318-19 ┬Д22.4.2.2 + Drysdale-Hamid ┬Д10)** РюЁ Рђћ `check_pier_axial(PierSpec, P_factored_kN, phi=0.65) -> PierAxialReport` implements axial-load capacity of slender masonry and reinforced concrete piers with TMS Eq 8-22 h/r slenderness reduction. **ARCH-RETAINING-WALL-STABILITY (Bowles 5e ┬Д12.3 + Das ┬Д13 Рђћ Rankine active)** РюЁ Рђћ `check_retaining_wall(RetainingWallSpec, SoilSpec) -> RetainingWallReport` implements overturning, sliding, and bearing stability checks for cantilevered concrete retaining walls under Rankine active earth pressure. Ka = tan┬▓(45Рѕњ¤є/2); Pa = 0.5┬и╬│_s┬иH┬▓┬иKa (horizontal resultant, at H/3). Weight components per metre: W_stem = ╬│_c┬иt┬и(HРѕњh); W_base = ╬│_c┬иB┬иh; W_soil = ╬│_s┬иl_heel┬и(HРѕњh). Moments about toe: M_resist = W_stem┬и(l_toe+t/2) + W_base┬и(B/2) + W_soil┬и(BРѕњl_heel/2); M_overt = Pa┬и(H/3). FoS_overturning = M_resist/M_overt (min 2.0). FoS_sliding = ╬БW┬иtan(╬┤)/Pa (min 1.5). Bearing: e = B/2 Рѕњ (M_resistРѕњM_overt)/╬БW; q_max = (╬БW/B)┬и(1+6e/B) (trapezoidal; triangular when e>B/6); FoS_bearing = q_a/q_max (min 3.0). `RetainingWallReport` returns Ka, Pa_kN_per_m, FoS_overturning, FoS_sliding, q_max_kPa, FoS_bearing, all_adequate, governing_failure_mode, honest_caveat. Oracle (H=3m, B=2m, t=0.3m, h=0.3m, l_heel=1.5m, l_toe=0.2m, ╬│_c=24, ╬│_s=18, ¤є=30┬░): Ka=1/3, Pa=27.0 kN/m, FoS_overt=4.16 (adequate), FoS_sliding=1.44 (inadequate at ╬┤=20┬░; adequate at ╬┤=25┬░). `arch_check_retaining_wall_stability` LLM tool registered in plugin (gated import); re-exported from arch/__init__.py. 27 hermetic oracle tests pass Рђћ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/arch/retaining_wall_stability.py`. *SCOPE: Rankine ACTIVE pressure only Рђћ level backfill, cohesionless (c=0). **ARCH-SHEAR-WALL-OOP (ACI 318-19 ┬Д11.7 + ┬Д22.3 + Wight ┬Д13.13)** РюЁ Рђћ `check_shear_wall_oop(ShearWallSpec, phi=0.65) -> ShearWallOOPReport` implements out-of-plane (OOP) flexural capacity check for RC shear walls under combined axial + lateral (wind/seismic) loads. **ARCH-PUNCHING-SHEAR (ACI 318-19 ┬Д22.6 + Wight ┬Д13.10)** РюЁ Рђћ `check_punching_shear(ColumnSlabSpec, V_applied_kN, phi=0.75) -> PunchingShearReport` implements two-way (punching) shear capacity check for flat concrete slabs around columns per ACI 318-19 ┬Д22.6. **ARCH-LATERAL-BRACING (AISC 360-22 ┬ДF2 + ┬ДB3.1/┬ДB3.2 + AISC Manual Table 3-2)** РюЁ Рђћ `check_lateral_bracing(WSectionSpec, L_b_mm, Cb=1.0, design_method="LRFD") -> LateralBracingReport` implements AISC 360-22 ┬ДF2 for compact doubly symmetric I-shaped members bent about the major axis. Both design methods per ┬ДB3 are supported: **LRFD** (default, ┬ДB3.1): design strength = ¤є_b┬иMn, ¤є_b = 0.90; **ASD** (opt-in, ┬ДB3.2): allowable moment = Ma = Mn/╬Е_b, ╬Е_b = 1.67. Equations: Lp = 1.76┬иry┬иРѕџ(E/Fy) (F2-5); Lr = 1.95┬иrts┬и(E/0.7Fy)┬иРѕџ(Jc/Sxho + Рѕџ((Jc/Sxho)┬▓+6.76┬и(0.7Fy/E)┬▓)) (F2-6); Zone 1 LbРЅцLp Рєњ Mn = Mp = Fy┬иZx (F2-1, yielding); Zone 2 Lp<LbРЅцLr Рєњ Mn = Cb┬и[MpРѕњ(MpРѕњ0.7┬иFy┬иSx)┬и(LbРѕњLp)/(LrРѕњLp)]РЅцMp (F2-2, inelastic_LTB); Zone 3 Lb>Lr Рєњ Mn = Fcr┬иSxРЅцMp, Fcr = Cb┬и¤ђ┬▓E/(Lb/rts)┬▓┬иРѕџ(1+0.078┬иJc/(Sx┬иho)┬и(Lb/rts)┬▓) (F2-3/4, elastic_LTB). ¤є_b = 0.90; c=1.0 (F2-8a). `LateralBracingReport` returns Lp, Lr, Mp, Mr, Mn, phi_Mn, governing_mode ("yielding"|"inelastic_LTB"|"elastic_LTB"), Lb_to_Lp_ratio, honest_caveat, **design_method**, **safety_factor_or_phi** (¤є_b=0.90 LRFD / ╬Е_b=1.67 ASD), **allowable_moment_kNm** (¤є_b┬иMn LRFD / Ma ASD). W14x90 oracle (Fy=345 MPa): Lp=3 983 mm (РЅѕ4.0 m), Lr=12 962 mm (РЅѕ13.0 m), Mp=887.6 kN┬иm, Mr=565.9 kN┬иm Рђћ consistent with AISC Manual Table 3-2. `arch_check_lateral_bracing` LLM tool registered in plugin (gated import). 35 hermetic tests pass (27 existing LRFD + 8 new ASD) Рђћ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/arch/lateral_bracing_check.py`. *SCOPE: doubly symmetric compact I-shaped members (W-shapes) ONLY. Channels (┬ДF6), tees (┬ДF9), single angles (┬ДF10), and built-up sections (┬ДF4/F5) are out of scope. Compact section assumed Рђћ bf/(2┬иtf) and h/tw flange/web compactness NOT verified here. Cb must be supplied by caller; not computed from moment diagram. ASD demands must be service-level (unfactored); LRFD demands must be factored. Fully backward-compatible: default design_method="LRFD" preserves existing behaviour.*

**GDT-DATUM-PRECEDENCE-WARN (ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬Д4.7 + ┬Д4.11)** РюЁ Рђћ `analyze_datum_precedence_consistency(frames, datums) -> PrecedenceReport` checks a set of feature control frames for cross-frame datum inconsistencies: P1 feature-type conflict (same datum letter as planar in one frame, FOS in another Рђћ ERROR); P1b datum at multiple precedence levels Рђћ WARNING; P2 precedence reversal (A|B|C vs B|A|C Рђћ WARNING, ┬Д4.11); P3 DOF over-constraint (>6 DOF from declared datum sequence Рђћ ERROR, ┬Д4.7); P4 modifier conflict (RMB vs MMB vs LMB on same datum Рђћ WARNING, ┬Д4.11.5). `PrecedenceReport` dataclass: `warnings`, `consistent`, `frames_analysed`, `recommendations`. Each `PrecedenceWarning`: `code`, `severity` (ERROR/WARNING), `message`, `rule`, `affected_frames`, `datum_label`, `recommendation`. `gdt_warn_datum_precedence` LLM tool registered. DOF budget per ┬Д4.7: planar primary=3, cylinder primary=2, sphere primary=3, planar secondary=2, FOS secondary=1, tertiary=1. HONEST FLAG: analyses declared datum properties only Рђћ geometric consistency requires the solid model. Oracles: Fig. 4-1 (3-2-1 planar Рєњ clean); Fig. 4-2 (FOS cylinder primary RMB Рєњ clean); ┬Д4.11 text (A|B|C vs B|A|C Рєњ PRECEDENCE_REVERSAL). 41 tests Рђћ `packages/kerf-gdnt/src/kerf_gdnt/datum_precedence_warn.py`.

**BREP-SOLID-CONTAINS-POINT** РюЁ Рђћ Ray-casting Jordan-curve inside/outside test for B-rep solids: `solid_contains_point(body, point, tolerance=1e-6) -> ContainmentResult` casts a generic-direction ray (1, 0.013, 0.029) from the query point and counts boundary crossings; odd = inside, even = outside. `ContainmentResult` dataclass: `inside` (bool|None), `on_boundary`, `ray_hits`, `degenerate_ray`. Planar faces use exact ray-polygon (loop vertices); analytic/NURBS faces use UV-grid triangulation (M├Хller-Trumbore per triangle, default 32├Ќ32 grid). Degenerate-ray honest flag: if primary direction is parallel to a face, fallback direction (0.017, 1, 0.011) is tried; if both disagree on parity, `degenerate_ray=True` and `inside=None`. LLM tool `brep_solid_contains_point` registered. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. Oracles: cube interior/exterior/boundary; sphere interior/exterior/near-boundary/boundary; torus tube-interior/hole-outside/boundary; L-shape concave notch; 25 tests green. Refs: Mortenson ┬Д11.5; Ericson 2005 ┬Д5.1; O'Rourke ┬Д7.4 Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/geom/solid_contains_point.py`.

**NURBS-CURVE-FRESNEL-PARAMETERIZE** РюЁ Рђћ `fresnel_parameterize_curve(curve, num_samples=200, target_kappa_rate=1.0)` returns `FresnelParameterizationResult(curve_out, max_curvature_residual, fresnel_S, fresnel_C, honest_caveat)`; re-parameterizes a NurbsCurve so that curvature grows linearly with arc-length (╬║(s) РЅѕ ╬▒┬иs Рђћ Euler spiral / clothoid / Cornu spiral law). Algorithm: (1) arc-lengthРђЊuniform sampling via adaptive 5-pt Gauss-Legendre; (2) Fresnel integral evaluation C(¤Ѓ), S(¤Ѓ) with ¤Ѓ=s┬иРѕџ(╬▒/¤ђ) (Abramowitz-Stegun ┬Д7.3); (3) monotone Fresnel-C parameter sequence drives NURBS re-interpolation (Piegl-Tiller ┬Д9.2); (4) monotone-blend fallback when spiral winds past first inflection. Degree-1 polyline caveat; zero-length degenerate guard; negative-alpha treated as positive. LLM tool `nurbs_fresnel_parameterize_curve` registered (gated import). Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 25 hermetic tests. HONEST: sampling-based, not closed-form; Fresnel monotone blend active for long curves; curvature residual is approximate. Refs: Walton & Meek (2009) ┬Д┬Д2РђЊ3; Bertolazzi & Frego (2015) ┬Д3 Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/geom/fresnel_parameterize.py`.

**NURBS-CURVE-INFLECTION** РюЁ Рђћ v2 API: `find_curve_inflections(curve, num_samples=200, tol=1e-6)` returns `CurveInflectionReport(inflection_points, num_inflections, max_curvature, min_curvature, is_fair_class_a, warnings, honest_caveat)`; each inflection is an `InflectionPoint(parameter_u, xy_mm, curvature_left, curvature_right, sign_change)`. Signed curvature ╬║(u) = (x'┬иy'' Рѕњ y'┬иx'') / (x'┬▓ + y'┬▓)^1.5 (Piegl-Tiller ┬Д5.3; Farin ┬Д10.6). Algorithm: sample ╬║(u) at `num_samples` uniform u-values via NURBS 1st/2nd derivatives Рєњ adjacent sign-change detection (|╬║| < tol treated as zero) Рєњ 5-iteration bisection per bracket Рєњ `is_fair_class_a = True` iff РЅц 1 inflection AND no abrupt ╬║-jump (>5├Ќ mean, Farin ┬Д10.6; Sapidis ┬Д3). Legacy v1 API (`find_curve_inflections_v1` Рєњ `InflectionResult`) retained for backward compat. LLM tool `nurbs_find_curve_inflections` updated to return v2 payload. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 38 hermetic tests (20 legacy + 18 new; oracles: S-curve Рєњ 1 inflection + fair, double-S sine Рєњ РЅЦ2 + not fair, circle Рєњ 0 + fair + ╬║РЅѕ1/R, straight line Рєњ 0 + fair + warns). HONEST: **2D only** Рђћ 3D space-curve inflections (requiring torsion) not supported; sampling-based, does NOT solve ╬║=0 analytically; near-zero-curvature regions may produce false positives or miss gentle crossings. Refs: Piegl-Tiller ┬Д5.3/┬Д9.2; Farin ┬Д10.6; do Carmo ┬Д1.5; Sapidis ┬Д3 Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/geom/curve_inflection.py`. **NURBS-CURVE-INFLECTION-STURM** РюЁ (analytic Sturm inflection now implemented) Рђћ v3 API: `find_curve_inflections_sturm(curve, tol=1e-9)` adds a true analytic root finder via Sturm sequences (Marden ┬Д1.4; Uspensky ┬Д5) on the polynomial numerator p(t) = x'(t)┬иy''(t) Рѕњ y'(t)┬иx''(t). Algorithm: (1) decompose non-rational B-spline into Bezier segments; (2) convert Bernstein CPs to monomial basis (Farin ┬Д5.1; Farouki-Rajan 1987); (3) form p(s) of degree 2dРѕњ3 per span; (4) build Sturm chain {p_0=p, p_1=p', p_{k+1}=Рѕњrem(p_{k-1},p_k)}; (5) count roots via V(0)РѕњV(1); (6) isolate each root by recursive Sturm-bisection to tol. Returns same `CurveInflectionReport` with `honest_caveat` noting `method='sturm-analytic'`. Rational NURBS fall back with warning (numerator is rational, not polynomial). 7 hermetic Sturm tests green (S-curve Рєњ 1 root near midpoint, double-S Рєњ РЅЦ2, Sturm vs v2 agreement, straight line Рєњ 0, circle rational Рєњ 0, honest_caveat content, asymmetric cubic accuracy). Refs: Marden (1966) ┬Д1.4; Uspensky (1948) ┬Д5; Farin (2002) ┬Д5.1; Farouki-Rajan (1987) CAGD 4(4).

**NURBS-CURVE-EVOLUTE** РюЁ Рђћ `compute_curve_evolute(curve, num_samples=200, min_curvature=1e-6)` returns `EvoluteResult(evolute_points, t_params, num_samples, num_cusps_detected, cusp_t_params, honest_caveat)`; computes the locus of centres of osculating circles E(t) = C(t) + n╠ѓ(t)/╬║(t) where n╠ѓ is the left-hand unit normal and ╬║ is the signed curvature. Algorithm: sample t Рѕѕ [t_min, t_max] at `num_samples` uniform points; evaluate ╬║(t) via standard plane-curve formula ╬║ = (x'y'' Рѕњ y'x'')/(x'┬▓+y'┬▓)^(3/2) using NURBS analytical derivatives; skip samples where |╬║| < min_curvature (evolute diverges); detect cusps (vertices of C) as local extrema of |╬║| via windowed comparison with amplitude guard (suppresses floating-point chatter on constant-╬║ curves). Circle oracle: all evolute points within 1.6e-15 of center. Parabola y=x┬▓/2: apex evolute = (0,1) exactly. Ellipse a=2,b=1: 4 cusps (stretched-astroid evolute). Straight line: evolute empty. LLM tool `nurbs_compute_curve_evolute` registered (gated import). Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 20 hermetic tests. HONEST: **2D curves only** Рђћ 3D Frenet-Serret evolutes (requiring torsion) are not yet supported; cusp detection is windowed/amplitude-gated and depends on sample density; may miss cusps for highly undersampled curves. Applications: cycloidal-gear design, cam-profile cusp analysis, CNC offset self-intersection prediction. Refs: do Carmo ┬Д1.6; Mortenson ┬Д4.2 Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/geom/curve_evolute.py`.

**NURBS-SURFACE-CROSS-SECTION** РюЁ Рђћ `compute_surface_cross_section(surface, plane_point, plane_normal, nu=50, nv=50)` returns `SurfaceCrossSectionResult(intersection_points_3d, num_intersections, num_components, is_closed_loop, honest_caveat)`; computes the planar cross-section curve C(t) of a NurbsSurface S(u,v) intersected with a plane P (point + normal). Algorithm (Sederberg CAGD ┬Д7.3; Patrikalakis-Maekawa ┬Д5): (1) sample S(u,v) on a (nu ├Ќ nv) uniform grid over the knot domain; (2) compute signed distance d(u,v) = (S Рѕњ P) ┬и n╠ѓ for each sample; (3) walk all u-direction and v-direction grid edges, detect sign changes (d_A * d_B < 0); (4) refine each crossing via 5 bisection iterations in (u,v) parameter space (positional error РЅѕ cell_size/32); (5) chain intersection points into polyline components via greedy nearest-neighbour walk; (6) detect closed loops (first РЅѕ last point within 3├Ќ mean spacing). Oracles: sphere R=2 РѕЕ XY plane (mean radius within 20%), cylinder РѕЕ XZ plane (2 components, yРЅѕ0), flat patch РѕЕ parallel plane (empty), torus РѕЕ z=0 (inner/outer rings), non-unit normal idempotent, zero normal safe. LLM tool `nurbs_compute_surface_cross_section` registered via gated import. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 22 hermetic tests green. HONEST: **sample-based** Рђћ sub-cell features (thin necks, tangential near-grazing crossings) may be missed at low nu/nv; 5-iteration bisection (not sub-pixel for coarse grids); component ordering greedy nearest-neighbour (may mis-order interleaved loops); closed-loop detection threshold-based. Refs: Sederberg CAGD ┬Д7.3; Patrikalakis-Maekawa ┬Д5 Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/geom/surface_cross_section.py`.

**NURBS uniform arc-length resample** РюЁ Рђћ `resample_uniform_arc_length(curve, samples=100)` returns `ResampleResult(points, parameters, arc_lengths, total_length, fitted_curve, degenerate)`; arc-length inversion via bisection on adaptive 5-pt Gauss-Legendre integral (Piegl-Tiller ┬Д9.4 + Patrikalakis-Maekawa ┬Д3.5); `fit=True` returns interpolated NurbsCurve; degenerate flag for zero-length curves; LLM tool `nurbs_curve_resample_uniform`; 12 analytic-oracle tests (circle 2¤ђ/100 ┬▒ 0.001, parabola arc-uniform < param-uniform variance, line sqrt(2)/10 ┬▒ 1e-6, degenerate flag). Honest: GL quadrature ~1e-9 accurate; highly-oscillatory curves may need larger `max_depth`.
**Mold MFR injection-speed check** РюЁ Рђћ `mold_check_melt_flow_ratio` LLM tool: given a polymer's Melt Flow Rate (ASTM D1238 g/10 min), wall thickness, and gate type, returns the recommended injection-speed envelope to avoid jetting, sink marks, and gate freeze-off. Four MFR bands (low < 5, medium 5РђЊ25, high 25РђЊ100, super-high > 100 g/10 min); wall-thickness and gate-type correction factors applied; qualitative risk flags for gate freeze, jetting, and sink marks. References: Beaumont 2007 ┬Д4 + Menges 2001 ┬Д6.2 + ASTM D1238. **Honest caveat**: heuristic only Рђћ MFR is a single-point viscosity proxy; real injection-speed tuning requires full shear-thinning viscosity curve and on-tool DOE with cavity-pressure measurement Рђћ `kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/melt_flow_ratio_check.py`.

**MOLD-SPRUE-BUSHING-MATCH** РюЁ Рђћ `check_sprue_bushing_match(SprueBushingSpec, MachineNozzleSpec) -> SprueMatchReport` in `kerf_mold.sprue_bushing_match`. Verifies that the cold-runner sprue bushing nozzle-seat radius (R) and orifice diameter (O) match the injection-moulding machine nozzle tip geometry per Beaumont 2007 ┬Д6.4 + DME standard sprue bushing catalogue ┬Д3.2. Compliance rules: sprue_R = nozzle_r + 0.5РђЊ1.0 mm; sprue_O = nozzle_O + 0.5РђЊ1.0 mm; taper 1.5РђЊ3.0┬░/side. Dataclasses: `SprueBushingSpec` (nozzle_radius_R_mm, sprue_orifice_diameter_O_mm, total_length_mm, taper_per_side_deg); `MachineNozzleSpec` (nozzle_tip_radius_mm, nozzle_tip_orifice_diameter_mm); `SprueMatchReport` (R_mismatch_mm, R_compliant, O_mismatch_mm, O_compliant, taper_compliant, recommendation, honest_caveat).
