**MOLD-COOLING-TURBULENT-RE-CHECK** РюЁ Рђћ `check_turbulent_re(CoolingFlowSpec) -> TurbulentReCheckReport` in `kerf_mold.cooling_turbulent_re_check`. Verifies cooling-channel Reynolds number Re = ¤Ђ┬иv┬иD/╬╝ against the fully-turbulent threshold (Re РЅЦ 10 000) required for Dittus-Boelter correlation validity (Incropera & DeWitt eq. 8.60: Nu=0.023┬иRe^0.8┬иPr^n). Flow-regime classification (White "Fluid Mechanics" ┬Д8.1): Re<2300 Рєњ "laminar" (AVOID Рђћ thermally stratified, very poor cooling), 2300РЅцRe<4000 Рєњ "transitional" (unpredictable; avoid), 4000РЅцRe<10000 Рєњ "turbulent" (Dittus-Boelter valid but h sub-optimal), ReРЅЦ10000 Рєњ "fully_turbulent" (target for mold cooling, Beaumont 2007 ┬Д11). Also computes minimum recommended flow rate [L/min] to reach Re=10000 for the given channel geometry and coolant. Dataclasses: `CoolingFlowSpec` (channel_diameter_mm, flow_rate_L_per_min, coolant_density_kg_m3=1000, coolant_viscosity_cP=1.0); `TurbulentReCheckReport` (reynolds_number, flow_regime, velocity_m_per_s, recommended_min_flow_rate_L_per_min, dittus_boelter_applicable, honest_caveat). Unit conversions: mmРєњm, L/minРєњm┬│/s├и60000, cPРєњPa┬иs. LLM tool `mold_check_turbulent_re` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 24 tests green. **HONEST SCOPE: Re classification ONLY** Рђћ does NOT compute Nusselt number / convective HTC (requires Prandtl number input), polymer-side boundary layer, mold-steel wall thermal resistance, or part-steel contact resistance; does NOT model wall heat flux or non-uniform temperature distribution along the channel; single-phase, isothermal, incompressible, Newtonian fluid only (no two-phase/supercritical COРѓѓ cooling); viscosity spatially uniform (re-run with exit viscosity for ╬ћT > 10 ┬░C); circular cross-section assumed (non-circular channels: supply hydraulic diameter D_h=4A/P) Рђћ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/cooling_turbulent_re_check.py`. Refs: Beaumont 2007 ┬Д11 (cooling-system Re requirement); White "Fluid Mechanics" 8th ed. ┬Д8.1 (Re thresholds); Incropera & DeWitt "Heat and Mass Transfer" 7th ed. ┬Д8.5 eq. 8.60 (Dittus-Boelter ReРЅЦ10000).

**MOLD-CORE-PIN-COOLING** РюЁ Рђћ `design_core_pin_cooling(CorePinSpec) -> CorePinCoolingReport` in `kerf_mold.core_pin_cooling`. Interior baffle/bubbler cooling design for slender injection-mold core pins (tall rib inserts). Re = 4┬иQ┬и¤Ђ/(¤ђ┬иD_h┬и╬╝) (volumetric form); Nusselt number Nu = 0.023┬иRe^0.8┬иPr^0.4 (Dittus-Boelter, Incropera eq. 8.60); HTC h = Nu┬иk_f/D_h; bubbler mode applies a 2├Ќ HTC multiplier relative to baffle per Menges 2001 ┬Д7.5 and Beaumont 2007 ┬Д11.4 (fountain-effect tip cooling + annular return turbulence). Core-tip temperature from 1-D lumped steady-state resistance network: R_poly = 1/(h_p┬иA_surface) (h_p = 2000 W/m┬▓K, Menges ┬Д7.1 midpoint); R_steel = L_half/(k_steel┬иA_cross) (k_steel = 15 W/m┬иK P20/H13); R_cool = 1/(h┬иA_bore). Cycle-time estimate by Menges 2001 ┬Д7.3.3 / Chen-Chiang 1985 first-term Fourier: t_c = (h_wall┬▓/¤ђ┬▓╬▒)┬иln[(8/¤ђ┬▓)┬и(T_meltРѕњT_cool)/(T_ejectРѕњT_cool)]; ╬▒ = 1.0e-7 m┬▓/s (ABS baseline). Oracle (30 mm core, 100 mm tall, baffle, 4 mm ID, 2 L/min water at 20 ┬░C, Pr=7): Re = 10610, Nu = 83.2, HTC = 12445 W/m┬▓K; bubbler HTC = 24890 W/m┬▓K (2.000├Ќ ratio); cycle-time = 248 s. `cooling_adequate = True` iff Re РЅЦ 10 000 AND T_tip РЅц target. `CorePinSpec` dataclass (core_diameter_mm, core_height_mm, baffle_or_bubbler: "baffle"|"bubbler", cooling_type_id_mm, coolant_flow_L_per_min, melt_temp_C, target_core_temp_C, polymer_grade, coolant_temp_C=20, density, viscosity, Pr, k_f); `CorePinCoolingReport` dataclass (reynolds_number, htc_W_per_m2K, estimated_core_tip_temp_C, cooling_adequate, cycle_time_estimate_s, honest_caveat). LLM tool `mold_design_core_pin_cooling` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 33 oracle tests green. **HONEST SCOPE: lumped-capacitance steady-state ONLY** Рђћ no transient FEA; uniform melt temperature assumed (no gate-to-far-end gradient); bubbler 2├Ќ multiplier is empirical (actual factor depends on tube OD/bore ID ratio, tip clearance, entry turbulence); polymer-side HTC fixed at handbook midpoint 2000 W/m┬▓K (range 1 000РђЊ4 000 W/m┬▓K); Dittus-Boelter valid only Re РЅЦ 10 000 and L/D РЅЦ 10; cycle-time is 1-D Fourier pin half-diameter only (not full mold cycle); confirm with transient FEA (Moldflow Insight / Moldex3D / SigmaSoft) for production tooling Рђћ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/core_pin_cooling.py`. Refs: Menges G., Michaeli W., Mohren P. "How to Make Injection Molds" 3rd ed. Hanser 2001 ┬Д7.5 (core-pin cooling) + ┬Д7.1 (polymer HTC) + ┬Д7.3.3 (cooling-time formula); Beaumont J.P. "Runner and Gating Design Handbook" 2nd ed. Hanser 2007 ┬Д11.4 (slender-core cooling; fountain-effect doubling); Incropera & DeWitt "Fundamentals of Heat and Mass Transfer" 7th ed. Wiley 2011 ┬Д8.5 eq. 8.60.

**MOLD-EJECTOR-PIN-PUSH** РюЁ Рђћ `compute_ejector_pin_push(EjectorPinPushSpec) -> EjectorPinPushReport` in `kerf_mold.ejector_pin_push`. Computes the Euler critical buckling load for an SPI/ANSI B151.1 ejector pin and verifies it against the required push force. Formula: F_cr = ¤ђ┬▓┬иE┬иI/(K┬иL)┬▓  (Roark's 9e ┬Д15.2); I = ¤ђ┬иdРЂ┤/64 (solid round section); E = 200 GPa for all tool-steel grades (M2_tool_steel, H13, S7, D2 Рђћ all share the same nominal Young's modulus). End-condition coefficient K: 1.0 pinned-pinned (SPI/ANSI B151.1 default for guided pins), 0.5 fixed-fixed, 0.7 fixed-pinned, 2.0 cantilever. Dataclasses: `EjectorPinPushSpec` (pin_diameter_mm, pin_length_L_mm, pin_material: "M2_tool_steel"|"H13"|"S7"|"D2", end_condition_K=1.0, required_push_force_N); `EjectorPinPushReport` (buckling_force_N, dcr=required/F_cr, adequate: bool, recommended_min_diameter_mm, recommended_pin_material, honest_caveat). Recommendation logic: searches SPI standard diameters (1, 1.5, 2, 2.5, 3, 4, 5, 6, 8, 10, 12, 16, 20 mm) for the smallest diameter with F_cr РЅЦ 1.1 ├Ќ required_push_force_N at the same L and K; prefers M2 when DCR > 0.8. Numeric oracle: 8 mm, L=100 mm, K=1: F_cr = ¤ђ┬│┬и200000┬и64/10000 РЅѕ 39 688 N; 4 mm pin is 16├Ќ weaker than 8 mm (I РѕЮ dРЂ┤); doubling L reduces F_cr by 4├Ќ. LLM tool `mold_compute_ejector_pin_push` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 45 oracle tests green. **HONEST SCOPE: Euler formula only** Рђћ non-conservative for short/stout pins (K┬иL/d < 30); use Johnson parabolic formula F_cr_J = A┬и¤Ѓ_y┬и[1 Рѕњ ¤Ѓ_y┬и(K┬иL/r)┬▓/(4┬и¤ђ┬▓┬иE)] in that regime (function flags the warning in honest_caveat); bushing friction (╬╝РЅѕ0.05РђЊ0.10 lubricated, reduces capacity 3РђЊ10 %) and pin eccentricity/TIR beam-column amplification (Roark's 9e ┬Д15.3) are NOT modelled; dynamic ejection impact and fatigue over millions of cycles are NOT assessed; confirm by mold-trial load-cell measurement Рђћ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/ejector_pin_push.py`. Refs: SPI/ANSI B151.1; Roark R.J. & Young W.C. Formulas for Stress and Strain, 9th ed., ┬Д15.2РђЊ15.3; ASM Handbook Vol.1 (tool-steel E values).

**MOLD-TUNNEL-GATE-DESIGN** РюЁ Рђћ `design_tunnel_gate(TunnelGateSpec) -> TunnelGateReport` in `kerf_mold.tunnel_gate_design`. Designs a tunnel (submarine) gate given part weight and polymer grade. Diameter: D = 0.5 ├Ќ wall_thickness (Beaumont 2007 ┬Д7.4); +10 % high-viscosity correction for PC/PA66/PMMA/POM/PEI/PPO; lower bound 0.8 mm (machining floor); upper cap D РЅц 2/3 ├Ќ wall_thickness (Menges 2001 ┬Д6.6.5). Break-off force: F = ¤ё_shear ├Ќ ¤ђ/4┬иD┬▓ using Menges 2001 Table 6.3 shear strengths (ABS=30, PC=45, PP=22, PA66=40, POM=38, PMMA=42, PEI=50, PPO=45 MPa). Shear rate: ╬│╠Є = 4Q/(¤ђ┬иr┬│) (Hagen-Poiseuille, Newtonian); Q = (m_part/¤Ђ_melt) / 1.0 s; Beaumont ┬Д7.4 limit 50 000 sРЂ╗┬╣; `shear_within_limit` flag. Gate freeze time: t_f = (D┬▓/¤ђ┬▓┬и╬▒)┬иln[(8/¤ђ┬▓)┬и(T_meltРѕњT_mold)/(T_ejectРѕњT_mold)] per Chen-Chiang ANTEC 1985 / Menges 2001 ┬Д7.3.3. Angle recommendation: 30┬░ for flexible/low-viscosity, 45┬░ for stiff/high-viscosity (Menges ┬Д6.6.5). Oracle: ABS, 30 g, wall 2 mm Рєњ D = 1.0 mm; F_break = 23.6 N; freeze time РЅѕ 1.42 s. `TunnelGateSpec` (part_weight_g, wall_thickness_at_gate_mm, polymer_grade, melt_temp_C, gate_angle_deg=30.0, gate_length_mm=1.5); `TunnelGateReport` (gate_diameter_mm, gate_break_off_force_N, gate_freeze_time_s, shear_rate_at_gate_per_s, shear_within_limit, recommended_angle_deg, honest_caveat). LLM tool `mold_design_tunnel_gate` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 35 tests green. **HONEST: Beaumont heuristic Рђћ diameter is a start-point only; complex multi-cavity timing and fill-pressure balance require Moldflow/Moldex3D full 3-D fill simulation; break-off force sensitive to mold temperature and specific resin grade ductility; shear rate is Newtonian approximation (actual shear-thinning ╬│╠Є РЅѕ 1.25РђЊ1.5├Ќ higher); freeze time is 1-D Fourier constant-diffusivity (PP/PA66/POM actual 15РђЊ25 % longer due to crystallisation latent heat); confirm by mold trial** Рђћ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/tunnel_gate_design.py`. Refs: Beaumont J.P. "Runner and Gating Design Handbook" 2nd ed. Hanser 2007 ┬Д7.4; Menges G., Michaeli W., Mohren P. "How to Make Injection Molds" 3rd ed. Hanser 2001 ┬Д6.6.5 + Table 6.3 + ┬Д7.3.3; Chen-Chiang ANTEC 1985.

**MOLD-SURFACE-FINISH-CHECK** РюЁ Рђћ `check_surface_finish(SurfaceFinishSpec, MoldSpec) -> SurfaceFinishReport` in `kerf_mold.surface_finish_check`. Validates that a molded part's resin + mold-steel + hardness combination can achieve the requested SPI Mold Finish Standard grade (A1РђЊD3), and recommends mold steel grade, minimum HRC, and polishing method. SPI grades (2017 standard): A1 Ra РЅц 0.012 ┬хm (diamond paste #3, S136 РЅЦ50 HRC), A2 Ra РЅц 0.025 ┬хm (diamond buff #6, S136 РЅЦ48 HRC), A3 Ra РЅц 0.050 ┬хm (diamond buff #15, S136/H13 РЅЦ44 HRC); B1 Ra РЅц 0.10 ┬хm (600-grit stone, H13 РЅЦ38 HRC), B2РђЊB3 Ra 0.20РђЊ0.40 ┬хm (stone, P20); C1РђЊC3 Ra 0.80РђЊ3.20 ┬хm (emery cloth, P20); D1РђЊD3 Ra 3.2РђЊ14 ┬хm (dry blast, P20). Glass-fiber rule (Menges ┬Д11.4.2): glass-reinforced resins cannot achieve A-grade on the molded part regardless of mold polish (fiber pull-out + print-through). Resin limits: PA66 Рєњ max A3 (crystalline skin haze); PP Рєњ max B1; POM Рєњ max B2; LDPE Рєњ max C1. Steel limits: S136 Рєњ A1; 420SS Рєњ A2; H13 Рєњ A3; P20 Рєњ B3. Dataclasses: `SurfaceFinishSpec` (required_finish, resin); `MoldSpec` (mold_steel, hardness_HRC, mold_finish_achieved=""); `SurfaceFinishReport` (achievable, recommended_steel, recommended_hardness_HRC_min, recommended_polishing_method, Ra_target_um, Ra_achievable_um, glass_filled_warning, honest_caveat). LLM tool `mold_check_surface_finish` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 27 tests green. **HONEST: catalog-based checker Рђћ does NOT model texture chemistry (etching achievability depends on etch bath + resin crystallinity), etcher capability (bath concentration + cycle count not modelled), polishing wear-life (abrasive filler content + shot count not modelled), part-geometry effects (weld lines + deep ribs harder to polish), or process variables (mold temperature, hold pressure, cooling time affect surface replication fidelity)** Рђћ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/surface_finish_check.py`. Refs: SPI/PLASTICS Mold Finish Standards 2017; Menges G., Mohren P. "How to Make Injection Molds" 3rd ed. Hanser 2001 ┬Д11; Bryce D. M. "Plastic Injection Molding: Mold Design and Construction Fundamentals" SME 1998 Ch. 8.

**MOLD-COLOR-CONCENTRATE-RATIO** РюЁ Рђћ `compute_color_ratio(ColorConcentrateSpec, ShotSpec) -> ColorRatioReport` in `kerf_mold.color_concentrate_ratio`. Gravimetric let-down ratio (LDR) dosing and mixing-quality assessment for color concentrate (masterbatch) in injection moulding. LDR formula (SPI Color Concentrates Handbook 3rd ed. ┬Д3): LDR (%) = target_pigment_loading_pct / pigment_loading_in_masterbatch_pct ├Ќ 100. Masterbatch per shot [g] = shot_weight_g ├Ќ LDR/100; masterbatch per kg natural resin [g/kg] = 1000 ├Ќ (LDR/100) / (1 Рѕњ LDR/100). SPI recommended LDR range: 1РђЊ5 %. Mixing index heuristic (Menges Plastics Manufacturing ┬Д10.2; Tadmor & Gogos ┬Д12.5): mixing_index = 1 Рѕњ exp(Рѕњbarrel_residence_s ├Ќ screw_L/D / 200); adequate if > 0.80. Streaking-risk classification: low (LDR 1РђЊ5 % AND mixing_index > 0.80), moderate (marginal LDR 0.5РђЊ1 % or 5РђЊ8 %, or mixing_index РЅц 0.80 with LDR in range), high (LDR < 0.5 % Рђћ too dilute for shot-to-shot uniformity Рђћ or LDR > 8 % Рђћ cost-waste territory / mechanical-property dilution risk per Menges ┬Д10.4). Dataclasses: `ColorConcentrateSpec` (pigment_loading_in_masterbatch_pct, recommended_let_down_pct, carrier_resin, melting_temp_C); `ShotSpec` (shot_weight_g, target_pigment_loading_pct, barrel_residence_time_s, screw_L_over_D=20.0); `ColorRatioReport` (let_down_ratio_pct, masterbatch_per_shot_g, masterbatch_per_kg_natural, mixing_index_estimate, color_streaking_risk, warnings, honest_caveat). Oracle: 100 g shot, target 1 % pigment, MB at 40 % Рєњ LDR = 2.5 %, MB = 2.5 g/shot, MB per kg natural РЅѕ 25.64 g/kg. LLM tool `mold_compute_color_concentrate_ratio` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 40 tests green. **HONEST: mixing index is a heuristic exponential-decay proxy from L/D and residence time only Рђћ does NOT model screw-flight geometry, back-pressure, screw speed, melt-viscosity mismatch between masterbatch carrier and natural resin, pellet size ratio, or colorant particle agglomerate size; LDR is gravimetric only (volumetric accuracy requires density-matched MB and natural resin); streaking-risk classification is a screening guideline Рђћ trial colour plaques with L*a*b* colorimetric measurement per ISO 11664-4 are the only reliable acceptance test; carrier resin compatibility must be confirmed against base resin; empirical mixing estimate, NOT a substitute for colour-master trial shots** Рђћ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/color_concentrate_ratio.py`. Refs: SPI "Color Concentrates Handbook" 3rd ed. ┬Д3, ┬Д6, ┬Д8, ┬Д11; Menges G., Kemper B., Klenk E. "Plastics Manufacturing" ┬Д10; Tadmor Z. & Gogos C. "Principles of Polymer Processing" 2nd ed. Wiley 2006, ┬Д12.5.

E/F/H members + connections + base-plate, LRFD+ASD); ACI 318-19 (flexure/shear/PM + punching ┬Д22.6 + torsion ┬Д22.7); NDS 2018 timber; AISI S100-16 cold-formed steel (effective-width, flexure/compression/web-crippling); TMS 402-16 masonry ASD (flexure/shear/axial); ASCE 7-22 load combos + ELF + RSA/Newmark seismic. Full Eurocode: EC2, EC3, EC5, EC8.

**Native FE** РюЁ Рђћ MITC4 plate/shell (Bathe-Dvorkin) + modal via inverse iteration; linear eigenvalue buckling + harmonic response + random-vibration PSD; 2D/3D frame stiffness + story drift; multi-axial critical-plane fatigue (Findley, SWT-3D, Brown-Miller); acoustics FEM/BEM + high-frequency EM + electrostatics/magnetostatics; geotech liquefaction triggering (Seed-Idriss/Tokimatsu).

**Machine elements depth** РюЁ Рђћ ISO 6336 gear rating Method B; ISO/TS 16281 bearing modified life (aISO); planetary gearbox (3 Willis modes + compound); Taylor extended tool-life + Gilbert economics.

**Thermo-fluid depth** РюЁ Рђћ IAPWS-IF97 steam Regions 1/2/3/4 (Region 3 supercritical/near-critical Helmholtz formulation РюЁ); Bell-Delaware shell-and-tube HX (TEMA + 5 correction factors); transient pipe-network (MOC waterhammer + surge-tank); ASHRAE CLTD/RTS transient cooling loads; equal-friction duct sizing optimizer (ASHRAE ┬Д35) РюЁ.

**Electronics / power depth** РюЁ Рђћ IBIS-AMI signal integrity (Bergeron + PRBS eye); AC PDN impedance + decap optimiser; Newton-Raphson AC load-flow; IEC 60255 + IEEE C37.112 protection coordination + IEEE 1584-2018 arc-flash; fibre-optic link budget; **ELEC-DECOUPLING-CAP-SIZE** decoupling capacitor sizing (Z_target + bulk/bypass) РюЁ.

**Manufacturing depth** РюЁ Рђћ **MOLD-EJECTOR-STROKE-VERIFY** (Beaumont 2007 ┬Д9 + Menges 2001 ┬Д7.4): `verify_ejector_stroke()` Рђћ (1) stroke adequacy: required_stroke (part_depth + safety_margin) РЅц machine_stroke; (2) force capacity: pin_count ├Ќ max_force РЅЦ ejection_force (Menges ┬Д7.4); (3) pin deflection: ╬┤=F┬иL┬│/(3┬иE┬иI) РЅц 0.05mm allowable (Euler-Bernoulli cantilever, Beaumont ┬Д9.3, I=¤ђ┬иdРЂ┤/64, E=200 GPa steel); (4) knockout bar contact: plate_thickness РЅЦ bar_diameter (Beaumont ┬Д9.5); `EjectorStrokeReport` dataclass (stroke_adequate, force_per_pin, max_deflection_mm, violations); LLM tool `mold_verify_ejector_stroke` registered; 33 oracle tests; static load only (honest-flagged: no dynamic ejection force, shrinkage grip, thermal expansion, or pin fatigue) Рђћ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/ejector_stroke_verify.py` РюЁ.
**Manufacturing depth** РюЁ Рђћ **MOLD-WALL-THICKNESS-FLOW-LEAD** (Beaumont 2007 ┬Д4 Table 4.2 + Menges 2001 ┬Д6.2.1): `compute_flow_length_check()` Рђћ flow-length-to-wall-thickness (L/T) ratio per cavity feature; primary short-shot risk indicator; MATERIAL_LT_LIMITS dict (ABS=150, PC=220, PP=300, PA66=250, POM=200, PMMA=180); risk: РЅц80% limit Рєњ safe, 80РђЊ100% Рєњ caution, >100% Рєњ short_shot; recommended_min_thickness_mm = flow_length/(limit├Ќ0.85) (15% safety margin); `FlowFeature` + `FlowLengthReport` dataclasses; LLM tool `mold_check_flow_length` registered; 23 oracle tests; honest-flagged: L/T ratio only Рђћ NOT Hagen-Poiseuille pressure-drop simulation, melt-front thermal analysis, or multi-gate flow balance; use Moldflow/Moldex3D/SigmaSoft for full fill simulation Рђћ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/flow_length_check.py` РюЁ.
**Manufacturing depth** РюЁ Рђћ **MOLD-COOLING-TIME-CHEN-CHIANG** (Chen-Chiang 1985 + Menges 2001 ┬Д7.3.3 + Beaumont 2007 ┬Д10.4): `compute_cooling_time_chen_chiang()` Рђћ 1-D Fourier first-term cooling-time formula: t_c = (h┬▓/¤ђ┬▓╬▒)┬иln[(8/¤ђ┬▓)┬и(T_mРѕњT_w)/(T_eРѕњT_w)]; `MaterialThermalProps` dataclass (name, thermal_diffusivity_m2_per_s, T_melt_C, T_ejection_C); `CoolingTimeReport` dataclass (wall_thickness_mm, cooling_time_s, dominant_factor, material_used, honest_caveat); MATERIAL_THERMAL_DB (Menges 2001 Table 7.3): ABS ╬▒=1.00e-7, PC ╬▒=1.50e-7, PP ╬▒=0.95e-7, PA66 ╬▒=1.40e-7, POM ╬▒=0.95e-7, PMMA ╬▒=1.13e-7 m┬▓/s; dominant-factor diagnosis (thickness_squared|diffusivity|temp_window) via log-sensitivity; LLM tool `mold_compute_cooling_time_chen_chiang` registered; 24 oracle tests; honest-flagged: 1-D Fourier first-term approximation only Рђћ ignores cooling-channel layout and conformal-cooling effects; does NOT model crystallisation latent heat (semi-crystalline PP/PA66/POM times 15РђЊ30% longer), thermal contact resistance, or hot-spot effects from varying wall thickness; use Moldflow/Moldex3D/SigmaSoft for a full cooling-circuit simulation Рђћ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/cooling_time_chen_chiang.py` РюЁ.
**Manufacturing depth** РюЁ Рђћ **MOLD-RUNNER-BALANCE-CHECK** (Beaumont 2007 ┬Д6.6 + Menges 2001 ┬Д6.6.4): `check_runner_balance()` Рђћ Hagen-Poiseuille hydraulic resistance path check for multi-cavity runner networks; R_norm = L/rРЂ┤ per segment (╬╝ cancels in ratios); path resistance summed sprueРєњgate via parent-pointer walk; max_imbalance_pct = 100├Ќ(R_maxРѕњR_min)/R_mean; balanced=True iff max_imbalance_pct < 5 % (Beaumont 2007 ┬Д6.6 criterion); `RunnerSegment` dataclass (id, length_mm, diameter_mm, parent_id); `RunnerBalanceReport` dataclass (cavity_paths[{cavity_id, total_length_mm, total_resistance, fill_ratio}], max_imbalance_pct, balanced, honest_caveat); LLM tool `mold_check_runner_balance` registered; 42 oracle tests; honest-flagged: geometric resistance only Рђћ does NOT model temperature-dependent or shear-thinning viscosity, shear-heating asymmetry in graduated-diameter (artificially balanced) runners (Beaumont RPI runner), or transient filling inertia; use Moldflow/Moldex3D/SigmaSoft for full rheological fill simulation Рђћ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/runner_balance_check.py` РюЁ.
**Manufacturing depth** РюЁ Рђћ mold draft-angle validation per face: arcsin(|n╠ѓ┬иpull╠ѓ|) draft angle; SPI finish grades A1РђЊD3 minimum lookup (Menges 2001 ┬Д3.4 + Beaumont 2007 ┬Д4); region-aware minimums (outer 0.5┬░, inner 1.0┬░, rib 1.0┬░, boss 0.5┬░); top/bottom face pass-through; degenerate-normal flagging; LLM tool `mold_validate_draft`; **undercut detection РюЁ** (Menges ┬Д6.4): `detect_undercuts(UndercutSpec) Рєњ UndercutReport`; ╬И=acos(n╠ѓ┬иp╠ѓ) face classification: direct undercut (╬И>90┬░ below parting line), hidden undercut (bounding-box shadow proxy for occluded faces), vertical wall (╬ИРЅѕ90┬░); severity buckets none/minor/major/severe; `requires_side_action` + `requires_lifter` flags; `FaceData` + `UndercutSpec` + `UndercutReport` dataclasses; 34 new oracle tests (72 total); honest-caveat: centroid-normal + bbox-shadow proxy Рђћ confirm with Moldflow/Moldex3D/SigmaSoft or DFM review РюЁ.

**Manufacturing depth** РюЁ Рђћ **MOLD-DRAFT-DEMOLD-FORCE** (Beaumont 2007 ┬Д9.3 + Menges 2001 ┬Д7.4 + Table 7.6): `compute_demold_force()` Рђћ cavity-ejection force per F = ╬╝┬и¤Ѓ_h┬иA┬иcos╬▒/(cos╬▒ + ╬╝┬иsin╬▒); shrinkage stress ¤Ѓ_h from Menges Table 7.6 (ABS=4.0, PC=3.0, PP=5.0, PA66=3.5, POM=4.5 MPa); friction ╬╝ from SPI finish class (SPI_A1=0.15 polished Рђд SPI_D1=0.40 textured); `MoldedPartSpec` dataclass (polymer_grade, contact_area_cm2, draft_angle_deg, mold_steel_finish_class); `DemoldForceReport` dataclass (demold_force_N, contact_pressure_MPa, ejector_pin_count_required, friction_coeff_used, polymer_shrinkage_stress_MPa, honest_caveat); ejector pin count = ceil(F / single_pin_capacity_N); LLM tool `mold_compute_demold_force` registered; 28 oracle tests; honest-flagged: empirical formula only Рђћ ignores chemical adhesion (resin stick, relevant for PC/POM on polished steel), undercut/side-action geometry, dynamic ejection force, and pin fatigue; confirm by mold-trial load-cell measurement Рђћ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/demold_force_check.py` РюЁ.
**Manufacturing depth** РюЁ Рђћ **MOLD-VENT-DEPTH-CHECK** (Beaumont 2007 ┬Д8.3 Table 8.2 + Menges 2001 ┬Д6.4 Table 6.7): `check_vent_depth()` Рђћ verify that a mold parting-line vent depth (air-escape gap) is within the polymer-specific recommended range; too shallow Рєњ trapped air Рєњ short shot / burn marks (diesel effect); too deep Рєњ flash; polymer database (mm): ABS 0.025РђЊ0.038, PC 0.013РђЊ0.025, PP 0.025РђЊ0.050, PA66 0.013РђЊ0.025, POM 0.013РђЊ0.025, PMMA 0.025РђЊ0.038, PE 0.038РђЊ0.075; `VentSpec` dataclass (polymer_grade, proposed_depth_mm, land_length_mm=1.5, vent_width_mm=6.0); `VentDepthReport` dataclass (recommended_depth_min_mm, recommended_depth_max_mm, compliant, depth_class, polymer_notes, honest_caveat); depth_class: "too_shallow"|"correct"|"too_deep"|"flash_risk" (>25% above max); unknown polymers receive fallback range [0.013РђЊ0.038 mm] with caveat; LLM tool `mold_check_vent_depth` registered; 35 oracle tests; honest-flagged: empirical handbook ranges only Рђћ actual safe vent depth depends on resin batch viscosity, melt temperature, injection speed, mold surface finish, land length, and part geometry; filled/FR/rubber-toughened grades may flash within the correct band for base resin; confirm by mold trial + visual flash inspection Рђћ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/vent_depth_check.py` РюЁ.
**Manufacturing depth** РюЁ Рђћ **MOLD-VENT-SLOT-LAYOUT** (Beaumont 2007 ┬Д8.5 Vent Slot Count and Width + Menges 2001 ┬Д6.4): `generate_vent_slot_layout()` Рђћ propose vent slot count, width (6 mm standard), and spacing for a parting-line perimeter given cavity volume, polymer grade, and injection speed; Beaumont 0.5 %-projected-area rule: total_vent_area РЅЦ 0.005 ├Ќ cavity_volume_mm┬│/wall_thickness; speed scaling: vent_area_factor = max(1.0, injection_speed / 50 cm┬│/s); per-slot area = 6 mm width ├Ќ depth_mid ├Ќ 6 mm land length (polymer-specific depth from Beaumont Table 8.2); minimum 4 slots (one per quadrant, Beaumont ┬Д8.5; Menges ┬Д6.4); maximum slots = floor(perimeter / (6 + 10 mm steel bridge)); spacing = perimeter / n_slots; `MoldVolumeSpec` dataclass (cavity_volume_cm3, parting_line_perimeter_mm, polymer_grade, injection_speed_cm3_s); `VentSlotLayoutReport` dataclass (num_vent_slots, vent_slot_width_mm, vent_slot_spacing_mm, total_vent_width_mm, air_displacement_rate_cm3_s, adequate, honest_caveat); LLM tool `mold_generate_vent_slot_layout` registered; 47 oracle tests; honest-flagged: heuristic 0.5 %-area rule from production experience Рђћ NOT a first-principles fluid-dynamic calculation; wall thickness assumed 3 mm for area estimation; uniform spacing only (use mold_optimize_vent_placement for last-to-fill location optimisation); vent depth handled separately by mold_check_vent_depth; confirm by fill simulation (Moldflow / Moldex3D / SigmaSoft) + mold-trial visual inspection Рђћ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/vent_slot_layout.py` РюЁ.
**Manufacturing depth** РюЁ Рђћ **MOLD-RUNNER-COLD-SLUG** (Beaumont 2007 ┬Д6.7 Cold Slug Wells + Menges 2001 ┬Д6.5): `check_cold_slug_design()` Рђћ verify cold-slug well dimensions at runner junctions in a multi-cavity mold to trap the cold leading-edge polymer melt before it reaches the gate, preventing flow lines and weak weld lines; Beaumont rule: slug well diameter = 1.5 ├Ќ runner diameter, depth = 2.0 ├Ќ runner diameter, ┬▒20 % tolerance band (1.2├ЌРђЊ1.8├Ќ diameter, 1.6├ЌРђЊ2.4├Ќ depth); `RunnerJunctionSpec` dataclass (junction_id, runner_diameter_mm, slug_well_diameter_mm, slug_well_depth_mm, polymer_grade); `ColdSlugReport` dataclass (junction_results list, total_junctions, compliant_count, honest_caveat); per-junction result: diameter_compliant, depth_compliant, slug_well_compliant, recommended_diameter_mm, recommended_depth_mm, tolerance bounds, reason; LLM tool `mold_check_cold_slug_design` registered; 32 oracle tests; honest-flagged: geometric rule-of-thumb only Рђћ actual cold-slug capture depends on melt temperature, injection speed, and resin freeze-off time; fast-crystallising resins (POM, PA66, LCP) and filled grades may require larger wells; confirm by mold trial + gate-area visual inspection; use Moldflow / Moldex3D / SigmaSoft for full melt-front thermal and weld-line simulation Рђћ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/cold_slug_check.py` РюЁ.

**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ Gaussian beam (complex-q + ABCD + M┬▓ + fibre coupling); non-sequential ray tracing + ghost detection; wave-domain room acoustics (image-source IR + Schroeder RT60 + SEA); Seidel S5 corrected; **Zernike polynomial wavefront fitting** (OPTICS-ZERNIKE-WAVEFRONT-FIT): first 15 Noll-ordered terms (j=1..15, piston through tetrafoil); explicit Z_j(¤Ђ,╬И) formulas (Noll 1976 Table 1 orthonormal basis); least-squares fit via numpy.linalg.lstsq; RMS residual; dominant aberration = argmax(|c_j|) for jРЅЦ2 (piston excluded); LLM tool `optics_fit_zernike_wavefront`; 32 hermetic tests. Honest: unit-disk pupil only; first 15 terms only Рђћ higher-order content aliases into residual; no wavefront OPD tracing (sampled W(¤Ђ,╬И) input only). Ref: Noll (1976) J. Opt. Soc. Am. 66 207; Born & Wolf ┬Д9.2; Wyant & Creath (1992).
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ Gaussian beam (complex-q + ABCD + M┬▓ + fibre coupling); non-sequential ray tracing + ghost detection; wave-domain room acoustics (image-source IR + Schroeder RT60 + SEA); Seidel S5 corrected; **sequential paraxial + meridional ray trace** through multi-element lens stacks (Welford 1986 ┬Д3.3/┬Д5, exact Snell + Newton-Raphson conic intersect; EFL/BFL/FFL; Hecht oracle biconvex BK7 <0.1% error; Cooke triplet converging verified); **MTF across field angle** (OPTICS-MTF-ACROSS-FIELD) Рђћ ray-bundle PSF histogram + numpy.fft.rfft pipeline; tangential MTF curves at multiple field angles; BK7 biconvex off-axis MTF drop verified; LLM tool `optics_mtf_across_field` (monochromatic); **polychromatic MTF across field** РюЁ (OPTICS-MTF-ACROSS-FIELD-POLYCHROMATIC): `compute_polychromatic_mtf_across_field(spec, wavelength_samples_nm, spd_weights)` Рєњ `MTF_poly(f) = ╬Б W(╬╗_i)┬иMTF(f, ╬╗_i) / ╬Б W(╬╗_i)`; per-wavelength monochromatic MTF computed then interpolated onto a common frequency grid; standard SPD helpers: `photopic_spd` (CIE V(╬╗), peak 555 nm), `d65_spd` (CIE D65, CIE Pub.15:2004), `blackbody_spd` (Planck 1901); `PolychromaticMTFSpec` input dataclass; per-angle chromatic failure isolation; 32 hermetic tests (11 monochromatic + 21 polychromatic). Ref: Hecht SS11.2; Smith SS11.3; CIE DS 013.3:2018; CIE Pub. 15:2004.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ Gaussian beam (complex-q + ABCD + M┬▓ + fibre coupling); non-sequential ray tracing + ghost detection; wave-domain room acoustics (image-source IR + Schroeder RT60 + SEA); **Seidel third-order aberrations** (OPTICS-SEIDEL-ABERRATIONS): five Seidel coefficients S_I..S_V via dual paraxial-ray trace (Welford 1986 ┬Д6.2 / Born & Wolf ┬Д5.3); per-surface breakdown; LLM tool `optics_seidel_aberrations`; 33 hermetic tests. **Zernike wavefront decomposition via finite-ray OPD РюЁ** (OPTICS-SEIDEL-ZERNIKE-OPD): `decompose_wavefront_zernike(surfaces, field_height_mm, aperture_radius_mm, num_pupil_samples=128)` traces a 4-ring hexapolar pupil bundle (¤Ђ=0.25/0.5/0.75/1.0) as 3-D skew rays (trace_skew_ray, Born & Wolf ┬Д4.6); OPD_k = OPL_k Рѕњ OPL_chief (Welford ┬Д5.5); fits Z_1..Z_36 (Noll 1976 orthonormal basis, piston through 7th-order) via numpy.linalg.lstsq; returns `ZernikeReport(coefficients[36], rms_waves, pv_waves, strehl_estimate=exp(Рѕњ(2¤ђ┬иRMS)┬▓), coefficient_names, fit_rms_residual, n_rays_valid, honest_caveat)`; key map: Z_4=defocus, Z_5/Z_6=astigmatism, Z_7/Z_8=coma, Z_11=primary spherical (W040), Z_12/Z_13=5th-order astig, Z_16/Z_17=secondary coma, Z_22=secondary spherical (W060); Strehl by Mar├Еchal approx (Born & Wolf ┬Д9.3.2); 15 hermetic tests (aberration-free РЅѕ 0, defocus Z_4 dominant, coma off-axis nonzero, Strehl Рѕѕ [0,1], PVРЅЦRMS, afocal/empty/bad-args error paths, 36-coeff names). Honest: monochromatic; conic surfaces only; stop at first surface; Mar├Еchal Strehl valid only for RMSРЅф1 wave.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Chief-ray vignetting + relative illumination** (OPTICS-CHIEF-RAY-VIGNETTING): marginal-ray bundle traced at each field angle; per-surface clear-aperture clipping check; RI = surviving fraction; cosРЂ┤(╬И) photometric baseline; excess-vignetting ratio; LLM tool `optics_compute_vignetting` (Welford 1986 ┬Д4.5 / Hecht ┬Д6.6; circular symmetric apertures; 33 hermetic tests).
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **2-D relative illumination map** (OPTICS-RELATIVE-ILLUM-MAP): extends vignetting analysis to a full (grid ├Ќ grid) heatmap across the image plane; for each (x, y) sensor position computes ╬И = arctan(r/EFL) and evaluates RI(╬И) = surviving ray fraction via compute_vignetting; ri_map (aperture-clipping model) + cos4_map (natural cosРЂ┤(╬И) photometric baseline, Hecht ┬Д6.6 / Slyusarev ┬Д3.4); rotational-symmetry shortcut (1-D radial pre-computation, full 2-D output for visualisation); corner_ri + corner_cos4 diagnostics; BK7 biconvex @ sensor_half_height=60 mm Рєњ ╬И_corner РЅѕ 60┬░, cos4_corner РЅѕ 0.063; LLM tool `optics_compute_relative_illum_map`; 38 hermetic tests. Honest: monochromatic only; rotationally-symmetric stack assumed; sensor tilt / telecentricity not modelled. Ref: Welford 1986 ┬Д4.5; Hecht ┬Д6.6; Slyusarev ┬Д3.4.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Spot diagrams + pupil illumination maps** (OPTICS-PUPIL-DIAGRAM): uniform pupil-grid ray trace (Welford 1986 ┬Д8.2); per-field intercept loci at image plane; 2-D RMS + meridional y-only RMS spot radius; max ray distance from chief ray; exit-pupil illumination map (surviving pupil coords); paraxial exit-pupil position estimate (Welford 1986 ┬Д3.5 / Hecht ┬Д5.7); stigmatic stack Рєњ RMS < 1e-6 mm; BK7 biconvex at 14┬░ Рєњ y-RMS > 3├Ќ on-axis; Seidel coma cross-check; LLM tool `optics_pupil_diagram` (monochromatic; sagittal x = first-order estimate; 33 hermetic tests). **3-D skew-ray pupil diagram** РюЁ (`use_skew_ray=True`): hexapolar bundle (Born & Wolf ┬Д4.6 / Welford ┬Д5) via `Ray3D`/`OpticalSurface`/`trace_skew_ray` from `skew_ray_tracer.py`; rigorous x+y intercepts; vignetting fraction (TIR/missed-surface rays counted); `vignetting_fraction` per field; entry-pupil + exit-pupil illumination shape from surviving hexapolar coords. **Chief-ray back-trace for exit-pupil position** РюЁ: `compute_exit_pupil_chief_ray(surfaces, stop_index) Рєњ ExitPupilReport`; chief ray (h=0 at aperture stop) traced forward through downstream surfaces; axis-crossing in image space gives exact exit-pupil position (`exit_pupil_z_mm`, `exit_pupil_distance_from_last_surface_mm`); image-space telecentric detection (EP Рєњ Рѕъ); asymmetric stack (stop at different surface) verified Рєњ EP moves; Welford 1986 ┬Д3.5. **45 hermetic tests** (33 original + 12 new: skew on-axis RMS nonzero, skew RMS grows with field, use_skew_ray flag, rays-traced positive, vignetting fraction zero (no clear-ap clipping), pupil-coords count, EP symmetric lens virtual, EP asymmetric lens differs, EP bad-stop error, to_dict ok, y-RMS comparable skew vs meridional, all intercepts finite). `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/optics/pupil_diagram.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Through-focus defocus curve** (OPTICS-DEFOCUS-CURVE): Welford 1986 ┬Д11.5 / Hecht ┬Д6.5; per-╬ћz meridional RMS spot-size via exact Snell + Newton-Raphson conic intersect; best-focus shift quantified; parabolic curve verified for paraxial singlet (min at ╬ћz=0); spherical-aberration-shifted minimum verified for full-aperture BK7 singlet (╬ћzРЅѕРѕњ0.5 mm); field-angle dependency; LLM tool `optics_defocus_curve`; **skew-ray defocus** РюЁ: `use_skew_ray=True` traces 2-D polar pupil grid via `trace_skew_ray` (Born & Wolf ┬Д4.6 / Welford ┬Д5) computing full 3-D RMS including sagittal+tangential contributions; **spectral defocus** РюЁ: `spectral_weights=[(╬╗_nm, w), ...]` with `use_skew_ray=True` computes polychromatic weighted-RMS defocus curve (Hecht ┬Д6.3 / Welford ┬Д6.5) Рђћ chromatic focus shift verified (blue BFL < red BFL for BK7 singlet); 47 hermetic tests (33 original + 14 new: skew-ray V-shape, skew vs paraxial agreement in paraxial limit, spectral chromatic shift, honest-flag mode content, error paths for spectral without skew). Honest: meridional mode = monochromatic tangential RMS only; skew-ray mode = full 2-D spot RMS, spectral weighting supported; conic surfaces only (no higher-order aspheric terms). `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/optics/defocus_curve.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **3-D skew-ray tracing** (OPTICS-SKEW-RAY): full 6-DOF ray tracing through sequential conicoid surfaces (Born & Wolf ┬Д4.6 / Welford 1986 ┬Д5). `Ray3D(origin_xyz, direction_xyz, wavelength_nm=587.6)`, `OpticalSurface(vertex_z_mm, radius_mm, refractive_index_after, conic_k=0)`, `RayTraceResult(ray_history, final_position_xyz, final_direction_xyz, tir_occurred, honest_caveat)`. Algorithm: (1) rayРђЊconicoid parametric quadratic intersection; (2) grad-F surface normal oriented to oppose incident ray; (3) 3-D vector Snell's law d' = (n1/n2)┬иd + (n1/n2┬иcos_i Рѕњ cos_t)┬иN╠ѓ (Born & Wolf ┬Д1.5.3 eq. 1.5.23 / Shirley ┬Д8.2); (4) TIR detected when sin┬▓╬И_t > 1; full ray history preserved. Supports sphere (k=0), paraboloid (k=Рѕњ1), hyperboloid (k<Рѕњ1), oblate ellipsoid (k>0), flat plane (R=0). LLM tool `optics_trace_skew_ray`; 20 hermetic tests (axial on-axis symmetry, skew x/y height refraction, TIR at >41.3┬░ in glassРєњair, paraboloid vs sphere intersection, flat surface same/different n, biconvex BK7 convergence, Snell angle verify, azimuthal symmetry, wavelength preservation, history length, empty surface list, honest_caveat). Honest: monochromatic only; conic surfaces only (no A4/A6 higher-order aspheric terms); sequential only; no aperture-stop clipping Рђћ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/optics/skew_ray_tracer.py`. Refs: Born & Wolf (1999) ┬Д1.5.3, ┬Д4.6; Welford (1986) ┬Д5; Kingslake (1978) ┬Д2; Hecht (2017).
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Geometric distortion map** (OPTICS-DISTORTION-MAP): chief-ray tangential distortion vs field angle (Hecht ┬Д5.6 / Welford 1986 ┬Д6.3); D=(y_actualРѕњy_paraxial)/|y_paraxial|├Ќ100; barrel (D<0) / pincushion (D>0) / mixed classification; Seidel S_V third-order cross-check (Welford ┬Д6.3); BK7 biconvex singlet shows measurable barrel distortion at moderate field (>0.5% at 20┬░); kind classification verified for high-power singlet and telephoto stacks; LLM tool `optics_distortion_map`; 30 hermetic tests. Honest: monochromatic only; tangential (meridional) distortion only; stop assumed at first surface. **Spectral distortion integration** РюЁ (OPTICS-DISTORTION-MAP-SPECTRAL): `compute_spectral_distortion(distortion_func, field_angles_deg, wavelength_samples, spd_weights) Рєњ SpectralDistortionReport`; trapezoidal quadrature D╠ё(╬И)=РѕФD(╬И,╬╗)┬иSPD(╬╗)d╬╗/РѕФSPD(╬╗)d╬╗; chromatic residual ╬ћD(╬И)=D╠ё(╬И)РѕњD(╬И,╬╗_design); standard SPD helpers: `photopic_spd` (CIE V(╬╗), peak 555 nm), `d65_spd` (CIE D65, CIE Pub.15:2004), `blackbody_spd` (Planck 1901, Wien law verified); constant-D across ╬╗ Рєњ spectral==mono verified; linear-D Рєњ spectral average == mid-band value; photopic-weighted D╠ё biased toward 555 nm region; 10 new hermetic tests (tests 31РђЊ40). Ref: CIE DS 013.3:2018; CIE Pub. 15:2004; Press et al. NR3 ┬Д4.2.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Coma aberration metrics** (OPTICS-COMA-COMPUTE): comatic flare length from pupil-rim ray bundle trace (Welford 1986 ┬Д11.4 / Born & Wolf ┬Д5.3); for each field angle traces N marginal rays at entrance-pupil rim azimuths and propagates to paraxial focal plane; tangential coma = mean Y-displacement of tangential-fan rays from chief-ray image point; sagittal coma = tangential/3 (Welford ┬Д11.4 eq. 11.4.4); total coma = sqrt(tan┬▓+sag┬▓); Seidel S_II prediction = 3├Ќ|S_II|├Ќ|y_chief| (Born & Wolf ┬Д5.3 eq. 5.3.29); depth bar: BK7 biconvex at 14┬░ Рєњ coma > 1 ╬╝m; Seidel match < 0.1% at 5┬░ field; **finite-ray OPD coma РюЁ** (Welford ┬Д5.5 / Born & Wolf ┬Д9.2): `compute_finite_ray_coma(surfaces, field_height_mm, num_pupil_samples=64)` traces N pupil samples as 3-D skew rays (trace_skew_ray), accumulates OPL = ╬Б n_k┬и|seg_k|, computes OPD_i = OPL_i Рѕњ OPL_chief, fits Noll Z_7 (coma_y = Рѕџ8┬и(3¤Ђ┬│Рѕњ2¤Ђ)┬иsin╬И) via direct inner-product estimator; returns `FiniteRayOpdReport(wave_aberration_W131_rms_waves, zernike_Z7_coeff, compared_to_seidel, seidel_rms_waves, n_rays_valid, honest_caveat)`; opt-in via `compute_coma(..., compute_opd=True)` Рєњ `ComaReport.opd_per_field`; afocal stacks return error dict; LLM tool `optics_compute_coma`; 43 hermetic tests (10 new OPD tests). Honest: monochromatic only; stop at first surface; higher-order aspheric terms (A4, A6...) not modelled by skew tracer; Z_7-only RMS projection excludes higher-order coma Zernike terms (Z_14, Z_17...).
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Seidel coma coefficient S_II** (OPTICS-SEIDEL-COMA): per-surface third-order Seidel coma sum S_II = ╬Б (РѕњA_j┬и─ђ_j┬иh_j┬и╬ћ(u/n)_j) via dual paraxial-ray trace (Welford 1986 ┬Д7 eq. 7.42 / Born & Wolf ┬Д5.3); SeidelComaReport dataclass: S_II (total Seidel coma sum), coma_waves_at_lambda (|3┬иS_II┬иy_chief|/(8╬╗)), dominant_surface_idx (argmax|S_II_j|), per_surface_contributions (A, ─ђ, h, ybar, delta_un, SII_contrib per surface), honest_caveat; BK7 biconvex R1=+50/R2=Рѕњ50 mm on-axis Рєњ coma_waves = 0; same lens at 5┬░ Рєњ S_II nonzero; aplanatic BK7+SF2 contact doublet Рєњ |S_II| reduced vs singlet; flat slab Рєњ S_II = 0 exactly; **Seidel-vs-finite-ray coma comparison РюЁ**: `compute_seidel_coma(..., compare_seidel_to_finite_ray=True)` Рєњ `SeidelComaReport` with `finite_ray_W131` (Zernike Z_7 OPD waves), `residual_higher_order_W131` (finite_ray Рѕњ seidel, waves), `comparison_caveat` populated via `compute_finite_ray_coma()`; new `compare_seidel_vs_finite_ray_coma(surfaces, field_height_mm, num_pupil_samples=64) Рєњ ComaCompareReport` for direct head-to-head: `ComaCompareReport(seidel_W131_waves, finite_ray_W131_waves, residual_W131_waves, residual_fraction, seidel_S_II, finite_ray_zernike_Z7, n_rays_valid, field_height_mm, wavelength_mm, comparison_caveat)`; residual positive = higher-order coma present beyond Seidel third-order prediction; LLM tool `optics_compute_seidel_coma`; 42 hermetic tests (34 original + 8 new: backward-compat, compare flag, low-aberration residual РЅѕ 0, strong-coma residual finite, to_dict keys, ComaCompareReport contract, afocal error). Honest: paraxial Seidel only for S_II path; finite-ray path via 3-D skew rays + Zernike Z_7 Рђћ higher-order aspheric terms not modelled; no chromatic coma; stop at first surface. Ref: Welford (1986) ┬Д7 eq. 7.42 + ┬Д5.5; Born & Wolf (1999) ┬Д5.3 eq. 5.3.29 + ┬Д9.2; Noll (1976); Kingslake (1978).
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Seidel coma coefficient (thin-lens polynomial)** (OPTICS-COMA-COEFFICIENT): closed-form S_II and Hopkins W_131 for a single thin lens via Welford ┬Д7.4 shape-factor/conjugate-factor polynomial; `ThinLensSpec(focal_length_mm, refractive_index_n, aperture_radius_mm, shape_factor_q, conjugate_factor_p)` + `ImageSpec(object_height_mm, image_distance_mm)` Рєњ `ComaCoefficientReport(seidel_S_II, wave_aberration_W_131, sagittal_coma_arcsec, tangential_coma_arcsec=3├Ќsagittal, coma_blur_mm, q_aplanatic, honest_caveat)`; formula: S_II = u_bar┬иh┬│┬и¤є┬▓┬и[(n+1)/(2n(nРѕњ1))┬иq + (Рѕњ(2n+1)/(2n))┬и(p+2)] where q=(RРѓЂ+RРѓѓ)/(RРѓЂРѕњRРѓѓ) and p=(uРђ▓+u)/(uРђ▓Рѕњu); numerically verified vs two-surface paraxial trace across qРѕѕ{Рѕњ1,Рѕњ0.5,0,0.5,1} and pРѕѕ{Рѕњ1,0,1} for nРѕѕ{1.4,1.5,1.5168,1.6,1.7,1.8} (all within 1e-10 relative); aplanatic shape q=(2n+1)(nРѕњ1)(p+2)/(n+1) gives S_II=0 exactly; BK7 (n=1.5168, p=Рѕњ1): q_aplanaticРЅѕ0.8283; angular coma = S_II/(8┬иF#┬иv)├Ќ206265 arcsec; W_131=РѕњS_II (Hopkins sign convention, Born & Wolf ┬Д5.5.3); LLM tool `optics_compute_coma_coefficient`; 25 hermetic tests. Honest: third-order Seidel only Рђћ fifth-order Schwarzschild coma and higher-order Hopkins terms NOT included; single thin lens in air; stop coincident with lens; monochromatic only. Ref: Welford (1986) ┬Д7.4; Born & Wolf (1999) ┬Д5.3 eq. 5.3.29 + ┬Д5.5.3; Smith MOE (2008) ┬Д4.3.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ Gaussian beam (complex-q + ABCD + M┬▓ + fibre coupling); non-sequential ray tracing + ghost detection; wave-domain room acoustics (image-source IR + Schroeder RT60 + SEA); Seidel S5 corrected. **Longitudinal chromatic aberration + achromatic doublet design** (OPTICS-CHROMATIC-FOCUS): Sellmeier dispersion n(╬╗) = sqrt(1 + ╬Б B_i ╬╗┬▓/(╬╗┬▓РѕњC_i)) for BK7/F2/SF6/K5/SF11/BK10/K7/BAK4/SF2 (Schott catalog 2023); per-wavelength BFL via ABCD thin-lens stack; LCA_FC = BFL(486nm)РѕњBFL(656nm); Abbe V-number (singlet); BK7 VРЅѕ64.2 verified; achromat LCA < 0.1 mm verified; **`design_achromatic_doublet(f_mm, crown, flint)` РюЁ** (Smith MOE ┬Д6.4): first-order colour null via ¤єРѓЂ = ¤є┬иVРѓЂ/(VРѓЂРѕњVРѓѓ), ¤єРѓѓ = Рѕњ¤є┬иVРѓѓ/(VРѓЂРѕњVРѓѓ); supports BK7/K7/BAK4 crowns ├Ќ F2/SF2/SF11 flints; `AchromaticDoubletReport` with f1_mm, f2_mm, nd/V per element, residual Sellmeier LCA; near-apochromatic guard (|╬ћV| < 5 Рєњ error); power conservation and achromatic condition validated to 1e-14; doublet residual < 10% of equivalent singlet LCA; 47 hermetic tests (34 LCA + 13 doublet designer). Honest: first-order thin-lens only; secondary spectrum not nulled; thick-lens principal-plane chromatic shift not modelled; LLM tool `optics_compute_chromatic_focus`.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Abbe number + partial dispersion** (OPTICS-ABBE-NUMBER-COMPUTE): V_d = (n_d Рѕњ 1) / (n_F Рѕњ n_C) from Sellmeier Fraunhofer lines d/F/C (Hecht ┬Д6.3 / ISO 10110); secondary spectrum partial dispersion P_{F,g} = (n_g Рѕњ n_F) / (n_F Рѕњ n_C) for g-line (435.84 nm); six glasses BK7/F2/SF6/K5/SF11/BK10 (Schott 2023); BK7 V_d = 64.17, F2 = 36.37, SF6 = 25.43, K5 = 59.45, BK10 = 66.95 Рђћ all within 0.1% of catalog; SF11 = 25.37 (catalog 25.76, 1.5% gap documented Рђћ Sellmeier fit vs direct spectrophotometric measurement, Schott TIE-29 ┬Д3.3); LLM tool `optics_compute_abbe_number`; 30 hermetic tests. Honest: catalog nominal/melt-mean coefficients; melt-to-melt V_d variation ┬▒0.3РђЊ0.5% (Schott TIE-31).
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ Gaussian beam (complex-q + ABCD + M┬▓ + fibre coupling); non-sequential ray tracing + ghost detection; wave-domain room acoustics (image-source IR + Schroeder RT60 + SEA); Seidel S5 corrected.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **2-D relative illumination map** (OPTICS-RELATIVE-ILLUM-MAP): extends vignetting analysis to a full (grid ├Ќ grid) heatmap across the image plane; for each (x, y) sensor position computes ╬И = arctan(r/EFL) and evaluates RI(╬И) = surviving ray fraction via compute_vignetting; ri_map (aperture-clipping model: all 1.0 with no CA, drops with finite CAs) + cos4_map (natural cosРЂ┤(╬И) photometric baseline, Hecht ┬Д6.6 / Slyusarev ┬Д3.4); rotational-symmetry shortcut (1-D radial pre-computation, full 2-D output for visualisation); corner_ri + corner_cos4 diagnostics; BK7 biconvex @ sensor_half_height=60 mm Рєњ ╬И_corner РЅѕ 60┬░, cos4_corner РЅѕ 0.063; LLM tool `optics_compute_relative_illum_map`; 38 hermetic tests.
