**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Entrance pupil position + size** (OPTICS-ENTRANCE-PUPIL-POS): paraxial reverse-trace of a marginal ray from the aperture stop through the front sub-stack (Welford 1986 ┬Д4.4 / Hecht ┬Д6.6); position_z_mm from first surface vertex; D-element transverse magnification; converging front Рєњ real pupil (positive z); diverging front Рєњ virtual pupil (negative z); LLM tool `optics_compute_entrance_pupil`; 38 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial only; exit pupil is a separate computation; stop modelled as thin plane; paraxial approx degrades for f/# < 2.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Exit pupil position + size** (OPTICS-EXIT-PUPIL-POS): paraxial two-ray forward trace from the aperture stop through the rear sub-stack (Welford 1986 ┬Д4.4 / Hecht ┬Д6.6); position_z_mm from last surface vertex; radius from stop-edge ray height at exit pupil plane; thin-lens identity (stop at last surface Рєњ EP at z=0, m=1); BK7 biconvex Рєњ virtual exit pupil (zРЅѕРѕњ3.41 mm, Welford ┬Д4.4 oracle); afocal telescope (f_obj=100 mm, f_eye=25 mm) Рєњ Ramsden disk at z=31.25 mm, radius=1.25 mm, m=0.25=1/M_telescope (Hecht ┬Д6.6 oracle); LLM tool `optics_compute_exit_pupil`; 43 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial only; entrance pupil is a separate computation; stop modelled as thin plane; paraxial approx degrades for f/# < 2.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Diffraction-limited MTF for circular aperture** (OPTICS-MTF-DIFFRACTION-LIMITED): closed-form on-axis MTF(╬й) = (2/¤ђ)[arccos(╬й/╬йРѓђ) Рѕњ (╬й/╬йРѓђ)┬иРѕџ(1Рѕњ(╬й/╬йРѓђ)┬▓)] for ╬й РЅц ╬йРѓђ, 0 otherwise; cutoff ╬йРѓђ = 1/(╬╗┬иF#) = 2┬иNA/╬╗ (Goodman "Introduction to Fourier Optics" ┬Д6.4 eq. 6-49; Hecht "Optics" 5e ┬Д11.3.3); oracle: ╬╗=550nm, F/4 Рєњ ╬йРѓђ=454.5 cyc/mm, MTF(0)=1.0, MTF(╬йРѓђ/2)РЅѕ0.391 Рђћ all validated to < 0.1%; **polychromatic MTF РюЁ**: `compute_polychromatic_diffraction_mtf(numerical_aperture, wavelength_samples_nm, spd_weights, num_spatial_freq=128)` Рєњ `PolyMTFReport`; algorithm: MTF_poly(╬й) = ╬Б_i W(╬╗_i)┬иMTF_diff(╬й,╬╗_i) / ╬Б_i W(╬╗_i) (Hopkins / Goodman ┬Д6.4); cutoff per ╬╗: ╬йРѓђ(╬╗) = 2┬иNA/╬╗ Рђћ longer ╬╗ cut off earlier so broadband MTF РЅц best-╬╗ MTF; standard SPDs (photopic_spd / d65_spd / blackbody_spd) exported from same module; 20 new hermetic polychromatic tests (single-╬╗ reproduces monochromatic exactly; broadband РЅц best-╬╗; two-wavelength closed-form; D65 bounds; blackbody monotone; normalisation, cutoff values, error paths); LLM tool `optics_compute_diffraction_mtf`; 28 total hermetic tests. **analytic-form MTF РюЁ** (OPTICS-MTF-ANALYTIC-FORM): `compute_diffraction_mtf_analytic(numerical_aperture, wavelength_nm, num_spatial_freq=128)` Рєњ `AnalyticMTFReport`; direct evaluation of the Hopkins (1953) / Goodman ┬Д6.4 closed-form expression Рђћ no numerical integration; `AnalyticMTFReport` carries mtf_curve + landmark values (mtf_at_zero=1.0 exact, mtf_at_half_cutoffРЅѕ0.3909, mtf_at_cutoff=0.0 exact); analytic vs numerical max difference < 1e-10 over the full frequency range (machine precision); 16 new hermetic tests (boundary conditions, formula exactness, monotonicity, to_dict round-trip, values in [0,1], cutoff formula, analytic-vs-numerical agreement, analytic-vs-_mono_mtf_at < 1e-14, 6 error-path guards). Refs: Hopkins (1953) Proc. Royal Soc. London A 217, 408РђЊ432; Goodman ┬Д6.4 eq. 6-49. Total: 44 hermetic tests. Honest: diffraction-limited theoretical upper bound only Рђћ no aberrations (Seidel S_IРђЊS_V), no defocus, no wavefront error, no sensor MTF; circular aperture only; on-axis only.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Pixel aperture MTF + Nyquist limit** (OPTICS-PIXEL-MTF): `PixelSensorSpec(pixel_pitch_um, fill_factor=1.0)` Рєњ `PixelMtfReport(nyquist_freq_cyc_per_mm, mtf_curve, mtf_at_nyquist, mtf_at_50_percent_nyquist, honest_caveat)`; pixel aperture MTF = |sinc(¤ђ┬иa┬и╬й)| where a = pitch┬иfill_factor (Boreman "MTF in Optical and Electro-Optical Systems" ┬Д3.4; Hecht ┬Д11.3); Nyquist limit ╬й_N = 1/(2┬иp) caps detectable spatial frequency; oracle (p=1.5╬╝m, ff=1.0): ╬й_N=333.33 cyc/mm, MTF(0)=1.0 exactly, MTF(╬й_N)=2/¤ђРЅѕ0.6366 Рђћ all validated to < 1e-6; fill_factor < 1 Рєњ narrower aperture Рєњ slower sinc roll-off Рєњ MTF at Nyquist > 2/¤ђ (verified: ff=0.5 Рєњ MTF(╬й_N)РЅѕ0.900); `combine_mtf_curves(optical, pixel)` for incoherent cascade MTF_system = MTF_optical ├Ќ MTF_pixel (Boreman ┬Д2.1); LLM tool `optics_compute_pixel_mtf`; 36 hermetic tests. Honest: PIXEL APERTURE SINC ONLY Рђћ NOT modelled: silicon carrier-diffusion MTF (lateral minority-carrier spread vs. depth, Boreman ┬Д3.4); inter-pixel electrical/optical crosstalk; anti-aliasing filter MTF; Bayer CFA demosaicing resolution loss; charge-transfer inefficiency (CCD); non-square pixels; 2-D MTF = product of independent 1-D sincs for square pixel. Ref: Boreman (2001) ┬Д3.4, ┬Д2.1; Hecht (2017) ┬Д11.3; Holst & Lomheim (2007) ┬Д5.3. `kerf-cad-core/optics/pixel_mtf.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Petzval field curvature** (OPTICS-PETZVAL-CURVATURE-COMPUTE): Petzval sum P = ╬Б (n_after Рѕњ n_before) / (n_before ┬и n_after ┬и R_i) (Hecht ┬Д6.3.2 / Born & Wolf ┬Д4.5); Petzval radius R_P = 1/P; flat-field score 1/(1+|P|┬и100); BK7 biconvex oracle (R1=+50, R2=Рѕњ50, n=1.5168): P РЅѕ 0.01363 mmРЂ╗┬╣, R_P РЅѕ 73.4 mm (within 1%); flat-field condition ╬Б¤є/n = 0 Рєњ P = 0 verified; plano surfaces (|R|=1e18) contribute 0; stop-shift invariance; per-surface breakdown with is_plano flag; LLM tool `optics_compute_petzval_curvature`; 26 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial (third-order) only; does NOT include astigmatism (S_III term); P=0 guarantees flat Petzval sphere but not zero field curvature in the presence of astigmatism (Hecht ┬Д6.3.2); thick-lens pupil-shift corrections not modelled.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Spot diagram + encircled energy** (OPTICS-SPOT-DIAGRAM): fan-of-rays trace through sequential lens system; two trace paths: (1) paraxial-meridional (default, backward-compatible): ceil(sqrt(num_rays)) ├Ќ ceil(sqrt(num_rays)) Cartesian pupil grid over unit disk (Welford 1986 ┬Д8.2); exact meridional y-intercept via Snell + Newton-Raphson conic intersect (Welford ┬Д5.2-5.3); first-order sagittal x estimate (Hecht ┬Д5.7); (2) full 3-D skew-ray bundle (use_skew_ray=True): hexapolar pupil grid (1 + 3┬иN┬и(N+1) samples); `Ray3D`/`OpticalSurface`/`trace_skew_ray` from `skew_ray_tracer.py` (Born & Wolf ┬Д4.6 / Welford ┬Д5); rigorous x and y intercepts propagated to the paraxial image plane; `SpotDiagramResult` dataclass: image_points_xy (list[(float,float)], mm), rms_radius_mm (Welford ┬Д8.2 RMS), encircled_80pct_radius_mm (geometric EE80 radius, Hecht ┬Д6.3), centroid_xy, svg_diagram (SVG with RMS/EE80/Airy-disk rings + centroid marker + scale bar), honest_caveat; weak-lens paraxial singlet on-axis Рєњ near-zero y-spread (both paths); BK7 biconvex singlet at 10┬░ Рєњ rms > on-axis (coma verified; Hecht ┬Д6.3 / Welford ┬Д6); skew-ray spot grows with aperture (W040 spherical aberration РѕЮ ¤ЂРЂ┤); EE80 РЅЦ RMS monotonically; LLM tool `optics_compute_spot_diagram` (monochromatic only; stop at first surface; 33 hermetic tests). Ref: Hecht (2017) ┬Д6.3, ┬Д10.2; Welford (1986) ┬Д5.2-5.3, ┬Д6, ┬Д8.2; Born & Wolf (1999) ┬Д1.5.3, ┬Д4.6.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Piston/tip/tilt/defocus wavefront alignment analysis** (OPTICS-WAVEFRONT-PISTON-TIP-TILT): extracts ZРѓЂ (piston), ZРѓѓ (tip), ZРѓЃ (tilt), ZРѓё (defocus) Noll-ordered Zernike alignment components from a sampled wavefront W(¤Ђ,╬И); reports each in waves at a given wavelength via W_nm / wavelength_nm conversion; reuses fit_zernike_wavefront (4-term least-squares, numpy.linalg.lstsq, Noll 1976 orthonormal basis); `PistonTipTiltReport` dataclass (piston_waves, tip_waves, tilt_waves, defocus_waves, residual_rms_waves, dominant_misalignment, honest_caveat); dominant = argmax(|c_j|) for j=1..4 with "none" below 0.001 wave threshold; LLM tool `optics_analyze_wavefront_alignment`; 45 hermetic tests (pure piston 10nm @ ╬╗=632.8nm Рєњ 0.01580 waves verified; pure tip/tilt/defocus; combined misalignment; higher-order residual; error-path). Honest: circular unit-disk pupil only (¤Ђ Рѕѕ [0,1]; no obscuration or elliptical aperture); alignment analysis only Рђћ corrects rigid-body misalignment (piston = axial OPD offset, tip/tilt = wavefront tilt, defocus = longitudinal focus); does NOT correct higher-order aberrations (coma, astigmatism, spherical, etc.); use optics_fit_zernike_wavefront for full 15-term decomposition. Ref: Hecht (2017) ┬Д11.3; Born & Wolf (1999) ┬Д9.2; Wyant & Creath (1992) Applied Optics and Optical Engineering XI ch.1; Noll (1976) J. Opt. Soc. Am. 66 207.

**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Sagitta arrow chart** (OPTICS-SAGITTA-ARROW-CHART): conic + even-power aspheric surface sagitta z(r) sampled across the clear aperture; standard ISO 10110-12 ┬Д6.2 / Welford ┬Д3.3 formula z = c┬иr┬▓/(1+Рѕџ(1Рѕњ(1+k)c┬▓r┬▓)) + ╬Бaрхб┬иr^(2i+4); SVG chart with horizontal axis = radius (mm), vertical = sagitta (mm), arrow markers at every 5th sample showing local slope dz/dr; `AsphericSurfaceSpec` dataclass (radius_mm, conic_k, aspheric_coeffs, clear_aperture_radius_mm); `SagittaArrowChartResult` (sagitta_samples, max_sagitta_mm, conic_only_sagitta_mm, aspheric_contribution_mm, svg_chart, honest_caveat); sphere R=50 r=10 oracle zРЅѕ1.0102 verified < 1e-6; paraboloid k=Рѕњ1 z=r┬▓/(2R) exact; hemisphere z=R at edge; domain-violation guard (radicand РЅЦ 0 + fp-epsilon clamp); LLM tool `optics_compute_sagitta_arrow_chart`; 28 hermetic tests. Honest: standard conic + even-power polynomial asphere ONLY; no Zernike / freeform / XY-polynomial / Q-polynomial / off-axis / tilted surface support; arrow markers show dz/dr (slope), not surface normal; ISO 10110-12:2019. Ref: Welford (1986) ┬Д3.3; ISO 10110-12:2019.

**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Vignetting fraction check** (OPTICS-VIGNETTING-CHECK): computes the fraction of entrance-pupil area occluded by clear-aperture limits at a given field angle; `LensClearApertureSpec` dataclass (surfaces: list of {clear_aperture_radius_mm, axial_position_mm}); `VignettingReport` dataclass (field_angle_deg, vignetting_pct, limiting_surface_idx, effective_pupil_area_pct, honest_caveat); `compute_vignetting(spec, field_angle_deg, marginal_ray_at_stop_mm=10.0)` Рђћ paraxial chief-ray displacement ╬ћ_j = z_j┬иtan(╬И); effective pupil area = exact two-circle intersection area (Weisstein formula) of entrance-pupil disk (radius R) with per-surface CA disk (radius r_j, centred at ╬ћ_j); vignetting_pct = (1 Рѕњ A_eff/A_full)├Ќ100; limiting_surface_idx = argmin of per-surface intersection areas; on-axis (field=0┬░) Рєњ vignetting=0 verified; wide-angle (30┬░) with tight CA Рєњ significant clipping verified; LLM tool `optics_compute_vignetting_check`; 34 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial chief-ray displacement only (no exact ray trace through glass); circular, rotationally-symmetric CAs only; diffraction-induced vignetting NOT modelled; chromatic pupil walk NOT modelled. Ref: Welford (1986) ┬Д3.7; Hecht (2017) ┬Д5.7.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Telecentricity check** (OPTICS-TELECENTRICITY): `compute_telecentricity(lens_system_dict, field_height_mm=10.0, focus_shift_mm=0.5)` Рєњ `TelecentricityReport(chief_ray_angle_object_deg, chief_ray_angle_image_deg, object_telecentric, image_telecentric, both_telecentric, max_magnification_variation_pct, honest_caveat)`; paraxial chief-ray trace via Welford nu-form (`nРђ▓uРђ▓ = nu Рѕњ hc(nРђ▓Рѕњn)`); chief-ray solved by superposition: Ray A (H, 0) + ╬▒┬иRay B (object-dist, 1) at first surface, ╬▒ = Рѕњh_A_stop/h_B_stop forces h=0 at aperture stop; object-space telecentric Рєћ |angle_obj| < 0.5┬░; image-space telecentric Рєћ |angle_img| < 0.5┬░; magnification variation across ┬▒focus_shift_mm computed from u_last of marginal field ray relative to Lagrange-invariant reference magnification; oracle: single-lens (f=100 mm, stop at front focal plane from 5 m object) Рєњ object_telecentric=True, image_telecentric=False; doubly-telecentric relay (two equal lenses, stop at shared focal plane) Рєњ both_telecentric=True; LLM tool `optics_compute_telecentricity`; 25 hermetic tests. Honest: PARAXIAL (first-order) ONLY Рђћ chief ray forced through h=0 at stop surface; aspheric surface terms do not affect first-order angle; stop modelled as thin plane; infinite-conjugate objects approximated by large finite distance; magnification variation uses thin-lens paraxial formula (nu-form). Telecentric threshold: |angle| < 0.5┬░ (conventional machine-vision). Ref: Welford "Aberrations of Optical Systems" (1986) ┬Д3, ┬Д4.4; Smith "Modern Optical Engineering" ┬Д5.4; Hecht "Optics" ┬Д6.6. `kerf-cad-core/optics/telecentricity_check.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Depth-of-field + hyperfocal distance** (OPTICS-FOCAL-DISTANCE-DEPTH): `LensFocusSpec(focal_length_mm, f_number, focus_distance_mm, circle_of_confusion_mm=0.03)` Рєњ `DepthOfFieldReport(hyperfocal_distance_mm, near_limit_mm, far_limit_mm, depth_of_field_mm, behind_focus_fraction, infinity_focus_at_hyperfocal, honest_caveat)`; standard photographic thin-lens DoF formulae (Greenleaf "Photographic Optics" ┬Д3 / Hecht "Optics" ┬Д6.4): H = f┬▓/(N┬иc) + f; D_near = D┬и(HРѕњf)/(H+DРѕњ2f); D_far = D┬и(HРѕњf)/(HРѕњD) [Рѕъ when D РЅЦ H]; oracle 50mm f/2.8 @ 5 m c=0.03 mm Рєњ H РЅѕ 29811.9 mm (РЅѕ29.81 m); near РЅѕ 4286 mm; far РЅѕ 5993 mm; DoF РЅѕ 1707 mm Рђћ all verified to < 0.01%; at focus=H: D_near = H/2 exactly, D_far = Рѕъ verified; D РЅЦ H Рєњ DoF infinite; larger f/# Рєњ wider DoF; LLM tool `optics_compute_depth_of_field`; 25 hermetic tests. Default CoC 0.03 mm = 35mm full-frame standard (Greenleaf ┬Д3 / 1/1400 diagonal). HONEST: geometric thin-lens model only Рђћ does NOT add diffraction-limited Airy-disk blur to geometric CoC; at small apertures (f/# РЅ│ f/16 for visible light) Airy disk 1.22┬и╬╗┬иN approaches 0.03 mm CoC, so geometric DoF is slightly optimistic; for combined blur circle use c_eff = sqrt(c_geom┬▓ + c_airy┬▓). Ref: Hecht (2017) ┬Д6.4; Greenleaf (1950) ┬Д3; Kingslake (1978) ┬Д4.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Working f-number (finite-conjugate)** (OPTICS-FNO-WORKING): `FnoWorkingSpec(nominal_f_number, magnification)` Рєњ `FnoWorkingReport(nominal_f_number, working_f_number, exposure_loss_stops, image_irradiance_factor, honest_caveat)`; thin-lens working f-number formula N_w = N┬и(1+|m|) (Hecht "Optics" ┬Д6.4 / Smith "Modern Optical Engineering" ┬Д4.5); magnification convention m = Рѕњs_i/s_o (negative for real inverted images); oracle f/4 at 1:1 macro (m=Рѕњ1) Рєњ N_w=8.0, loss=2.0 stops exactly; f/2.8 at 1:2 (m=Рѕњ0.5) Рєњ N_w=4.2, lossРЅѕ1.17 stops; image irradiance factor = (N/N_w)┬▓ = 1/(1+|m|)┬▓; exposure_loss_stops = 2┬иlogРѓѓ(1+|m|); m=0 (infinity focus) Рєњ N_w=N, loss=0, factor=1.0 (no penalty); absolute value of m used so positive (virtual-image) magnifications are handled; LLM tool `optics_compute_working_fno`; 28 hermetic tests. HONEST: thin-lens (symmetric-pupil) approximation ONLY Рђћ real asymmetric lenses (retrofocus, telephoto, macro with floating elements) have pupil magnification p = D_exit/D_entrance РЅа 1; exact formula N_w = (1/p)┬иN┬и(1+|m|/p) (Smith MOE ┬Д4.5) can differ by 0.5РђЊ1 stop for extreme retrofocus designs; pupil-position measurement requires an aperture-stop trace not in scope here. Ref: Hecht (2017) ┬Д6.4; Smith (2008) ┬Д4.5; Ray (2002) ┬Д2. `kerf-cad-core/optics/fno_working.py`.

**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Iris (aperture stop) diameter map** (OPTICS-IRIS-DIAMETER-MAP): `IrisMapSpec(lens_system_dict, target_f_number, target_efl_mm=None)` Рєњ `IrisDiameterReport(iris_diameter_mm, effective_f_number, efl_mm, surface_clearance_check, clipped, honest_caveat)`; paraxial formula D = EFL/f# (Welford "Aberrations" ┬Д3.4 / Smith "Modern Optical Engineering" ┬Д6); EFL computed via canonical marginal-ray trace (h=1, u=0) or supplied via `target_efl_mm`; marginal ray h=D/2 at stop (u=0) traced forward through surfaces after the stop and backward through a reversed sub-system for surfaces before the stop; per-surface clearance_ratio = CA_radius / |h| (>1 = clears; <1 = clips); clipping flag when h > 0.95 ├Ќ CA_radius; oracle: EFL=50 mm, f/4 Рєњ D=12.5 mm exactly; f/1.4 fast lens Рєњ DРЅѕ35.7 mm; stop_surface_index configurable; LLM tool `optics_compute_iris_diameter_map`; 25 hermetic tests. HONEST: paraxial (first-order) marginal-ray trace only Рђћ aspheric higher-order sag terms ignored; D=EFL/f# is infinity-conjugate formula only (finite-conjugate requires working f-number N_w=N┬и(1+|m|), Smith MOE ┬Д4.5); clear apertures are caller-supplied; production design requires exact skew-ray analysis (Zemax OpticStudio / CODE V / Welford ┬Д5). Ref: Welford (1986) ┬Д3.4; Smith (2008) ┬Д6; Hecht (2017) ┬Д6.4. `kerf-cad-core/optics/iris_diameter_map.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Airy-disk diffraction-limited PSF** (OPTICS-DIFFRACTION-PSF): `DiffractionPSFSpec(wavelength_nm, aperture_diameter_mm, focal_length_mm)` Рєњ `DiffractionPSFReport(airy_disk_radius_um, rayleigh_resolution_um, fwhm_um, psf_profile, honest_caveat)`; radial intensity I(r) = [2┬иJРѓЂ(x)/x]┬▓ where x = ¤ђ┬иD┬иr/(╬╗┬иf) (Hecht "Optics" 5e ┬Д10.2, eq. 10.22; Born & Wolf "Principles of Optics" 7e ┬Д8.5.2, eq. 8.41); Airy disk radius r_Airy = 1.22┬и╬╗┬иF# (first zero of JРѓЂ, Born & Wolf ┬Д8.5.2); Rayleigh resolution criterion ╬ћr = r_Airy (Hecht ┬Д10.2.7, eq. 10.28); FWHM РЅѕ 1.03┬и╬╗┬иF# (Hecht eq. 10.59); uses scipy.special.j1 when available with pure-Python ascending-series fallback (Abramowitz & Stegun ┬Д9.1.10); oracle ╬╗=550nm, D=10mm, f=50mm (F#=5): r_Airy=3.355 ╬╝m, FWHM=2.833 ╬╝m, I(0)=1.0, I(r_Airy)РЅѕ0 Рђћ all validated to <1e-6; LLM tool `optics_compute_diffraction_psf`; **polychromatic PSF РюЁ** (OPTICS-DIFFRACTION-PSF-POLYCHROMATIC): `compute_polychromatic_psf(numerical_aperture, focal_length_mm, wavelength_samples_nm, spd_weights, radial_grid_um=None)` Рєњ `PolychromaticPSFReport`; algorithm: I_poly(r) = ╬Б_i W(╬╗_i)┬иI(r,╬╗_i) / ╬Б_i W(╬╗_i) where each I(r,╬╗_i) = [2┬иJРѓЂ(x)/x]┬▓ with x = ¤ђ┬иD┬иr/(╬╗_i┬иf) (Hecht ┬Д10.2; Born & Wolf ┬Д8.5.2); broadband PSF is effectively broader than best-╬╗ monochromatic PSF (longer ╬╗ Рєњ wider Airy disk, weighted by W(╬╗)); single-wavelength SPD reproduces monochromatic result exactly; I_poly(0) = 1.0 exactly; standard SPD helpers inlined: `photopic_spd` (CIE V(╬╗), peak 555 nm, Gaussian approx), `d65_spd` (CIE D65, 5-nm tabulation, CIE Pub. 15:2004), `blackbody_spd` (Planck 1901); `PolychromaticPSFReport` includes per-wavelength Airy radii + normalised weights + to_dict(); custom radial_grid_um override; 9 new hermetic polychromatic tests (tests 33РђЊ41): single-╬╗ matches mono; I_poly(0)=1.0; broadband broader than best-╬╗; photopic peak at 555 nm; intensity in [0,1]; to_dict structure; error paths (bad NA, focal, single-wavelength, length mismatch, all-zero weights); custom grid; D65 profile shape + monotone lobe; **45 total hermetic tests**. HONEST: scalar diffraction only; circular aperture; aberration-free; on-axis and paraxial (NA = D/(2f) РЅф 1); accuracy depends on spectral sampling density (РЅЦ 5 samples recommended). Ref: Hecht (2017) ┬Д10.2; Born & Wolf (1999) ┬Д8.5; Goodman (2005) ┬Д4.4; CIE DS 013.3:2018; CIE Pub. 15:2004. `kerf-cad-core/optics/diffraction_psf.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Singlet lens glass volume and weight** (OPTICS-LENS-VOLUME): `SingletLensSpec(radius_R1_mm, radius_R2_mm, center_thickness_mm, clear_aperture_radius_mm, glass_density_g_cm3=2.51)` Рєњ `LensVolumeReport(volume_mm3, weight_g, edge_thickness_mm, sag1_mm, sag2_mm, lens_form, honest_caveat)`; sag h = |R| Рѕњ Рѕџ(|R|┬▓ Рѕњ r┬▓) (Smith "Modern Optical Engineering" ┬Д13.3 eq. 13.6 / Mahajan "Optical Imaging and Aberrations" ┬Д1.2); cap volume V_cap = ¤ђ┬иh┬▓┬и(3|R|Рѕњh)/3 (Smith ┬Д13.3 eq. 13.7); lens volume V = ¤ђ┬иr┬▓┬иt_c ┬▒ V_cap1 ┬▒ V_cap2 with sign from Cartesian-sign surface convention (convex Рєњ subtract, concave Рєњ add); oracle: BK7 plano-convex R1=+100 mm, R2=Рѕъ, ct=5 mm, CA_r=12.5 mm, ¤Ђ=2.51 g/cm┬│ Рєњ sag1=0.7843 mm, V=2261.6 mm┬│, weight=5.677 g (analytically verified); biconvex symmetric V = cylinder Рѕњ 2┬иcap (both surfaces subtract); biconcave V = cylinder + 2┬иcap (both surfaces add; edge > center thickness); meniscus R1=+100/R2=+200 classified correctly; lens_form Рѕѕ {biconvex, biconcave, plano_convex, plano_concave, meniscus, plano_plano}; LLM tool `optics_compute_lens_volume`; 35 hermetic tests. HONEST: SPHERICAL SURFACES ONLY Рђћ aspheric sag h=Rc┬иr┬▓/(1+Рѕџ(1Рѕњ(1+k)c┬▓r┬▓))+╬Б A_i┬иr^(2i) requires numerical integration (out of scope); no anti-reflection coating thickness (AR layers 100РђЊ500 nm, negligible mass); homogeneous density assumed (GRIN / melt-gradient glass differs РЅц0.3%, Schott TIE-31 ┬Д3); clear_aperture_radius РЅа physical blank radius Рђћ blank is always larger, giving higher actual weight. Ref: Smith (2008) ┬Д13.3; Mahajan (2011) ┬Д1.2; Schott TIE-31 (2023). `kerf-cad-core/optics/lens_volume.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Paraxial chief-ray height trace** (OPTICS-CHIEF-RAY-HEIGHT): `trace_chief_ray(lens_system_dict, field_angle_deg, stop_surface_idx)` Рєњ `ChiefRayHeightReport(per_surface_heights, image_height_mm, magnification, stop_surface_idx, chief_ray_at_stop_mm, object_angle_deg, image_angle_deg, honest_caveat)`; paraxial chief-ray (principal ray from off-axis object through stop centre) traced via nu-form superposition (Welford "Aberrations" ┬Д3 / Mahajan "Optical Imaging" ┬Д2): two auxiliary rays (Ray A: object height H, slope 0; Ray B: height obj_dist, slope 1) solve h_stop=0 Рєњ u_obj=Рѕњh_A_stop/h_B_stop; oracle: f=50mm plano-convex thin lens, ╬И=5┬░ Рєњ image_height=f┬иtan(5┬░)=4.374mm (verified to <1e-3mm); chief-ray height at stop = 0 exactly; image-space telecentric condition (stop at front focal plane Рєњ u_img=0) verified; per-surface {surface_idx, ray_height_mm, ray_angle_deg}; LLM tool `optics_trace_chief_ray`; 30 hermetic tests. HONEST: PARAXIAL ONLY Рђћ first-order heights differ from exact at large field/fast optics; APERTURE STOP POSITION MUST BE SUPPLIED (no auto-detect); rotationally symmetric systems only; image height = f┬иtan(╬И) (no distortion correction). Ref: Welford (1986) ┬Д3, ┬Д3.7; Mahajan (2011) ┬Д2; Smith (2008) ┬Д5. `kerf-cad-core/optics/chief_ray_height.py`.

**Optics / acoustics** РюЁ Рђћ **Schmidt corrector plate aspheric profile** (OPTICS-SCHMIDT-CORRECTOR-PLATE): `SchmidtSpec(primary_radius_R_mm, aperture_diameter_D_mm, glass_index_n=1.5168, neutral_zone_factor_kappa=1.5)` Рєњ `SchmidtReport(aspheric_profile, max_sag_mm, neutral_zone_radius_mm, schwarzschild_constant_k, honest_caveat)`; classical Schmidt (1932) corrector sag z(r) = r┬▓┬и(r┬▓Рѕњ2┬и¤Ђ_n┬▓)/[8┬и(nРѕњ1)┬иR┬│] where ¤Ђ_n = (D/2)/Рѕџ╬║ is the neutral zone radius (Born & Wolf ┬Д6.3); kappa=1.5 places neutral zone at rРЅѕ0.8165┬иD/2 (classic Schmidt optimum that minimises peak-to-valley sag); max_sag = |z(¤Ђ_n)| = ¤Ђ_nРЂ┤/[8┬и(nРѕњ1)┬иR┬│]; neutral-zone slope check (dz/dr=0 at r=¤Ђ_n); Schwarzschild constant k=Рѕњ1 (paraboloid equivalent); oracle: 200mm f/2 BK7 corrector Рєњ neutral zone 81.65mm, max_sagРЅѕ0.168mm; sag scales as (nРѕњ1)РЂ╗┬╣ verified; LLM tool `optics_design_schmidt_corrector`; 28 hermetic tests. HONEST: classical Schmidt (1932) ONLY Рђћ modern SchmidtРђЊCassegrain and SchmidtРђЊNewtonian designs add a secondary mirror, field-flattener, and refined aspherics for a flat corrected field; these are NOT modelled; monochromatic (chromatic residual is second-order, Wilkins 1950, not computed); on-axis only (off-axis coma requires corrector at exact centre-of-curvature position); field curvature R_PetzvalРЅѕРѕњR/2 not corrected; thin-plate approximation. Ref: Schmidt (1932) Zentralzeitung f├╝r Optik und Mechanik 52, 25-26; Born & Wolf (1999) ┬Д6.3; Rutten & van Venrooij "Telescope Optics" (1988) ┬Д6.3. `kerf-cad-core/optics/schmidt_corrector.py`.

**Implicit geometry** РюЁ Рђћ F-rep CSG (union/intersect/subtract/blend/shell) + domain warps (twist/taper/wave) in `kerf_cad_core.frep.csg`.

**Materials + LCA** РюЁ Рђћ Ashby database to ~200 materials (14 families) with Pareto-frontier multi-objective selection; full ISO 14040/44 LCA (4 phases, 6 impact categories, Monte-Carlo uncertainty). **Embodied-carbon DB (ICE v3 lookups)** РюЁ Рђћ `kerf_lca.database` module with 30-material `MATERIAL_DATABASE` (steel, aluminium, copper, composites, concrete, timber, plastics, elastomers, glass, ceramics); `lca_lookup_material` + `lca_compute_embodied_carbon` LLM tools; EN 15978 Module D EoL credits. Data: ICE v3.0, Hammond & Jones, University of Bath, 2019 Рђћ NOT Ecoinvent (license-restricted).
**Materials + LCA** РюЁ Рђћ Ashby database to ~200 materials (14 families) with Pareto-frontier multi-objective selection; full ISO 14040/44 LCA (4 phases, 6 impact categories, Monte-Carlo uncertainty); EoL circularity (EN 15978 Module D + Ellen MacArthur MCI) РюЁ.

**Compare matrices** РюЁ Рђћ feature-matrix YAML for 14 reference CADs: Fusion 360, SolidWorks, Onshape, FreeCAD, Rhino, KiCad, CATIA, Creo, NX, Inventor, AutoCAD, Altium, Revit, Blender Рђћ 741 grounded rows total.

**Security hardening** РюЁ Рђћ `/run-topo` auth gate; NFP `grid_step` clamped; PVT `n_mc` clamped; Yosys module-name injection blocked; shared `_guard_*` helpers extracted across 68 files (Рѕњ2009/+129 lines net).

**SUBD-LIMIT-WALK-CROSS-CURVE** РюЁ Рђћ walk a parametric path on the Catmull-Clark subdivision-surface limit and intersect with a planar cut to produce a cross-section curve: `walk_subd_limit_cross_plane(cage_mesh, plane_point, plane_normal, num_walk_samples=400)` returns `CrossCurveResult(points, face_indices_crossed, num_intersections, honest_caveat)`; samples a uniform (u,v) grid on each cage face using the Stam (1998) closed-form limit-position evaluator (`stam_limit_position` Рђћ bi-cubic B-spline for regular valence-4 patches, eigenstructure for extraordinary vertices); sign changes in signed plane distance are detected between adjacent grid samples (u-adjacent + v-adjacent separately); each crossing refined by 5 bisection iterations (positional error РЅѕ cell_size/32 РЅѕ face_size/32); honest caveats: discrete sample walk (coarse grid can miss sub-cell features), 5-iter bisection (not sub-pixel), boundary edge duplicates possible, extraordinary vertices use Stam eigenstructure approximation; LLM tool `subd_walk_limit_cross_plane`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; 20 oracle-asserted tests (cube XY/XZ/diagonal cuts, parallel planes Рєњ empty, flat patch, grid cage, extraordinary vertex cage, degenerate cage, non-unit normal, sample-count monotonicity) Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/limit_walk_cross_curve.py`. Refs: Stam (1998) SIGGRAPH ┬Д3РђЊ4; Schaefer-Warren (2004).

**SUBD-LIMIT-WALK-ALONG-EDGES** РюЁ Рђћ sample the Catmull-Clark limit-surface curve corresponding to a chain of cage edges: `walk_along_cage_edges(cage, vertex_sequence, samples_per_edge=8)` returns `SubDEdgeWalk(points, arc_length)`; boundary edges Рєњ limit = cage (crease rule); creased interior edges Рєњ limit on sharp crease curve; smooth interior edges Рєњ smooth arc through CC limit positions; intermediate points via index-tracked CC subdivision (k = ceil(log2(spe)) levels, max 6) + per-vertex limit stencil; honest ValueError for non-adjacent vertices or out-of-range indices; LLM tool `subd_walk_edge_chain`; 14 oracle-asserted tests Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_edge_walk.py`.

**SUBD-CAGE-RING-FROM-EDGE** РюЁ Рђћ edge ring traversal on Catmull-Clark quad cages: `compute_edge_ring(cage, start_edge)` returns `EdgeRingResult(edge_indices, is_closed, is_degenerate, transition_face_indices)`; follows opposite edges across each quad face (Maya/Blender Bridge pattern); closed on cube (4-ring) and torus (ring length = opposite-axis count); open at mesh boundary; honest degenerate flag at non-quad faces; start_edge accepts `(v0, v1)` pair or integer edge index; LLM tool `subd_compute_edge_ring`; 25 oracle-asserted tests Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_edge_ring.py`.

**SUBD-CAGE-EDGE-LOOP-SELECT** РюЁ Рђћ directional edge-loop walk on a quad cage mesh: `select_edge_loop(cage_mesh, start_edge_idx, max_steps=1000)` returns `EdgeLoopResult(edge_indices, vertex_indices, closed, terminated_at_irregular, irregular_vertex_valences, honest_caveat)`; walks the opposite-edge chain (Bommes-L├Еvy-Pietroni 2013 ┬Д3.2 'skip-2' rule): at each step crosses the current quad face to its opposite edge; terminates at irregular vertex (valenceРЅа4), boundary edge, non-quad face, or loop closure; oracles: 4├Ќ4 torus (all valence-4) Рєњ closed loops length 4; 6├Ќ8 torus Рєњ lengths {6, 8}; cube (all valence-3) Рєњ terminates at first irregular vertex, valence=3 reported; cylinder axial-interior edge Рєњ closed ring length nu; mixed tri/quad Рєњ terminates; ValueError on out-of-range start_edge_idx; honest caveats: quads only, no tris; assumes manifold mesh; boundary vertices treated as irregular; traversal direction fixed by first adjacent face winding; LLM tool `subd_select_edge_loop`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; 25 oracle-asserted tests Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/edge_loop_select.py`. Refs: Bommes-L├Еvy-Pietroni (2013) CG&F ┬Д3.2; L├Еvy-Liu (2010) SIGGRAPH ┬Д4.

**SUBD-CAGE-FACE-LOOP** РюЁ Рђћ walk a face loop on a quad cage mesh by hopping through opposite-edge adjacent quads: `select_face_loop(cage_mesh, start_face_idx, walk_direction=0, max_steps=1000)` returns `FaceLoopResult(face_indices, closed, terminated_at_irregular, irregular_face_indices, honest_caveat)`; dual of the edge-loop walk Рђћ tracks faces rather than edges, useful for ring-cut planning and subdivision sweep selection; `walk_direction` 0/1 selects which opposite-edge pair to traverse: dir=0 crosses (v0,v1)Рєћ(v2,v3) edges, dir=1 crosses (v1,v2)Рєћ(v3,v0) edges; on a regular torus the two directions produce orthogonal face rings; terminates at non-quad face, boundary edge, or loop closure; oracles: 4├Ќ4 torus dir=0 Рєњ closed ring length 4; 4├Ќ6 torus dir=0Рєњlength 4, dir=1Рєњlength 6; cylinder (nu=12) dir=1 Рєњ circumferential closed ring length 12; cube Рєњ closed 4-ring; mixed tri/quad Рєњ terminated; single-quad cage Рєњ terminated; non-quad start face Рєњ immediate termination; ValueError on out-of-range start_face_idx or walk_direction not in {0,1}; honest caveats: quads only Рђћ non-quad face terminates immediately; boundary edges terminate walk; walk_direction relative to start face winding; one-directional (no back-propagation); manifold mesh assumed; LLM tool `subd_select_face_loop`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; 20 oracle-asserted tests Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/face_loop_select.py`. Refs: Bommes-L├Еvy-Pietroni (2013) CG&F ┬Д3.2; Hoppe (1996) Progressive Meshes ┬Д3.2.

**SUBD-CAGE-SUBDIVIDE-EDGE** РюЁ Рђћ localized single-edge refinement on a SubD control cage (not a full Catmull-Clark pass): `subdivide_edge(cage, edge_index, position_t=0.5, split_strategy='quad') -> SubdivideEdgeResult`; inserts midpoint vertex v_m = lerp(v_a, v_b, t) on the target edge; each of the 1РђЊ2 adjacent faces split into face_a [p0, v_m, p_{n-1}] (triangle) + face_b [v_m, p1, ..., p_{n-1}] (quad for n=4); cube oracle: V=8Рєњ9, F=6Рєњ8, E=12Рєњ15, Euler 9Рѕњ15+8=2 РюЊ; boundary-edge split: 1 adjacent face only; invalid edge_index Рєњ ValueError; position_t clamp [1e-9, 1Рѕњ1e-9]; honest flag `has_non_quad_input` for non-quad input faces; sharpness/bevel-weight not preserved across edge-index remapping; LLM tool `subd_subdivide_edge`; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 24 oracle-asserted tests Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_subdivide_edge.py`. Ref: Catmull & Clark 1978; Stam 1998 ┬Д4 local refinement; Maya polySplit API.

**SUBD-CAGE-EDGE-COLLAPSE** РюЁ Рђћ collapse a SubD cage edge (merge two endpoints into one vertex) while maintaining mesh validity; used for mesh decimation and cage simplification: `collapse_edge(cage: SubdCage, v_keep, v_remove, midpoint=True) -> EdgeCollapseResult`; `EdgeCollapseResult(new_cage: SubdCage, num_vertices_removed, num_faces_removed, collapsed_position_xyz_mm, degenerate_faces_removed, became_invalid, honest_caveat)`; midpoint=True (default): v_new = (V[v_keep] + V[v_remove]) / 2; midpoint=False: v_new = V[v_keep]; all face refs to v_remove rewritten to v_keep; degenerate faces (containing both endpoints Рєњ repeated vertex) removed; vertex list compacted; adjacency check Рђћ if v_keep and v_remove do not share a face (not a valid edge), became_invalid=True and input cage returned unchanged; cube oracle: collapse top-front edge (v_keep=4, v_remove=5) Рєњ 7 verts, 2 degenerate faces removed РюЊ; pyramid base edge: 5Рєњ4 verts, РЅЦ1 degenerate face РюЊ; non-adjacent pair Рєњ became_invalid=True, cage unchanged РюЊ; midpoint position oracle РюЊ; endpoint position (midpoint=False) oracle РюЊ; all face indices valid post-collapse РюЊ; v_keep/v_remove out-of-range Рєњ ValueError РюЊ; honest caveats: TOPOLOGY ONLY Рђћ no QEM cost function (Garland-Heckbert 1997); caller chooses which edge to collapse; midpoint placement can deviate from CC limit surface; crease annotations not preserved; all indices invalidated; non-manifold edges handled conservatively; LLM tool `subd_collapse_edge`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in `plugin.py _TOOL_MODULES`; 14 oracle-asserted tests Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/edge_collapse.py`. Refs: Hoppe (1993) Mesh Optimization; Hoppe (1996) Progressive Meshes ┬Д3.2; Garland-Heckbert (1997) QEM ┬Д3; Bommes-L├Еvy-Pietroni (2013) CG&F ┬Д4.

**SUBD-CAGE-EDGE-FLIP** РюЁ Рђћ topological edge flip for two adjacent triangles sharing an edge: `flip_edge(cage_mesh, edge_idx) -> EdgeFlipResult`; finds the two triangles T1=(v_a, v_b, v_c) and T2=(v_a, v_b, v_d) sharing edge (v_a, v_b); replaces them with T1'=(v_a, v_c, v_d) and T2'=(v_b, v_d, v_c) connecting the opposite vertices; winding order of T1 is preserved in both output triangles; vertex list unchanged (no vertices added or removed); face count unchanged (2 in Рєњ 2 out); canonical oracle: triangles ABC+BCD (share BC) Рєњ flip gives {A,B,D}+{A,C,D} (share AD); new shared edge is AD, old shared edge BC no longer present РюЊ; double flip restores original topology (flip is its own inverse) РюЊ; only non-incident faces unchanged РюЊ; out-of-range edge_idx Рєњ ValueError; boundary edge (1 incident face) Рєњ ValueError; non-manifold edge (> 2 incident faces) Рєњ ValueError; quad or n-gon face Рєњ ValueError; honest caveats: TOPOLOGICAL FLIP ONLY Рђћ no Delaunay in-circle test; callers must test in-circle criterion themselves if Delaunay quality is required; triangles only (quad faces raise ValueError); no crease/UV/colour attribute preservation on flipped edge; vertex positions unchanged; LLM tool `subd_flip_edge`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; 14 oracle-asserted tests Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/edge_flip.py`. Refs: Bommes-L├Еvy-Pietroni (2013) CG&F ┬Д3; Edelsbrunner (2001) Geometry and Topology for Mesh Generation ┬Д2; de Berg et al. (2008) Computational Geometry ┬Д9.3.

**SUBD-CAGE-AREA** РюЁ Рђћ compute total surface area of a subdivision control cage (control polygon) and estimate the asymptotic Catmull-Clark limit-surface area: `compute_cage_area(cage) -> CageAreaReport`; `SubdCage(vertices_xyz_mm, faces)` accepts tris, quads, and n-gons; triangle area = 0.5┬и|cross(v1-v0, v2-v0)|; quad area = 0.5┬и|cross(d1, d2)| (diagonal cross-product, exact for planar quads); n-gon area = centroid fan triangulation (exact for planar n-gons); limit-surface estimate = cage_area ├Ќ 0.94 (empirical Catmull-Clark shrinkage ratio); `CageAreaReport` fields: `total_cage_area_mm2`, `estimated_limit_surface_area_mm2`, `per_face_areas`, `min_face_area_mm2`, `max_face_area_mm2`, `degenerate_face_indices`, `num_quads`, `num_tris`, `num_ngons`, `honest_caveat`; unit cube oracle: 6 mm┬▓ cage, 5.64 mm┬▓ estimate РюЊ; degenerate triangle (collinear) flagged РюЊ; pyramid (1 quad + 4 tris) area oracle РюЊ; pentagon n-gon area = exact formula within 1e-9 РюЊ; hexagon n-gon РюЊ; area scales by k┬▓ on vertex rescaling РюЊ; limit estimate = cage ├Ќ 0.94 exactly РюЊ; LLM tool `subd_compute_cage_area`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; 23 oracle-asserted tests Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/cage_area.py`. HONEST: LIMIT-SURFACE AREA IS AN EMPIRICAL ESTIMATE ONLY Рђћ exact value requires Stam (1998) eigenanalysis at each extraordinary vertex or GL integration over Stam B-spline patches; empirical 0.92РђЊ0.95 range applies to typical organic closed all-quad cages; error vs exact limit area can exceed 5% for cages with many extraordinary vertices or high non-planarity; non-planar quad/n-gon face areas are first-order approximations only. Refs: Catmull-Clark (1978) CAD 10(6); Stam (1998) SIGGRAPH ┬Д2; Warren-Weimer (2001) ┬Д5; Zorin-Schr├Хder (2000) SIGGRAPH Course ┬Д3.

**SUBD-CAGE-VERTEX-MERGE** РюЁ Рђћ merge a list of N cage vertices (by index) into their centroid, updating all adjacent face indices and removing degenerate faces: `merge_vertices(cage_mesh, vertex_indices) -> VertexMergeResult`; computes v_c = mean of all named vertex positions; replaces every face reference to any named vertex with v_c; faces containing РЅЦ 2 named vertices become degenerate (repeated vertex) and are removed; vertex list compacted (net -(|S|-1) vertices); special cases: empty or single-vertex list Рєњ no-op; duplicate indices Рєњ deduplicated; non-adjacent vertices (no shared edge) Рєњ no faces removed, vertex count drops by |S|-1; cube oracle: merge all 4 corners of isolated quad Рєњ 3 verts removed, 1 face removed, 0 faces survive; 2-vertex merge on plane Рєњ equivalent to edge_collapse (same vertex count, same faces removed, centroid=midpoint); 3-vertex centroid oracle РюЊ; all face indices valid post-merge РюЊ; out-of-range index Рєњ ValueError; honest caveats: centroid placement only Рђћ NO quadric error metric (Garland-Heckbert 1997 ┬Д3); CC limit surface shape changes; crease annotations on incident edges not preserved; vertex/face indices invalidated after merge; LLM tool `subd_merge_vertices`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; 20 oracle-asserted tests Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/vertex_merge.py`. Refs: Hoppe (1996) Progressive Meshes ┬Д3.2; Garland-Heckbert (1997) QEM ┬Д3.

**SUBD-LIMIT-CRITICAL-POINTS** РюЁ Рђћ discrete Morse critical points (РѕЄf = 0) on Catmull-Clark SubD limit surfaces: `find_critical_points(cage, scalar_field, sample_density=4) -> CriticalPointsReport`; classifies interior vertices using lower/upper link under Simulation-of-Simplicity total order (Edelsbrunner-M├╝cke 1990) Рђћ minima (LkРЂ╗ empty), maxima (LkРЂ║ empty), saddles (#components(LkРЂ╗) + #components(LkРЂ║) > 2); Morse-Euler verification #max Рѕњ #sad + #min = ¤Є(VРѕњE+F); scalar fields: height_z/height_x/height_y/radius; oracle depth bar: sphere from cube cage Рєњ 1 max + 1 min + 0 sad (¤Є=2, Euler passes); torus (axis along Y, Morse generic) Рєњ 1 max + 1 min + 2 sad (¤Є=0); flat/tilted-plane open mesh Рєњ 0 critical points; honest caveat: Bott-Samelson degenerate fields (axis-symmetric height on upright torus) not handled Рђћ euler_check flags violations; LLM tool `subd_find_critical_points`; 16 oracle-asserted tests Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_critical_points.py` (Edelsbrunner-Harer 2010 ┬Д1).

**BREP-SHELL-WALL-CHECK** РюЁ Рђћ post-shell wall-thickness verification against manufacturing process requirements: `check_shell_walls(body, process, material) -> ShellWallReport`; injection moulding spec from Menges 2001 ┬Д3.3 Table 3.3 (t_min/t_max per material, flow-length correction +0.5 mm/100 mm); sheet metal from Boothroyd-Dewhurst ┬Д5 (constant-wall + ┬Д5.4 bend-radius multiplier); FDM/SLA/SLS/DLP/MJF nozzle-diameter minimum wall; per-face `FaceWallResult` with violation text; `violations_thin`/`violations_thick` lists; honest caveat: static rule-based only, no CFD or mould-fill simulation; LLM tool `brep_check_shell_walls`; 20 oracle-asserted tests (2mm ABS Рєњ pass; 0.5mm ABS Рєњ thin; 0.5mm FDM Рєњ pass; 0.2mm FDM Рєњ thin; 6mm ABS Рєњ thick; Menges Table 3.3 oracle for PP/PC/LCP/PVC/POM/PEEK; flow-length correction; sheet-metal Al; SLA; nozzle override) Рђћ `kerf-cad-core/geom/shell_wall_check.py`.

### Core platform

- **Auth + projects + files + chat (CRUD)** РюЁ Рђћ Postgres, JWT, Google OAuth.
- **Plugin monorepo (`packages/kerf-*`)** РюЁ Рђћ `kerf-core` app factory + entry-point loader; ~25 plugin packages; 864+ tests.
- **Single-binary build + brew/curl install** РюЁ Рђћ embedded Vite SPA (~32 MB).
- **Auth-optional local mode** РюЁ Рђћ `POST /auth/bootstrap-local` singleton user.
- **Cloud: workshop sharing, billing, LLM pricing, free/paid buckets + wallet** РюЁ Рђћ USD-display, credits at cost, BYO-key plumbing.
- **Cloud: git (commits/branches/merge/GitHub sync) + git Storer** РюЁ.
- **Large-file git handling** РюЁ Рђћ pointer kind, Phase 1.
- **Diff-based + compressed revisions** РюЁ Рђћ 82├Ќ shrink.
- **Workspaces (orgs), activity timeline, avatars/CDN, collapsible chat** РюЁ.
- **E2E Playwright + per-plugin pytest suites** РюЁ.
- **Billing-ledger schema on fresh databases** РюЁ.

### Scripting / SDK

- **`.script.py` via `kerf-sdk`** РюЁ Рђћ `/v1/rpc` JSON-RPC over the LLM tool registry; API tokens; PyPI publish.
- **SDKs: Python ┬и TypeScript ┬и Rust ┬и Go ┬и Lua** РюЁ Рђћ same `/v1/rpc` wire format.

### Parametric core

- **Equations / global parameters** РюЁ Рђћ `.equations`, mathjs.
- **Configurations / variants** РюЁ Рђћ per-file param overrides, BOM rollup.
- **Materials database** РюЁ Рђћ `.material` kind, 200 seeded materials.
- **Two coexisting kernels** РюЁ Рђћ `.jscad` (mesh) + `.feature` (OCCT BRep), shared `.sketch`/`.assembly`/`.drawing`.
- **Pure-Python B-rep + NURBS kernel** РюЁ Рђћ validated `Body` topology, tolerant booleans, G1/G2 fillets, closest-point, hardened SSI, parametric history DAG with persistent face naming. 620 hermetic analytic-oracle-asserted tests.

### Geometry kernel Рђћ depth

The pure-Python kernel (`packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/geom/`) now matches Rhino/Blender-class construction depth with an analytic foundation:

| Module | Description | Status |
|---|---|---|
| **`brep.py`** | B-rep topology: radial-edge `BodyРєњSolidРєњShellРєњFaceРєњLoopРєњCoedgeРєњEdgeРєњVertex`, nine Euler operators, EulerРђЊPoincar├Е invariant enforced | РюЁ shipped |
| **`geom/topology_euler_check.py`** | **BREP-TOPOLOGY-EULER-CHECK**: full generalised Euler-Poincar├Е verifier V-E+F = 2(S-G)+H (Mantyla 1988 ┬Д6; Hoffmann 1989 ┬Д5); `verify_euler_topology(Body)` + `verify_euler_topology_from_dict(faces, ...)` + `EulerCheckReport` dataclass; union-find shell count; oracle helpers for cube/torus/disjoint cubes; LLM tool `brep_verify_euler_topology`; 16 hermetic tests (cube ¤Є=2, torus ¤Є=0, disjoint cubes S=2/¤Є=4, inner loops, violation flags). Pure-Python. CAVEATS: genus/inner-loops require caller hints in dict mode; vertex dedup after sew/heal may cause spurious failure (degenerate_vertices_hint flag). | РюЁ shipped |
| **`brep_build.py`** | Analytic verbs (box/cylinder/sphere/Coons patch) Рєњ `validate_body`-clean `Body` | РюЁ shipped |
| **`geom/brep_connect_inspector.py`** | **BREP-CONNECT-INSPECTOR**: radial-edge connectivity classification (Weiler 1985 ┬Д3 + Mantyla 1988 ┬Д6); counts dangling / boundary / manifold / non-manifold edges; isolated vertices; degenerate (zero-length) edges; union-find shell connectivity components; EulerРђЊPoincar├Е V-E+F residual; `inspect_connectivity` + `is_manifold_closed`; LLM tools `brep_inspect_connectivity` + `brep_is_manifold`; 11 hermetic oracle tests (closed cube Рєњ manifold=12/boundary=0/components=1; open box Рєњ boundary=4/manifold=8; T-shape Рєњ nonmanifoldРЅЦ1; two disconnected cubes Рєњ components=2). Pure-Python, no OCCT. | РюЁ shipped |
| **`geom/brep_connect_inspector.py`** | **BREP-CONNECT-INSPECTOR**: radial-edge connectivity classification (Weiler 1985 ┬Д3 + Mantyla 1988 ┬Д6); manifold/boundary/nonmanifold/dangling counts; isolated vertices; degenerate edges; union-find shell components; EulerРђЊPoincar├Е V-E+F; `inspect_connectivity` + `is_manifold_closed`; LLM tools `brep_inspect_connectivity` + `brep_is_manifold` | РюЁ shipped |
| **`geom/vertex_degree_check.py`** | **BREP-VERTEX-DEGREE-CHECK**: count incident edges per vertex; flag boundary (degree < expected_degree) and non-manifold (degree > expected_degree + 2); `VertexDegreeReport` dataclass with `num_vertices`, `degree_histogram` (dict[int,int]), `num_boundary_vertices`, `num_non_manifold_vertices`, `max_degree`, `irregular_vertex_indices`, `honest_caveat`; `check_vertex_degrees(brep_or_mesh, expected_degree=4)`; oracle helpers for cube + tetrahedron; LLM tool `brep_check_vertex_degrees`; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 20 hermetic tests. Pure-Python. CAVEATS: edge-based degree only Рђћ does NOT analyse face-fan angular order or non-manifold edges at high-degree vertices. Refs: Mantyla 1988 ┬Д3.4; Hoffmann 1989 ┬Д4. | РюЁ shipped |
| **`geom/brep_edge_metrics.py`** | **BREP-SUM-EDGE-LENGTHS**: total edge length + kind/curve-type breakdowns for cutting-cost estimation; `total_edge_length` / `edge_length_by_kind` / `edges_by_curve_type` / `compute_edge_metrics`; linearРєњEuclidean, circularРєњradius├Ќangle, freeformРєњadaptive 5-pt Gauss-Legendre (Stoer-Bulirsch ┬Д3 + Piegl-Tiller ┬Д5.4); oracles: 100├Ќ50 rect=300, unit cube=12, sphere 12 great-circle r=50=3769.91; LLM tools `brep_total_edge_length` + `brep_edge_length_by_kind`; 20 hermetic tests | РюЁ shipped |
| **`boolean.py`** | Tolerant pure-Python solid booleans (regularised cut/fuse/common) over the primitive matrix, 2-manifold result | РюЁ shipped |
| **`fillet_solid.py` / `chamfer.py`** | G1/G2 surface blend + edge fillet + variable chamfer | РюЁ shipped |
| **`geom/auto_chamfer.py`** | Auto-chamfer recommendation (ISO 13715): dihedral-angle classification Рєњ safety / manufacturing / cosmetic / no-chamfer; `brep_recommend_chamfers` + `brep_apply_chamfer_recommendations` LLM tools | РюЁ shipped |
| **`geom/auto_fillet.py`** | Auto-fillet recommendation engine (Peterson 1974 + Boothroyd-Dewhurst 2002) Рђћ classifies interior/exterior corners, sizes radii per design intent, estimates Kt reduction; LLM tools `brep_recommend_fillets` + `brep_apply_fillet_recommendations` | РюЁ shipped |
| **`geom/fillet_recommend_radius.py`** | BREP-FILLET-RECOMMEND-RADIUS Рђћ per-edge radius recommendation combining 4 criteria: (1) face-size cap rРЅцface_min/4 (Boothroyd-Dewhurst ┬Д4), (2) Peterson 1974 ┬Д2.3 notch Kt formula r=0.1├Ќnotch_depth (tension+bending, analytic only, NOT FEA), (3) material stress-relief floor rРЅЦfactor├Ќwall_thickness (steel 0.05, cast_iron 0.08, etc.), (4) tool constraint rРЅЦtool_radius_mm + sharp-edge preservation; `RadiusRecommendation` dataclass with criteria_radii transparency dict; LLM tool `brep_recommend_fillet_radius`; 21 hermetic oracle tests | РюЁ shipped |
| **`fillet_recommend_radius.py`** | Per-edge fillet radius recommendation (Peterson 1974 ┬Д2.3; Boothroyd-Dewhurst 2002 ┬Д4) Рђћ LLM tool `brep_recommend_fillet_radius` | РюЁ shipped |
| **`chamfer_recommend_size.py`** | Per-edge chamfer size recommendation (Drozda-Wick ┬Д3-7; DIN 74:1974 Form A/B; ISO 13715:2017 ┬Д5) Рђћ deburring 0.5mm├Ќ45┬░; countersink; cosmetic; manufacturing Рђћ LLM tool `brep_recommend_chamfer_size`; **asymmetric chamfers (e.g. 30┬░├Ќ60┬░, 1├Ќ2 leg ratio) РюЁ** via `recommend_asymmetric_chamfer(edge, application, ratio_a_to_b)` + `ratio=` param on `recommend_chamfer_size()`; `AsymmetricChamferRecommendation` dataclass with `leg_a_mm`, `leg_b_mm`, `angle_a_deg`, `angle_b_deg`, `is_symmetric`; angles derived from `atan2(leg_b, leg_a)`; symmetric 45┬░ path unchanged (ratio=1.0 default, backward compatible) | РюЁ shipped |
| **`offset.py`** | Exact-distance surface/curve/loop offsets with self-intersection trim | РюЁ shipped |
| **`surface_offset.py`** | NURBS surface offset (Tiller-Hanson 1984 + Hoschek 1988): CP face-normal displacement, iterative isotropic-error refinement, M├Хller 1997 self-intersection detection, local-loop trim; `nurbs_surface_offset` LLM tool; 4 analytical oracle tests (plane/cylinder/sphere/C-shape) | РюЁ shipped |
| **`curve_offset_2d.py`** | NURBS 2D curve offset + self-intersection trim (Tiller-Hanson 1984) Рђћ foundation for flat patterns, CAM toolpath offset, hatch fill; **NURBS-CURVE-OFFSET-2D** adds `Offset2DResult` (max/mean actual offset, self-intersection count, honest caveat) + `offset_nurbs_curve_2d(curve, offset_distance_mm, side)` wrapper + LLM tool `nurbs_offset_curve_2d`; HONEST: linear CP-offset approx (Piegl-Tiller ┬Д10.7), NOT exact NURBS offset; max_actual_offset_mm may differ from target for high-curvature regions; 26 hermetic tests | РюЁ shipped |
| **`coons.py`** | Boundary-interpolation Coons patches, exact to 1e-12 | РюЁ shipped |
| **`network_surface.py`** | N-sided patch: N=3 Hosaka-Kimura triangular Coons, N=4 Gregory twist-corrected Coons, NРЅЦ5 Wachspress polygon blend; `fairness_metric` bending energy; LLM tool `nurbs_n_sided_patch` | РюЁ shipped |
| **`inversion.py`** | Closest-point / point-inversion (Piegl 6.1, analytic partials on rational surfaces) | РюЁ shipped |
| **`curve_projection.py`** | PointРєњcurve / pointРєњsurface projection (Newton-Raphson + arc-length fallback, Hu-Wallner 2006); `ProjectionResult` dataclass; `distance_curve_to_curve`; LLM tool `nurbs_project_point` | РюЁ shipped |
| **`intersection.py`** | Hardened SSI: loop-detection, tangential-branch detection, small-loop guard, analytic specialisations; **NURBS-CURVE-SELF-INTERSECT enhanced** Рђћ `curve_self_intersect_robust`: Piegl-Tiller ┬Д5.5 AABB-tree recursive subdivision + Sederberg 1985 bisection stop criterion + NewtonРђЊRaphson on \|C(t1)РѕњC(t2)\|┬▓; figure-8 B├Еzier oracle verified РЅц1e-9; 33 new tests green; honest-flag: multiplicity-3 intersections not detected | РюЁ shipped |
| **`intersection_degen.py` Рђћ Degenerate SSI (Legendre canonical forms)** | `detect_degenerate_ssi` + `compute_degenerate_ssi_curve` + `ssi_extended`; handles coaxial cylinders, coplanar planes, sphere-tangent-plane, Legendre/Weierstrass conic section for tangent quadric pairs; LLM tool `nurbs_ssi_with_degenerate_check` registered; 27 hermetic tests with analytical oracles | РюЁ shipped |
| **`intersection.py`** | Hardened SSI: loop-detection, tangential-branch detection, small-loop guard, analytic specialisations | РюЁ shipped |
| **`edge_curve_from_face_pair.py`** | B-rep edge-curve extraction: SSI Рєњ longest branch Рєњ degree-3 NURBS fit + UV traces on both faces (Sederberg-Parry 1986 / Patrikalakis-Maekawa ┬Д7); LLM tool `brep_extract_edge_curve_from_faces` | РюЁ shipped |
| **`geom/edge_convexity.py`** | **BREP-EDGE-CONVEXITY**: classify B-rep edge as convex / concave / tangent / smooth / sharp-convex / sharp-concave from sampled face normals (no B-rep topology access required). `EdgeSample(point_xyz_mm, face_a_normal, face_b_normal, edge_tangent)` / `SampledEdgeConvexityReport(classification, mean_dihedral_deg, max_dihedral_deg, min_dihedral_deg, num_samples, honest_caveat)` / `classify_edge_convexity(samples, tangent_tol_deg=2.0, sharp_threshold_deg=135.0)`. Sign convention: cross(n_a, n_b) ┬и edge_tangent > 0 Рєњ convex; < 0 Рєњ concave; РЅѕ 0 Рєњ smooth/tangent. Dihedral = arccos(n_a ┬и n_b) Рѕѕ [0┬░, 180┬░]. "sharp-convex" / "sharp-concave" when dihedral > sharp_threshold_deg. Also ships B-rep-topology API: `EdgeClass` / `EdgeConvexityReport` / `classify_edges` / `classify_body_edges`. LLM tools `brep_classify_edges` (topology) + `geom_classify_edge_convexity` (sampled-normals) registered. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 16 hermetic tests. **Honest caveats**: sampled API requires pre-evaluated outward normals from the caller Рђћ does NOT parse B-rep topology directly; inverted normals flip the convex/concave label; tangent_tol_deg threshold is caller-tunable. Refs: Mantyla 1988 ┬Д5; Hoffmann 1989 ┬Д5.3. | РюЁ shipped |
| **`geom/edge_curve_extend.py`** | **BREP-EDGE-CURVE-EXTEND**: extend a B-rep edge's underlying NurbsCurve beyond its parametric domain by ╬ћL mm, preserving G1 or G2 continuity at the join. G1: cubic B├Еzier tangent-extrapolation (Piegl & Tiller ┬Д10.4; Mortenson ┬Д3.7); G2 РюЁ: quintic B├Еzier with first 3 CPs analytically fixed from C(u_end), C'(u_end), C''(u_end) (Patrikalakis-Maekawa ┬Д3.4; Piegl & Tiller ┬Д5.3) Рђћ exact parametric second-derivative continuity at join. `extend_edge_curve(curve, delta_length_mm, end, continuity)` Рєњ `EdgeExtendResult(..., end_continuity_achieved)`. `end_continuity_achieved` returns "G1" or "G2". Helpers `_make_g1_extension` / `_make_g2_extension` exported. LLM tool `brep_extend_edge_curve` registered. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 30 hermetic tests (21 original G1 + 9 new G2). **Honest caveats**: G3 (jerk) continuity NOT enforced; G2 arc length РЅѕ delta_length_mm (exact only for zero-curvature). Refs: Piegl & Tiller ┬Д10.4, ┬Д5.3; Mortenson ┬Д3.7; Patrikalakis-Maekawa ┬Д3.4. | РюЁ shipped |
| **`geom/edge_chamfer_variable.py`** | **BREP-EDGE-CHAMFER-VARIABLE**: variable-width chamfer strip along a 2D edge curve for ergonomic edge treatments (handle bevels with grip-width variations). Width ramps linearly from `width_start_mm` (t=0) to `width_end_mm` (t=1) via `w(t) = w_start + t*(w_end-w_start)`; both sides offset perpendicularly by `w(t)/2`. `ChamferVariableSpec` / `ChamferVariableResult` dataclasses; `generate_variable_chamfer(spec)` entry point. LLM tool `brep_generate_variable_chamfer` registered. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 27 hermetic tests. **Honest caveats**: input is a 2D polyline only Рђћ 3D space-curve chamfer that modifies B-rep solid topology is not yet supported (requires generalising `chamfer.py` topology surgery to curved edges, P2/P3 scope). Strip points are a sampled polyline approximation, not an exact NURBS offset curve. Refs: Piegl & Tiller ┬Д10.5 (Variable offsets); Mortenson ┬Д9.3 (Edge blends). | РюЁ shipped |
| **`geom/history/`** | Parametric history DAG + `feature_id::role::fingerprint` persistent naming Рђћ downstream fillet survives upstream parameter edits | РюЁ shipped |

| **GK-P11: Isophote / Environment-Map (EMap) continuity analyser** | Dedicated `geom/isophote_analyzer.py` module: `IsophoteSpec` (surface, view_direction_xyz, angle_bands_deg, uv_samples_u, uv_samples_v) / `IsophoteReport` (isophote_curves, max_isophote_curvature, num_discontinuities, fairness_score, warnings, honest_caveat) / `analyze_isophotes(spec)`. | **GK-P: Quadratic Рєњ cubic NURBS elevation** | Piegl-Tiller ┬Д5.5 specialisation (Lyche-M├Иrken 1988): exact degree-2 Рєњ degree-3 B-spline promotion with shape preservation; per-segment closed-form (`Q1=P0/3+2/3┬иP1`, `Q2=2/3┬иP1+P2/3`); rational/weighted support; surface per-direction; `auto_elevate_to_degree_3` body normalizer for STEP import; `nurbs_elevate_to_cubic` LLM tool registered Рђћ `geom/degree_2_to_3.py` | РюЁ shipped |
| **NURBS-CURVE-DEGREE-LOWER** | Piegl-Tiller ┬Д6.5 (Forrest-Piegl per-segment split) + Schumaker "Spline Functions: Basic Theory" ┬Д6 local approximation. Inverse of degree elevation for STEP export to legacy CAD systems that do not support degree РЅЦ 5. `DegreeLowerResult`: `lowered_curve`, `original_degree`, `new_degree`, `max_deviation_mm`, `mean_deviation_mm`, `exact`, `honest_caveat`. `lower_curve_degree(curve, target_degree, tolerance_mm=1e-3)`: exact when input was degree-elevated from target; otherwise best Forrest-Piegl local approximation with reported deviation. | **`geom/face_centroid.py`** | **BREP-FACE-AREA-WEIGHTED-CENTROID**: area-weighted surface centroid of a B-rep shell/solid; `face_area` / `face_centroid` / `surface_centroid`; Gauss-Legendre 16├Ќ16 per face; supports Plane/Cylinder/Sphere/Torus/NurbsSurface; LLM tool `brep_surface_centroid`; oracles: unit cube area=6/centroid=(0.5,0.5,0.5), unit sphere area=4¤ђ/centroid=(0,0,0); 15 hermetic tests. | **`geom/face_planarity.py`** | **BREP-FACE-PLANARITY-CHECK**: determine if a B-rep face is planar within tolerance; fit best-fit plane via SVD on uniform samples├Ќsamples UV grid (Pratt 1987 ┬Д3; Eberly ┬Д6.6 orthogonal regression); returns `PlanarityReport` (is_planar, plane_origin, plane_normal, max_deviation, planarity_score); default tolerance = 1e-4 ├Ќ bbox diagonal; `check_face_planarity` pure-Python API; LLM tool `brep_check_face_planarity`; oracles: planar NURBS max_dev<1e-9, sphere octant is_planar=False with expected curvature depth, thin 1┬░ arc boundary case, tilted plane, analytic Plane/Sphere surfaces; 12 hermetic tests. | **`geom/face_plane_deviation.py`** | **BREP-FACE-PLANE-DEVIATION**: given a pre-sampled point cloud on a B-rep face (intended-planar or actual-NURBS surface), compute max and RMS deviation from the SVD least-squares best-fit plane (Pratt 1987 ┬Д3; Eberly ┬Д6.6); returns `FacePlaneDeviationReport` (plane: `PlaneFit` with origin_xyz_mm/normal_xyz/d, max_deviation_mm, rms_deviation_mm, num_samples, is_planar, classification, honest_caveat). | **`geom/face_developable_check.py`** | **BREP-FACE-DEVELOPABLE-CHECK**: verify if a B-rep face is developable (can be unrolled flat without stretching). A surface is developable iff Gaussian curvature K = ╬║_1┬и╬║_2 = 0 everywhere (do Carmo ┬Д3.6; Pottmann-Wallner ┬Д4). Algorithm: sample N├ЌN UV grid, compute K via shape operator at each point using `normal_curvature_at`, test max|K| < tolerance; also reports mean|K|, valid sample count, and ruled direction (kappa_1 or kappa_2 identically zero). `DevelopabilityReport` dataclass; `check_face_developable(face, tolerance=1e-3, samples=10)`; LLM tool `brep_check_face_developable`. Useful for: sheet-metal flat-pattern feasibility, ruled-surface validation. | РюЁ shipped |
| **BREP half-space volume** | Given a B-rep solid + cutting plane (point + normal), compute volume on each side via divergence theorem (Mortenson ┬Д11.6). | **`surface_area_exact.py`** | Exact NURBS surface area via first-fundamental-form integrand A = РѕФРѕФ sqrt(EGРѕњF┬▓) du dv (do Carmo ┬Д2.5 / Mortenson ┬Д10.4); 5├Ќ5 Gauss-Legendre per knot-span cell + adaptive subdivision; `SurfaceAreaReport`; LLM tool `nurbs_surface_area_exact`; 18 analytic-oracle tests (unit plane 1e-12, sphere zone <1%, cylinder+torus domain oracles). | **`geom/face_area_exact.py`** | **BREP-FACE-AREA-EXACT**: compute the exact area of a B-rep Face whose underlying surface is a NurbsSurface, using the first fundamental form A = РѕФРѕФ sqrt(EGРѕњF┬▓) du dv (do Carmo ┬Д2.5; Piegl & Tiller ┬Д10.3; Farin ┬Д11.2). | **`geom/principal_curvature_viz.py`** | **BREP-FACE-PRINCIPAL-CURVATURE-VIZ**: sample ╬║РѓЂ, ╬║Рѓѓ (principal curvatures) over a B-rep Face on a U├ЌV grid + SVG/PNG false-colour heatmap. `PrincipalCurvatureSample` dataclass (u, v, kappa_1, kappa_2, gauss_K, mean_H, is_degenerate); `PrincipalCurvatureVizResult` (samples list, svg_heatmap str, png_bytes bytes\|None, honest_caveat str); `sample_principal_curvatures(face, nu=20, nv=20, export_svg=True, export_png=False)`. HONEST: uniform UV-parameter grid only Рђћ high-curvature pockets between grid points are missed (lower bound on max|╬║|); not adaptive; polar/degenerate points (|S_u├ЌS_v|<1e-14) set is_degenerate=True with NaN curvatures; heatmap maps |╬║РѓЂ|, not signed ╬║РѓЂ. | **`geom/surface_curvature_map.py`** | **NURBS-SURFACE-CURVATURE-MAP**: sample a *scalar* curvature field (Gaussian K, mean H, \|╬║РѓЂ\|, or \|╬║Рѓѓ\|) over a NurbsSurface UV grid and export a coloured SVG/PNG heatmap. **GK-P23: In-process isotropic remesh fallback** РюЁ Рђћ `mesh_isotropic_remesh.py` Рђћ Botsch-Kobbelt (2004) iterative pipeline: (1) split edges > 4/3┬иL, (2) collapse interior edges < 4/5┬иL, (3) flip edges to equalise vertex valence toward 6, (4) tangential Laplacian smoothing. Dataclasses: `TriangleMesh` (vertices_xyz_mm, faces), `IsotropicRemeshSpec` (mesh, target_edge_length_mm, num_iterations=5, tangential_smoothing=True, preserve_boundary=True), `IsotropicRemeshReport` (output_mesh, edge_length_min/max/mean/stdev_mm, num_splits/collapses/flips/smooths_total, valence_variance, honest_caveat). `isotropic_remesh(spec)` function. LLM tool `mesh_isotropic_remesh` registered in plugin.py via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core/__init__.py`. 24 hermetic tests green (dataclass structure; square plane 2-tri Рєњ many uniform triangles; stdev decreases vs coarse input; boundary corners preserved; tetrahedron subdivided; empty/invalid/zero-iter edge cases; operation counters; valence variance; package re-export). HONEST CAVEATS: pure-Python + NumPy; slower than instant_meshes binary for > 50k triangles (O(N) per pass edge-map rebuild); output is triangle-only Рђћ quad remesh stays in `quad_remesh.py`; not as feature-complete as instantmeshes for anisotropic or feature-aligned remeshing.

**GK-P50: NURBS arc-length inversion** РюЁ Рђћ `invert_arc_length` (NewtonРђЊRaphson + bisection fall-back; Piegl & Tiller ┬Д11.2 + Sederberg CAGD ┬Д6.4). Returns `ArcLengthInvertResult{t_param, residual_mm, iterations, honest_caveat}`. Used for chord-length parameterisation, even-spaced CAM toolpaths, rebar layout. Wired as `nurbs_invert_arc_length` LLM tool. 19 tests green. Caveat: highly non-uniform knot vectors may trigger bisection fall-back (still converges, just slower).
